caiva gokarṇe mudrālakuṭadhāriṇīm taḍijjaṅghasamopetāṃ namāmi ripumardanīm indrāṇīṃ marudeśetu trailokyākṛṣṭikārikām karālena samopetāṃ namāmyaṃkuśadhāriṇīm romajaṅghasamopetāṃ nagare tu halāyudhām vakrāṃ gacchanivāsinyāṃ namāmi varasiddhaye kumbhakena samopetāṃ khaṭvāṅgakarabhūṣitām namāmi pāpaśuddhyartha cāmuṇḍā pauṇḍravardhane purastīre prasannāsyāṃ vajraśṛṅkhaladhāriṇīm namāmi trijaṭopetāṃ bandhastambhanakārikām pṛṣṭhāpurya vidyunmukhīṃ daṇḍaśaktyāyudhodyatām naumi ghaṇṭāravopetāṃ daityastambhanakārikām kumārikākhaṇḍaulkāmukhasamopetāṃ ūdhvakeśa mahābalām mudrālakuṭahastāṃ tu naumi duṣṭāṅgabhañjanīm piśitāśasamopetāṃ naumi kaṭṭārikodyatām sopāre agnivaktrā tu aśeṣapaśughātanīm kṣīrike lokamātāṃ ca khaḍgahastāṃ namāmyaham mahāsenasamopetāmahitaughanikṛntanīm  vajrāṃkuśadharā naumi bhīmasenasamanvitām stambhākṛṣṭikarīṃ devīṃ māyāpurya prakampinīm mahākrodhasamopetāṃ pūtanāmrātikeśvare gadāhalāyudhā  naumi tāḍanākṛṣṭikārikām bhagnanāsāṃ rājagṛhe mahākarṇasamanvitām vajraśaktidharāṃ naumi aśeṣaphaladāyikām guhyeśvarīṃ mahābhogāṃ nityaṃ paśupateryutām nepāle saṃsthitā naumi bhavaghorāndhahāriṇīm  kāśmīre śāradā devīṃ vidyeśvarasamanvitām vidyāpīṭhasamopetāṃ vidyājñānapradāyikām gaddiharaṇe mahāśakti naumi duḥkhakṣayaṃkarīm mahāśarasamopetāṃ pārvatīṃ parvatasthitām kumārikākhaṇḍajayeśvarīṃ kulūtāyā cakreśa nagnavāsasām kapālīśasamopetāṃ bhogamokṣaphalapradām siṃghuhāre kulālākhyā citrabhogasamanvitām bhairavena samopetāṃ naumi kilviṣanāśanīm bhojapuryā mahācampā lulatī paramāṃ kalām kailāsena samopetāṃ naumi duḥsvapnanāśanīm strīrājye ambikādevīṃ durgamārgakṣayaṃkarīm naṭeśvarasamāyuktā naumi jñānārthasiddhaye mahendre tu mahāmāyāṃ khaḍgahastāṃ namāmyahaṃ mahāmerusamopetāṃ mahadārtinikṛntanīm antarvedyāṃ mahāraktāṃ sarvajñānaughadāyinīm caṇḍeśvarasamopetāṃ nityaṃ naumyaparājitām muśalahastāṃ mahāmāyāṃ trilocanasamāyutām krūrahasthā mahākālīṃ sarvadvandvavināśanīm mahāśmaśāne ghaṇṭāle ghaṇṭālīṃ paramāyudhām ahinoghasamopetāṃ  bhairavīṃ praṇamāmi tām ciñciṇīṃ tu kadambasthā ciñcinīvṛkṣanāyikām naumi bhadreśvarayutāṃ mahāpāpakṣayaṃkarīm kumārikākhaṇḍaḥkaravīre śmaśāne tu ūdhvakeśīṃ bhayaṃkarīm nagnavāsasamopetāṃ pānapātradharāṃ śubhām laṃguḍe cchinnamuṇḍākhyāṃ krodharājasamanvitām kartarīkarahastāṃ tu naumi pāpakṣayaṃkarīm kāmaśare śmaśāne tu kāmalakṣmī jagatpatim manmathena samāyuktāṃ trikoṇākārasaṃsthitām ekakoṇe śmaśānākhye trikoṇāṃ raktavāsasām triśireṇa samopetāṃ nṛmuḍakarabhūṣitām ekavīre śmaśāne tu mātaṅga kulanāyikām mātaṅgīśasamopetāṃ naumi nūpurahastikām ḍohare tu śivādūta asurasuravanditām hayaśīrṣasamopetāṃ dhanubāṇadharā parām śrīparvate mahāsiddhāṃ siddhamārgavikāsinīm jyotiliṅgasamopetāṃ mahāyudhadharāṃ śubhām oṇake tu mahāśakti apavargavikāsinīmparānandasamāyuktāṃ puṣpacāpakarodyatām cchāyācchatre tu caṇḍinyāṃ ūdhvakeśīṃ mahaujasīm ūdhvakeśasamopetāṃ mantramātṛkarodyatām kumārikākhaṇḍaśailapṛṣṭhe tu trijaṭāṃ śailarājasamāyutām mahāḍamarukahastā ca tamāndhabhayahāriṇīm hakkaḍokke rudraśaktiśrīkaṇṭhasahita naumi agnijvālākalānvitāmbhagākhyā siddhavāsanām devīkoṭṭe mahāmāyāṃ iṣupāśakarānvitām vikarālasamopetāṃ saṃsārabhayanāśanīm mahāmāyāvane ghore caṇḍakāpālinīṃ śubhām pracaṇḍasaṃyutāṃ naumi sarasṛṅgakarodyatām śrīmaccandrapure ramye ciñcinīkulamālinīm lambodarasamāyuktāṃ taḍitkoṭikarodyatām mahāmalayadeśe tu mahāmantramaheśvarīm cakreśvarasamopetāṃ kūṣmāṇḍāyudhahastikām mālave tu mahākālīṃ kālakaṅkālahastikām meghanādasamāyuktā jñānavijñānadāyikām śrīmatkedāranilayāṃ saṃsthitāre  tu mālinīm sadāśivasamopetāṃ naumyahaṃ śūlahastikām mahālakṣmīvane ghore mahālakṣmī jagatsukhām naumi tumburusaṃyuktāṃ varadābhayagocarām kumārikākhaṇḍakṣetropakṣetrasaṃdohāḥ catuḥpañcāśa  kīrtitāḥ pīṭhopapīṭhasaṃdohān daśānyān  kīrtayāmi te pūjākramavidhānena kathayāmi samāsataḥ candradvīpe kulālākhyā vidyārājasamanvitām ṭaṅkaṭīkarahastā tu paścime praṇamāmi tām raktā karālā caṇḍākṣī mahocchuṣmā tu bhairavīm Toṃkāre cāgnikāṃ naumi japyamālākarodyatām jālandharasthita devīṃ kāmalakṣmī jagatprabhām phaleśvarasamopetāṃ alakṣmītamanāśanīm  pūrṇagirye mahāgrīvā muṇḍakhaṭvāṅgadhāriṇīm pūrṇeśvarasamāyuktā vandeha sarvamaṅgalām manodbhavā kāmarūpe kādyakhaṭvāṅgahastikām kāmeśvarasamopetāṃ nityaṃ naumyaparājitām tisrapīṭhe tribhuvanāṃ tridaśādhipatīśvarīm kapāladaṇḍahastāṃ tu varadāṃ viśvarūpiṇīm  kṛtivāsasamopetāṃ cāmuṇḍā muṇḍadhāriṇīm ekāmre saṃsthitāṃ devīṃ namāmyaśubhahāriṇīm agnikena samopetā kṣuradhārakarārpitām kāmakoṭṭe mokṣalakṣmīṃ namāmi śrīvivṛddhayekumārikākhaṇḍaasvarā tu mahādevīṃ nityamarbudavāsinīm arbudeśvarasaṃyuktāṃ naumi vighnārtihāriṇīm hiraṇyapurasaṃsthāṃ tu parāṃ śivasamāyutām jñānapustakahastāṃ tu paramārthaphalapradāmkṣetropakṣetrasaṃdohe sthitā bhūcakramātaraḥ kṣetrapālasamopetā kīrtayed yaḥ samāhitaḥ prātarutthāya mantrajñaḥ svapnakālethavā sudhīḥ ādyapīṭhe kramāgre tu yoge samayamaṇḍale yuktopi pātakairghorairdevīnāṃ sammato bhavet pitṛhā mātṛhantā ca brahmahā goghna eva ca bruṇahā paśuhantā vā pāpiṣṭo gurutalpagaḥ vīradravyāpahārī  ca pramādāt samayacyutaḥ mantrācāraviluptātmā pīṭhānā kīrtanādapi sarvapātakanirmukto  naiva paśyati durgatimya puna śuddhabhāvātmā trikāla parikīrtayet prāpnoti cintitān kāmān mātṝṇā vallabho bhavetkuṇḍe vā maṇḍale vāpi pratimāyāṃpaṭepi vā liṅge dakṣiṇamūrtī vā jalamadhyagatopi vā trikālamekakāla vā ya paṭhet susamāhitaḥ viṣaśastrajalāgnibhyo vyādhibhūtagrahairapi ajita suciraṃ kālaṃ jīvate nirupadravaḥ sādhayet samyak saphalaṃ nātra saṃśayaḥ niṣphalaṃ bījarahita araṇye ropitaṃ yathā sabījaṃkumārikākhaṇḍaaṭṭahāsāt samārabhya yāvat   hāṭakaṃ puram taṃtāvad mantrānvayo hyeṣa aṇimādiphalapradaḥ śrīnātha uvācahemapīṭhāntakāvadhiḥ aṭṭahāsādipīṭhāṇāṃtāvat pīṭheṣu sarveṣu aśaktobījapañcake mātṛkūṭasamāyogāt tadupāyaṃ vadasva me śrīvakrā uvācaaṭṭahāsādipīṭheṣu kṛtvā vai dīpapañcakam tathaiva mātṛhṛdayaṃ hemakūṭasya uccaret ādyantoccārayogena sarve mātṛkule gatāḥ ādyantakaraṇaṃ yoga  sabījakaraṇottamam aśaktānāṃ samākhyātaṃ śrīgṛhe tasya sāṃpratam tasmād bhuktiśca muktiśca pīṭhānāṃ kīrtanād bhavet ādhārā stavarājasya praṇavāḥ pūrvapaścime guptoccārakṛte  siddhiryadi yogī ca mantravit mahābhaye samutpanne kapilāgomayena tu aṣṭāṣṭavidhānena kārayed vṛttamaṇḍalam śivaratnaṃ tathānyeṣu ekānte yāgamandire kumārikākhaṇḍasādhakānā putrakānā stavarājasya sevanāt sugandhai śvetapuṣpaiśca kuṃkumena suvāsitaiḥ dhūpaiḥ śrīkhaṇḍagandhādyai  sumanena palālinā naivedyabhakṣapānādyairdīpainanāvidhaiḥ śubhaiḥ  madhye tu kalaśaṃ sthāpya vīradravyaprapūritam aiṃkāramāsana datvā tena kandaṃ tu lāñcchitam svayaṃ cārṇaṃ mahāpiṇḍaṃ karau dehe tu vinyaset piṇḍānvitena dehena pīṭhayāga tu kārayet madhye hiraṇya saṃpūjya paścima sarvakāmadam anye vilomamārgeṇa yāvad vai aṭṭahāsakam pīṭhayāgaṃ tu kartavyaṃ pāvanta śrīpurādinā pīṭhopapīṭhasaṃdohakṣetropakṣetranāyakāḥ sarve te dvārabhūtāstu śivapīṭhasya madhyataḥ yuktāste pretanāthena śivavyāptyā haranti te tatrasthā pūjitā mantrāḥ kriyāmāgavalambakā jñānaṃ dadanti sarveṣāṃ bhaktyā saṃtarpitā śubhāḥ tasmāt sarvaṃ prayatnena hairaṇya  pīṭhamuttamam tatra pūjā kṛtā nityaṃ sarvakāmānavāpnuyāt digvidikṣu gatā  pīṭhā bāhyato madhyamāsane garbhasthāne mahāpīṭhaṃ tveva krameṇa yojayet catuḥṣaṣṭistu dīpāni pīṭhāni parivartayet kumārikākhaṇḍaḥahorātroṣito bhūtvā svapekākī suyantrita  brahmacārīvratasthañca piśitālivivarjitaḥ tatra japyaṃ prakartavyaṃ mātratriṃśatija yataḥ prabhāte vimale mantrī vīrabhojyaṃ tu kārayet tataḥ kṣamāpayet pīṭhān praṇipatya muhurmuhuḥ nirvighnastu tato mantrī sarvaṃ bhavati siddhidamupasargagrahādīni yakṣakūṣmāṇḍaguhyakāḥ śatrorutkaṭadeśe tu rājābhaṅge viśeṣataḥ mucyate sa upasargebhyo dhanadhānyamavāpnuyāt paropaghāṭakṛtyeṣu māraṇoccāṭanādiṣu pāpapaṅkād hi mucyeta nirmalaṃ vāstra vartate pīṭhānā  kramayogena pāpātmā na punarbhavet prāpnuyādabhīpsitān  kāmān mṛtavat sopi yo bhavet jīvavatsā bhavati putriṇī tadabhiṣecanāt putrārthī labhate putrān subhagatvamavāpnuyāt vidyārthī labhate vidyā dhanārthī dhanavān bhavetdārārthī labhate dārā rūpayauvanagarvitām bhūmyarthī labhate bhūmi pānārthī pānamāpnuyāt jñānārthī labhate jñānaṃ samayārthī samayaṃ labhet mantrārādhanaśīlastu jāyate nirupadravaḥ yogābhyāsarato nityaṃ prāpya siddhi paraṃ vrajet kumārikākhaṇḍaḥpādavidyāprasaṅgena pīṭhastavaprakāśitam samastavyastaprāptistu mantroccāraṇadhāraṇāt anvayesmin samastaṃ tu stavapāṭhamudāhṛtam  ityādyāvatāre mahāmanthānabhairavayajñe anvaye saptakoṭipramāṇe merumārgavinirgatelakṣapādādhike ādyapīṭhāvatārite kādibhede pīṭhastavādhikāre vidyāpīṭhamārge vimalaṣaṭkanirṇaye kādibhede ājñāpārameśvaresvāminīmate śrīcaturviśatsahasrasahitāyāṃ avvākramabhāṣite vidyādhikāro nāmānandaḥ  oṃ svasti śrīnāthapādukābhyāṃ namaḥ  śrīgaṇeśāya namaḥ manthāna bhairavatantre kumārikākhaṇḍesaptadaśānandaḥśrīvakrā uvācaanvayasya tu yat sāraṃ divyaughe saṃpradarśitam ṣoḍaśātmakasaṃketamadhunā kathayāmi te santāna merumārge ca anvayaṃ tatra devatā nirgamaṃ caiva oṃkāre siddhānvayeṃ prakīrtitam tuṣṇīdeva guhāvāsī vṛkṣaṃ caiva kadambakam siṃhasaṃketaka caiva avvā ca guhavāsinī gṛha candrapura proktaṃ bhedaṃ manthānabhairavam gotram amarikā devī vāmamārge prakalpitā anvaye pratyaya sāraṃ adhikāra tu koṅkaṇe janmabrahmaśilā siddhasthiti kāmarūpake kīrtiściñciṇivṛkṣaṃ tu siddhiścaiva tu sāgare tuṣṭohaṃ tasya deveśa yo jānāti kulakramam ayaṃ tu kaulika sāraṃ kulakramavinirgatam ṣoḍaśātmakasaṃketa jñātvā cānvayiko bhavet śrīnātha uvāca kumārikākhaṇḍakiṃ merumārga deveśi anvaye kātra devatā oṃkāranirgamaṃ brūhi siddhau caiva vadasva me guhāvāsāntara kiṃ tu kadambaṃ prakaṭaṃ kuru siṃhakaṃ ca na me jñāta candrapurya viśeṣataḥ gotraṃ manthānabhedaṃ ca prakaṭaṃ kuru kaulini anvaye pratyaya kiṃ tu adhikāra tathāmbike janmabrahmaśilā yoni nigadasva maheśvari sthitiḥ ki kāmarūpe tu kīrti kathaya ciñciṇīm sāgare tu kathaṃ siddhiḥ etat pṛcchāmi kaulini sphuṭaṃ kathaya ekaikaṃ saṃśayaṃ chetumarhasi śrīvakrā uvācasaṃketāni ca deveśa kulāmnāye vyavasthitāḥ candrapuryasya bimbasya anvayaṃ ṣoḍaśātmakam tasya santānasūtraṃ tu ṣaḍvidhasya kramasya ca adhunā śrūyatāṃ śambho amṛta sārasaṃgraham pade pade mayā khyātaṃ bhede bhede pṛthak pṛthak atigūḍhamidaṃ praśna devadevāvatāritam kumārikākhaṇḍatadahaṃ kathayiṣyāmi yena vindasi sarvaśaḥ meru bhuvana vikhyātaṃ devatālayaśobhanam trikūṭa śṛṅgaracitaṃ tribhirdevairadhiṣṭhitam brahmā viṣṇuśca rudraśca ete siddhakrame sthitāḥ ānanda vimala ciñca eṣāṃ saṃjñā triśuddhiṣu ānanda vyāpaka deva sarvabhūteṣvavasthitam sṛṣṭirvimalarūpeṇa cikārājñāgṛhe sthitā etairvijñātamātraistu mokṣaṃ yāsyanti mānavāḥ vyāpinyā ca mahādevī ekaikasya vyavasthitā taraṅginī mahācaṇḍā kāye kāyeṣu vyāpinī triratnabhūṣitaistvaṅgaiḥ  svabhāvena tu dīpitā mārga caiva ṛju spaṣṭaṃ suśuddhamamṛtopamam amā nāma kalā sā tu āśramaṃ guhyamaṇḍale āgatā sā parā devī dāḍimīkusumopamā dvau pakṣau guhakā māyā dṛśyete ṛtukālayoḥ vicitrā nāma vikhyātā tayā vyāptamaśeṣataḥ eṣā sā devatā devatayā khyātā mayā prabho guhāśramād viniṣkrāntā asvarā svaravāhinī śuddhasphaṭikasaṃkāśā śaktibhiḥ saha saṃsthitā niṣkrāntā kūrmanāḍyā yā indubimbasamāyutā kumārikākhaṇḍasiddhau dvāviti vikhyātau bhūṣita merumaṇḍalam sṛṣṭisaṃhārakartārau punaścāntapade sthita oṃ kāranirgamaṃ deva sādākhyaṃ parigīyate ayaṃ brahma aya viṣṇuraya rudro maheśvaraḥ sarvadevamaya hyeṣa oṃkāra iti gīyatemerormadhyamatuṅge tu sthitā samudramālayā trikoṇāyā guhāmadhye oṃkārastatra dṛśyate amṛtamadhye guhāvāsī bindunā gīyate tu sā saṃketa vṛkṣamūlaṃ tu yonimadhye kadambakam tena vyāptamidaṃ meru ālayaṃ sarvayoginām saṃjñābhedasthitā devī harayā bindusaṃjñayā bhāṣāmudrāṇi cinhāni saṃketena prakīrtitāḥ siṃhaka śṛṇu deveśa ambā yatra svayaṃbhairavī ramate tatra krīḍate bhairavai saha sthitā adhiṣṭhānaṃ mahāsthānaṃ samudrālayaveṣṭitam siṃhakaṃ taṃ vijānīyāt siṃhāsanamudīritam kumārikākhaṇḍaambarastha mahābimba ṣoḍaśasvarabhūṣitam tanmadhye tu amā devī gṛhametat prakīrtitam kūrmayantrapravāhena manthayecca parasparam manthānaṃ sṛṣṭirevokta kaulika kalasaṃbhavam tasmin madhye ramed dhīmān yatra mātā nirāmayā asmin gotraṃ pravakṣyāmi amaratva śṛṇu priya pañcaratnasya madhyasthaṃ śrīkaṇṭhādi prakīrtitam eṣa devyādigotro yana gotraṃ nāmasaṃjñayā vāmabhāge sthitā yā tā vāmācāreṇa pūjayet amaratveti vijñeyaṃ lambakaṃ nāma viśrutam sā kalā bhāvaye dravya pibasva amṛtopamam eṣā paraṃ mahāsthānaṃ merumaṇḍalaveṣṭitam pratyayaṃ śṛṇu deveśa mahāviśveti dṛśyate vartulaṃ ratnatuṅgābhaṃ varṇāvaṇīntapratyayamkumārikākhaṇḍatacca paśyanti yoginyo matyānāṃ prakaṭa hara mahāparvatabimbasya pūjā kurvanti yoginaḥ kramārcanaṃ prakurvanti ye sthitā viśvamadhyataḥ  divyākṣaraṃ tu taṃ paśyet kaulinīparilekhitam  sa eṣa pratyaya rudra pratyakṣa samudāhṛtam kṛtaṃ mayādhikāra tu pūrṇapīṭhe hyadhomukhī puna koṃkaṇāvatāre kamalāvvā prakīrtitā etad vai adhikāraṃ tu koṃkaṇe prakaṭīkṛtam brahmasthāne bhavet padmaṃ sṛṣṭyartha samupāgatam janmasthāna śilāmadhye tatra cāṃkuradevatā tayā ca sā śilākrāntā janmabrahmaśilā smṛtā kandamūlamadha sthāne vartulaṃ cātiśobhanam tacchravet kāminīcakre devadeva maheśvara kāmākhyaṃ guhyasaṃsthāne sthitvāśrama mameti ca kariṣyāmi hyahaṃ kīrti ciñcākhye vṛkṣasaṃjñake mayāpi vyāpita meru ramantī ca ahaṃ sthitā kumārikākhaṇḍasāgare hṛdi madhye tu nānāsiddhīnyanekaśa tatra mantrā hi yogadā vijñānaṃ cātra saṃsthitam bhogamokṣālayaṃ deva yat kiñcit sacarācaram etat sāraṃ mahāśambho jñātavyaṃ kaulikaiḥ saha yasya tuṣṭā ca avvāha sa vindati kulakramam kulapiṇḍe tu he nātha mithyā kliṣyanti yoginaḥ na vindanti rahasyeda yat sāraṃ kaulikānvaye tena te siddhinirmuktā vicaranti mahītale svānubhava merubimbe tu siddhīnāṃ klinnamaṇḍale kulasyāsya prabhāvena tasmāt siddhirna dūrataḥ kulakaulasya madhye tu yo ramet sādhakottamaḥ sa mukto mocayejjantūn yoginīsamatāṃ vrajet aya tu kaulikaṃ sāraṃ kulakramavinirgatam saṃketaṣoḍaṣa śambho mayā tadupalakṣitam na kathed bhinnabhāvasya bhaktihīnaśaṭhasya ca vyākhyeyaṃ bhaktiyuktasya gurudevaratasya cakumārikākhaṇḍaityādyāvatāre mahāmanthānabhairavayajñe anvaye saptakoṭipramāṇe merumārgavinirgatelakṣapādādhike ādyapīṭhāvatārite vidyāpīṭhamārge vimalaṣaṭkanirṇaye kādibhedeājñāpārameśvare svāminīmate śrīcaturviṃśatsahasrasaṃhitāyāṃ avvākramabhāṣite śrīsantānasūtrādhikāravarṇane kramodayo nāmānandaḥ aṣṭādaśānandaḥśrīnātha uvācakiñciccodyaṃ mama bhadre buddhikauśalyavistaram kena buddhisvarūpeṇa vasase mama dehagā kena jñānabhūyiṣṭhena tanme brūhi surārcite kiṃ kula kulā kiṃ mūla anvaya tathā saṃjñābhedavidhānāni rūpaṃ varṇā svarūpataḥ kule piṇḍasya nyāsaṃ hi padasthānavibhūṣaṇam kasmin sthāne tu nyastavya yo dhāraṇalakṣaṇam samayavidyā ca ājñā ca nyāsasūtraṃ vadasva me śrīvakrā uvāca sādhu sādhu mahāśambho yanme nigaditaṃ śṛṇu vistareṇa bahubhedaistatsarvaṃ kathayāmi te vāgjālaiḥ kiṃ prabhāvaiśca tūṣṇīṃ tvaṃ tiṣṭha śaṅkara ekayā jihvayā deva kathaṃ varṇayituṃ kṣamā śṛṇu rahasyaṃ paramaṃ sadbhāvaṃ varṇayāmi te yathā kṣīre sthitaṃ sarpiḥ avyucchinnaṃ na dṛśyate tathāhaṃ tava sarvāṅgai vyāpayitvā  vyavasthitā mayā vinā ca tvaṃ deva ajñānī mūḍhacetanaḥ paṃgulo jaḍavaccāndho mūko badhira vatsala kumārikākhaṇḍamayā prabodhamātrayā prabudhyante punastathā spandanaṃ calanaṃ caiva bhramaṇaṃ jalpanaṃ vibho krīḍanaṃ sṛṣṭikartṛtvaṃ yat kiñcit karotīcchayā sarvāvasthā mayā deva preritā mama sarvataḥ na mayā rahitaṃ kiñcit paśyasi ca trilocana yathā raśmisamūhena vyāpayecca divākaraḥ tathāha vyāpinī tubhyaṃ dehe tiṣṭhāmi sarvadā yathā vahneḥ sthitā jvālāśītāṃśuraśmimadhyataḥ evaṃ vyāptaṃ mayā sarvaṃ aśeṣa bhuvanāntikam vyāpita tu mayā śaktyā māyājālena mohitam karaṇaṃ kartṛ karmāṇi kurvāmi na karomyaham sarvaśāstrāṇyanekāni  citritā mama pustake śobhanāni ca vākyāni śṛṇu bhairava yatnataḥ śrīmateda mahādeva sarvāgamamanuttamam yena vijñātamātreṇa nirmala  sādhako bhavet vicareta mahīṃ sava niḥśaṅko vanahastivat śrīnātha uvācanyāsasūtraṃ mahādevi vada me śaṃkarārcite yena nyasitamātreṇa divyāmnāyaḥ pravartate kumārikākhaṇḍaśrīvakrā uvāca punaranya kramaṃ vakṣye mālinyā dehasantatim merumārgād viniṣkrāntā ṣoḍhānyāsasya paddhatiḥ mālinī śabdarāśiśca trividyāghorikāṣṭakam siddhāṅgapañcakāṅgāni vidyayā bījapañcakam pīṭhapañcakamevaṃ tu ṣoḍhānyāsa prakīrtitam samayādvādaśāṅgāni tathā kṣetraparigraham  adhikāratrayaṃ kṛtvā tathānyaṃ ratnapañcakam evaṃ nyāsakramaṃ kṛtvā paścād yajanamārabhet mālinyādisuvinyāsaṃ samaya  maṇḍalakramam prathamaṃ kulakaulasya kṛtvā yajanamārabhet tatra nyāsa yathā deva avatāraṃ kalau yuge ādipīṭhasya vakṣyāmi śṛṇu ekāgra sundara uddhāraṃ ca yathā deva śṛṇu vakṣyāmyanantaram rāvasyādhaḥ sthita ratna śikhā syācca adhomukhī tathā ca padmayoniśca śirosmākaṃ maheśvara ekapādāntacatvāri vilomācchiramālikā ādya śaktipurasyāsya nayanaṃ ca tṛtīyakam tathā dhūmradhvajasyādhau locanau dvau prakīrtitau ekapādaśira gṛhya dvāvetau karṇayonyaset kumārikākhaṇḍatathābhyā bhūṣaṇau śreṣṭhau ṭhaḍāntau ca sthitau hara īūmadhye gatā nāsā śivarūpā manonmanī puṭobhayasamāyuktā visargāntepi  bhedinī tasyādhaḥ paravaktraṃ tu sṛṣṭipūrva maheśvara hanumānujavarṇādya khādyaṃ vai khaśiraṃ punaḥ dviśiraṃ pañcabhirmadhyādubhayordantamālikā tasyāṃ lalanayā māyā kapālaśirabhuṣaṇam svarādyamamṛtaṃ yacca tasyāṃ vāgeśvarīṃ nyaset anaṅgāsana kaṇṭhaṃ tu chahāntaskandhayobhayoḥ uṭhāsanau tu dvau tasyāḥ kuryāt tau bāhudaṇḍayoḥ gauryādhaḥstha jaṭāhāraṃ kuryād hastatalāvubhau pudgalasya visargādyaṃ ubhayoḥ karapṛṣṭhayoḥ jaantaṃ ca i  anta ca hastāṃgulinakhāgragau vāmahastasthita pātraṃ kapālaṃ īyamadhyagam uttānamamṛtaṃ pūrṇa pañcaratnairadhiṣṭhitam triśūlaṃ dakṣiṇe haste adhodaṇḍānnidhānakamtasya codhva mukhaṃ kuryāt harasya surasundara etad vai rājasaṃ śūlaṃ rajobhāvena sundara kumārikākhaṇḍatārādyaṃ yat paraṃ varṇa prāṇe hi parigīyate hṛdi sthitaṃ prakartavyaṃ sarvapāpaharaṃ hara tasmād varṇamanaṅgādya prāṇātmānaṃ svayaṃ gatam hṛdayaṃ trividhaṃ prokta śākta śāmbhavamāṇavam dakṣiṇottaratastasyā harādyaṃ vāntadvayoḥ kucau divyau tu devyāyā sāvyāsāvya vijānataḥ tayoḥ kṣīraṃ jhakārānta tejorūpaṃ surārcitam mahāśaṅkhāmudara vartulaṃ kumbhaka pṛthu aṣṭamamamṛtasyādho nābhyakārāgnibhairavam āsanaṃ ca dvirabhyāsa devyāyā vā nitambakam ṣavāntastha bhagāntaṃ ta girijāsanapudgalam śukreda yonirandhrasthaṃ hyamṛtaṃ śravamāṇakam thaṇāntaṃ ca dvirabhyāsa devyāyāḥ sphijakāvubhau rāvaṇajāntagau gṛhya vilomājjānuka smṛtau pudgalāntāntagau jaṃghau savyāsavyakrameṇa tu auśireṇa śire dve ca devyāyāḥ pādayugmake nādiphāntasamuccāra kṛtvā khecaratāṃ vrajet khagati khegatī caiva mālinyāyā prabhāvataḥ kumārikākhaṇḍaḥnyastvā vai mālinīnyāsaṃ dvādaśābdestu siddhyatisakṛdāvartayed yastu satataṃ nyasatepi vā tasya tīvratarā ājñā bhavate nātra saṃśayaḥ varṇadevyodhunā vakṣye mālinyā  pūrvavat kramāt nādinī grāsinī caiva nivṛttiśca pratiṣṭhikā vidyā caiva tathā śāntiścāmuṇḍā priyadarśinī nārāyaṇī ca mohanyā prajñāśaktistathāparā gandhaśaktiśca vajriṇyā kaṅkaṭā kālikā viduḥ śivā ca ghoraghoṣā ca vicitrā ajayā punaḥ cavāgeśvarī śikhivāhī bhīṣaṇā vāyuvegikā sulāmā ca vināyakī tathā caiva tu pūrṇimā icchāśaktistu sakāyā raktā caiva kapālinī nandinī ca jayantī ca padminī parajāmbikā chagalā pūtanā caiva āmoṭī lambodarī saṃhārī ca mahākālī tathā ca kusumāyudhā guhyaśaktiśca tārākṣī jñānaśaktistathaiva ca kriyāśaktiśca gāyatrī sāvitrī tadanukramāt dahanī phetkārikā ca nādiphānte samāśritāḥ āśramapūrvato varṇaṃ bījaṃ devyastathā punaḥ tribhirekasamāyogānmālinīnyāsamārabhetkumārikākhaṇḍanādiphāntākṣarā ye ca pañcāśat pūrvamuddhṛtāḥ yathā kuryācca saṃsthānaṃ sṛṣṭinyāye krameṇa tu śirohīnamanaṅga tu tathā cākhaṇḍamaṇḍalam candrodhvāṅkitameva tu unmanyantaṃ tathā punaḥ evaṃ catuḥprakārasthaṃ mālinīnyāsamārabhet catuṣṭayavinirmukta nyāsaṃ yaḥ kartumarhati nāsau nyāsaṃ na saḥ śiṣyaḥ kṛtaṃ bhavati niṣphalam nādabindukalājyotiryeṣu varṇeṣu saṃsthitaḥ bījāste sarvata  khyātā  śeṣā varṇāśca kevalā kevaleṣu ca varṇeṣu na muktirbhavabandhanāt samyakjñāteṣu bījeṣu punarjanma na vidyate prākṛtaṃ pūrvakarma tu tailabindurivāmbhasi janānāṃ vartamānasya jñātairbīje kṣayo bhavet tasmādabhyāsakaraṇa mālinīnyāsarūpataḥśaktistu mālinī jñeyā prāṇaśaktiścidātmikā suṣumnāntarayogena gamāgamakrameṇa tu ravicandrasamāyogāt tadā prasādabhairavam prasāda binducakraṃ tu ūdhvaṃ cāṃkuśavartulam gambhīranādavegena teṣāṃ sampadyate sukham sukhāhlādamanānanda  avasthā prāpyate padam tadā sā mālinīśaktirvahnirutpadyate kalā sā ca turyasvarākārā vakradehodbhavā kalā kumārikākhaṇḍacandrārkānalakuṇḍeṣu mālinyāyādhikāraṇam viṣavahnigatā madhye āvartante vyavasthitā tasmāt sā tiryagā rekhā mālinyākāraveśmani tena sā mālinī proktā sthūlā sūkṣmā tathā parā parata parayogena parāparaparāyaṇā gṛhītvā bījarūpāṇi bindurūpānuyoginī tayā vyāptaṃ jagat sarvaṃ aśeṣabhuvanāntikam tasyāpyetanmahābīja vāgbhava garbhasaṃyutam māyābījaṃ dvitīya tu lakṣmībījaṃ tṛtīyakam evaṃ te dīpakaṃ trīṇi bīje bīje pṛthak pṛthak śikhāgrādinakhāgrāntaṃ kulavinyāsa sundaram dīpakeṣu vinirmukta nyastvā nyāsaṃ ca mālinīmśiṣyaṃ tatra na mucyeta prākṛtaṃ pūrvakarmaṇā pūrvakarmavināśārtha nyāsedida sudīpitam kathitaṃ kulayogīnā kaulayogāt paraṃ nahi śrīnātha uvācacaitanyaṃ vyomavigraham śiraśchedakanāmena prajvalantaṃ nabhasthitam puruṣasyāntarātmānaṃsa eva puruṣo vyāpī avyakto jyotirūpakaḥ śabdāḍhyaṃ ca guṇātītaṃ prabhutve saṃvyavasthitam kiṃ tasya bandhanaṃ proktaṃ raticakre tu bhāvini kumārikākhaṇḍakimetanmālinīnyāsa mukta bhavati kiṃ prabho etad vijñātumicchāmi mālinīkramahetunā śrīvakrā uvācaetat praśnavara guhyaṃ siddhināthāvatāritam tasyottara  pravakṣyāmi śṛṇu ekāgra bhairava kṣīramadhye sthitaṃ sarpi avyucchinnaṃ na dṛśyate tathāsau puruṣo loke mālinīhadimaṇḍale yadā na paśyate jīva svamanena tu sādhakaḥ tadāsau vartate karma prākṛtaṃ duratikramam sukhaduḥkhavaśaṃ gacchet na jñāta puruṣo yadā tadā te pañcabhūtaistu puruṣosau vaśaṃgataḥ vidite puruṣe deva kṣayasteṣāṃ na saṃśayaḥ evaṃ ca prākṛtaṃ karma puruṣasya vyavasthitam ādau ca puruṣo vyāpī paścāt karma pravartate puruṣeṇa vinā karma na pravarteta bhūtale pṛthivyādiṣu tattveṣu saṃsthitaḥ puruṣo hi saḥ sattvarajastamaikatve kṛtaṃ karma pravartate puruṣeṇa vinā karma natasmāccādau ca puruṣaṃpravarteta kevalam tato bhūtādipañcakam paścāt trīṇi guṇānyeṣāṃtataḥ karma pravartate yasmāt pāśā pravartante śubhāni aśubhāni ca kumārikākhaṇḍaḥprakṛtyāntargata jñātvā mālinīkuṇḍamadhyataḥ pañcabhūtāni mucyeta sādhako mokṣado bhavet etat sarva samāsena mālinyā  kramasaṃsthitiḥ sā caiva candrarūpeṇa puṃsaḥ śaktiśca cinmayā sā ca mātā ca mālinyā sthūlā sūkṣmāparājitā bījabhūtā samākhyātā mālinī bhuvanākṛtiḥ vaktrād vaktragatā jñeyā guruvako pratiṣṭhitā saṃsthitā ceśvare bhāge vāmamārge visarpitā tasyāmabhyāsakaraṇa ṣaḍaṅgaṃ ca yathā bhavet merumadhyagataṃ vaktraṃ ṣaḍvidhaṃ  kārayet punaḥ dīrgheḥ ṣaḍbhiḥ svarairbhedyai  nādabindulayaṃ kṛtam ṣaḍantaragatā vai ca kuryāt ṣaḍvidhamāsanam ṣaḍvadha kāmarājānaṃ mālinyā yoniyojitam hṛcchiraśca śikhā varmalocanāstra ca ṣaḍvidham devatāṣaḍbhiḥ saṃyukta mālinyāṅgakrameṇa tu śavarī vidyujjihvā ca śarvarī ca kulāmbikā mohanī māraṇī ṣaṣṭhī pṛthagaṅgeṣu devatāḥ kuryād bījatrayaṃ cādau tathā kāmeśvara punaḥ devatāmāśramaṃ  ṣaḍbhiḥ ādyanteṣu vilomataḥ pṛthakkūṭavidhānena aṅgānyetāni mālinī kumārikākhaṇḍasakṛdāvartayed yastu satataṃ nyasatepi vā ājñā pravartate tīvrā divyāveśaḥ pravartate na śṛṇoti na paśyeta tadāsau muktibhājana maṇḍalāgre gurorājñā suvinītaḥ prasannadhī vaktrāṇi saṃpravakṣyāmi yathāvadanupūrvaśaḥ cchāyācchatraṃ mahādeva ukāra śirasāhatam bindvindunāṅkita deva ūdhvavaktraṃ tu mālinī haṃsa ca mūrdhni vinyasya vāyubījaṃ ca pūrvataḥ ekapādayutaṃ kṛtvā agninā dīptatattvataḥ bindvinduśirasākrānta tṛtīyaṃ vaktramaṇḍalam agnidhāma ca saṃgṛhya pañcamena samanvitam binducandrayutaṃ deva dakṣiṇe vaktramaṇḍale vāruṇaṃ māyayā sārdhaṃ dīpanyāyā adhoyutam binducandrayutaṃ deva vāmavaktraṃ tu mālinī tupūtanā dīpanīyuktā mohanyādhaḥ kṛtālayā bindu  indusamākrāntā paścime vaktrasaṃsthitāḥete vaktrā mahādeva mālinyāyā prakāśitāḥ nyāsedamārabhet śreṣṭha sadyaḥ pratyayakārakam asaṃkhyāni ca pāpāni ye kṛtā pūrvajanmani ihaloke ca ye cānye kṛtā vātha kariṣyati te ca sarve vinaśyanti mālinīnyāsayogataḥ kumārikākhaṇḍaetaccātirahasyaṃ vai merumārgavinirgatam śaśicāravaśācchambho ekacakre  adhiṣṭhitam tasya yogaprayogoya gurorājñāvadhiṣṭhitam jānātya yadā deva mālinīkramarājakam sa muktaḥ sarvabandhebhyo na bhūyo bandhamāpnuyāt tāntrikānā tārkikānāṃ paraśiṣye viḍambake na dadyānmālinīnyāsaṃ dattaṃ vā maraṇaṃ bhavet tāvad bhramati saṃsāre ghorākāre mahārṇave yāvanna  prāpyate deva mālinīkramarājakam tathā kula kramaṃ nyāsa kā cintā bhavasāgare saubhāgya śreyasaṃpatti aṣṭaiśvaryaḥ pravartate bhavate nātra saṃdeho rudravat sādhako bhavet etad vai mālinīnyāsa sadbhāva kaulikānvaye tavākhyataṃ tu siddhasya nādiphāntasvarūpakam ityādyāvatāre mahāmanthānabhairavayajñe anvaye saptakoṭipramāṇe merumārgavinirgatelakṣapādādhike ādyapīṭhāvatārite vidyāpīṭhamārge vimalaṣaṭkanirṇayekādibhede ājñāpārameśvare svāminīmate śrīcaturviṃśatisahasrasaṃhitāyāṃ avvākramabhāṣite mālinīnyāsakramādhikāravarṇane kramodayo nāmānandaḥ  ūnaviṃśānandaḥśrīvakrā uvācaartha cānyakramaṃ vakṣye śabdarāśisvarūpataḥ amṛtādivisargāntaṃ kramaṃ pañcāśadrūpiṇam suśuddhe bhūpradeśe tu pāṃśugomayalepite puṣpaprakarasaṃkīrṇe sugupte paśuvarjite gurorājñāprasādena śabdarāśi samuddharet yosau sarvagato devo vibhuḥ katī sureśvaraḥ sa cāmṛtataraṅgeṣu turyastha bindumaṇḍale akhaṇḍamaṇḍalākāraṃ yoginīravabheditam taṃ para vyomni cakrasya tasya śabdamadhiṣṭhitam śabdarāśikrameṇoktaṃ varṇarūpādhikārakam piṇḍasthaṃ ca padasthaṃ ca rūpasthaṃ rūpavarjitam nirañjanapadāvastha  tadā muktaṃ maheśvara śabdabrahma bhavet piṇḍaṃ padaṃ bījākṣaraṃ smṛtam rūpaṃ ca maṇḍalaṃ yoga rūpātītaṃ ca bhairava nirañjana piṇḍasthaṃ ca rūpasthaṃ rūpavarjitam nirañjanapade jñeyāstadādho praśasyate kumārikākhaṇḍagurorgurutarāñcaiva ye cānye kramadhārakāḥ sarve nirañjanāvasthāstadā te mokṣadāyakāḥ śabdabrahma para brahma brahmākṣarasamudbhavaḥ tallayaṃ tatparātmānanaṃ brahmavṛkṣaṃ ca golakam tasya śākhākṣarā deva pañcāśadrūpasaṃkhyayā mantrarūpāstu te sarve pañcāśattanumaṇḍitāḥ vyāptisteṣāṃ kramācāra ādhāracandrapuryake candrapuryasya vinyasya śabdarāśyādhikārakam ānanda tu navātmāna tadā rudrānvaya bhavet rudrāṇāṃ mātṛkānyāsaṃ khecarakramanirṇayam khecara ca khamadhyasthaṃ madhyasthaṃ ca khakhecaram etaccatuḥ prakāreṇa śāmbhavaṃ śabdarāśikam anukrama merumārge mudrātattvavibheditam tanmadhye ca kramaṃ deva tvaṃ rudra śabdarāśikam tvaṃ ca pañcāśadbhirbhedaiḥ prakṛtirjñeyarūpataḥ vijñānabhūmikāyoga kārikākramasantatiḥ santānamekamākāśa bhedāste saptaviṃśatiḥ teṣāṃ mūrtidharaṃ devaṃ varṇarāśyā tu kevalam kumārikākhaṇḍaśrīnātha devatairyukta sa ca ulitraye guruḥ ulitraye kramāḥ trīṇi teṣāṃ rāśiprayojanam pūrvokta sahitāyāṃ tu ādināthena svāminā tasya mantrakramameva pratyaya pūrvabhāṣitam bhāṣāmudrāsamopetaṃ bhairavaṃ śabdarāśikam tacca ca tṛtīyakaṃ mārga ādyapīṭhaṃ surendrarāṭ asyoddhāra punarhayeva yathā sṛṣṭikrameṇa tu ātmānaṃ rudravat jñātvā rudramātmānavad dhara sabāhyābhyantaraṃ jñātvā śabdarāśyāvatārayet amṛtādihakārāntaṃ etad varṇaparam mātṛkākulamekaṃ tu bhagajāta tu pratyayam tacca pañcāśaddhirbhedaiḥ nyastvā kṣobhobhijāyate etadakṣaravinyāsa pūrvasaṃskārasaṃskṛtam tadā bījakramanyāsa avijñāta na mucyate  anaṅgasya śiraṃ nyasya lalāṭaṃ tava mūrdhani tathā caiva ñavarṇasya bhavet tad vaktramaṇḍalam tathā prānta  va tejasya ṣoḍhaṃ nyasya tathaiva ca tudvāvetau nayanau deva candrādityāvabhāsakau kumārikākhaṇḍatathā caiva kalā proktā mahendrasya tu mastakam etat karṇadvaya deva savyāsavyau udāhṛtau dve kalānte vilomena nāsādvārayutāvubhau mahendrādya dvayaṃ pātyaṃ mukhagaṇḍasthalāvubhau rāvaṇāntau vilomena adhove dantapaṃktiṣu rājendrādyaṃ dvayaṃ ceṣṭau adha ūdhve subhāvite girijāsanamuddhṛtya brahmarandhre maheśvara tasyādyaṃ yad visargākhyaṃ jihvāmūla vidhīyate akārādivisargāntaṃ svaracakramiti smṛtam brahmāṇī devatā tatra saṃsthitā śambhumaṇḍale athāṅgāni vadedānīṃ śṛṇu tathyaṃ svarūpataḥ dvijāsana prabhu pātya tena skandhaṃ tu dakṣiṇam siṃhasya āsanaṃ bāhu āsanādyaṃ ca kūrparam hanumanta śira pātyaṃ dakṣahasta tadopari siṃhāntaṃ ghāntara tasmād dakṣahastanakhāgragam kavarga pañcadhā deva māheśvarya samāyutam śaktipurasya bimbasya yadādya skandhamuttamam tathā tasya śira pātyaṃ vāmabāhuniyojitam kumārikākhaṇḍabhaśira kūrpara caiva ā ādyaṃ karapṛṣṭhagammāyādyaṃ ca karāṃgulyo  nakhāgreṣu ca vinyaset cavarga caiva kaumārya tava deva prakāśitam gauryāyā ādimaṃ kārya dakṣiṇe ca sthira kuru tasyāsana dakṣata rudra adho jānujaṅghayoḥ ḍakārādya gata pādaṃ dakṣiṇetalapṛṣṭhagam tadgrahaṃ cāṃgulīyojya  nakhāstathā vai kaulika ṭavarga vaiṣṇavīsāra dakṣamārge virājate pṛthivyādhaḥ sphijavāma nīrādhaścoruka bhavet mahāśaṅkhāsanaṃ jānu jaṃghāyā ca gata smṛtam tathā dhūmradhvajasyādhaḥ pādapṛṣṭhamadha  smṛtam anaṅgaśiramāśritya pādāṃgulyo nakhāgrataḥ vārāhyādhiṣṭhita  varga vinyaset kramapaddhatau evaṃ varṇodaye pā pārravadakṣiṇakukṣigam nacāntaragataḥ kukṣau tadanye sarvatomukhaḥ ṣaśira pṛṣṭivaṃśe tu sṛgūdhvamudara viduḥ tadagatānta  mahādeva hṛdaya śabdarāśikam indrāṇyadhiṣṭhita varga hṛdayaṃ kulayoginīṃ tvaca kapālamūdhvastha śoṇitaṃ jaṭāhārādi anantaragata māṃsa anaṅgādhaḥ sthitaṃ snāyu catvāro vyāpakāstattvā āgneyā ravimaṇḍale viddhi tattvaṃ yavargeda svapiṇḍakalayojitam kumārikākhaṇḍatathā majjā phakārāntā harādhaḥ śukramaṇḍalam  evaṃ śiraṃ kuverasya taccāsthiviniyojitammadhyasthaṃ madhya  prāṇa pāyutattvamadhomukham cāmuṇḍādhiṣṭhita vargaṃ aṣṭamaṃ parisaṃkhyayā vargātītamadhaḥsthaṃ tu visargasahitātmakam pratimāyā gataṃ deva kopasthānagataṃ viduḥ tasya sā navamī devyā mahālakṣmyadhikāriṇī amṛtādihakārānta para varṇaparigraham mātṛkākramameva tu bhagajāta tu pratyayam evaṃ pañcāśadbhirbhedairādikṣāntaṃ krameṇa tu etadakṣaravinyāsa pūrvasaṃskārasaṃskṛtam varṇabījakramanyāsa avijñāta na muñcati śabdabrahmākṣarā yānti mālinyā śabdarāśyā tu otaprota jagatrayam kumārikākhaṇḍaḥdīpanena vinirmukta antaḥśūnya maheśvara tasmāt tacchabdarāśyādau dīpanaṃ samudāharet yānujaṃ kharamadhyasthaṃ gajendrabhujabheditam candrakāntiśikhābhinnaṃ hṛdayaṃ kulakhecarī bīje bīje pṛthak deva kṛtvādau vīravigraham sudīptaṃ bhavate nyāsaṃ mālinīpraṇavatraye ādyante saṃpuṭa kṛtvā śabdarāśyāmanena tu tathā saṃpuṭitaṃ nyāsaṃ nyaset vaktrāṅgasaṃyutam vṛṣabhaṃ madhyagaṃ gṛhya śaktyāsanavyavasthitam saṃvarta ca mahākālaṃ pinākī tadadhasthitam etat kūṭaṃ samākhyātaṃ ṣaḍvidhaṃ kārayet punaḥ hrasvaiḥ ṣaḍbhiḥ svarairbhedya indubinduralaṃkṛtamūdhvamūdhve tathā pūrve paścime dakṣiṇottare vaktranyāsa mahādeva pūrvabījaiḥ pradīpitam tūṣṇīśaṃ ca kulīśa ca śrīkaṇṭhāghorabhairavam uttareśa anantīśaṃ paścimena sadāśivam bete siddhā niyuktavyā vaktraṣaṭke varānana athāṅgāni pravakṣyāmi saṃkṣepeṇa vadāmyaham vṛṣabhaṃ madhyamaṃ sthāpya harasyāsanabheditam atādiṣu sutaṃ kuryāt hṛcchireṇa vibheditam nīlakaṇṭhaśiraṃ kṛtvā kūṭeda ṣaḍvidhoddharet dīrdhaiḥ ṣaḍbhi svarairbhinna kalābinduśivāṅkitam kumārikākhaṇḍaaghoraṃ hṛdi saṃyukta amoghaṃ śirabhūṣaṇam nīlakaṇṭha śikhā yojya varmasthamekavīrakam piṅgalaṃ netraryonyasya kapilās ca bhairavam evaṃ tu bhairavai  ṣaḍbhiryuktā aṅgāni vinyaset dīpanādya tataḥ kṛtvā bhavennyāsa tu saṃpuṭam saṃpuṭena tu riktāṅgā antaḥśūnyā gabhastayaḥ vyāpakatvena tiṣṭhanti sudīptā kumārikākhaṇḍamadhyamaṃ ca ananṅgaṃ ca agnidhāmavibheditam khaśiraṃ khaśirākrāntaṃ kapālāsanamaṇḍalam ra eva vedhakākrāntaṃ varṇādyasya tu mastakam ekapādasthitaṃ śambho tathā vai merumadhyagam kāntayukta maheśāna tṛtīya padamuddhṛtam napūrvādyantādha saṃstha yaḍhānta bhānuditam haśiraṃ paṅkajasthaṃ tu ghādhaḥstha māyayā yutam caturthapadamākhyātaṃ pañcamaṃ cādhunā bhavet mādyaṃ gaurīsamāyukta tathā caiva bhānāntagam jāsanaṃ īśvarākrāntaṃ rāvāntaṃ rādhagaṃ ca i vādyaṃ caivaikavīraṃ tu dvirabhyāsena ṣaṣṭhamam ghanāntaṃ māyayā sārdhaṃ anaṅgāsanamaṇḍalam dvāvetau ca dvirabhyāsāt padameva tu saptamam sayāntaṃ ca dvidhābhūta ekāreṇa dvitīyakam aṣṭamaṃ padamevaṃ tu ṭhaantaṃ paṅkajasthitam kumārikākhaṇḍavargātītaṃ tu sabhinnaṃ dvidhābhūtaṃ niyojayet navamaṃ padamākhyātaṃ visargasthāgnidhāmakam kevalaṃ tu dvirabhyāsa daśamaṃ padamuddhṛtam viccekādaśameva tu padakramakrameṇa tu vāgbhava māyayā sārdhaṃ tathā prasādabhairavam ādyamante kṛtaṃ deva uddhṛtā ca parāparā pracatvāriṃśatī proktā tasyāmāsanapakṣakam vidyā parāparā hyeṣā ādhārāt tu vinirgatā eṣāsanaṃ kramasyokta āsanaṃ na mṛgājinam vidyārūḍhaṃ kṛtātmāna aparāṃ ca samabhyaset māyāpiṇḍaṃ sapheraṃ tu rāvasyodhvamadhaḥ kṛtam evaṃ trirakṣarā vidyā ādimena tu yojitā ādimaṃ tu yadā cānte tadā sārdhaṃ pada bhavet adhyuṣṭā jvalikā devī vidyā aparabhairavī eṣā vai mūrtipakṣasya anāhatavinirgatā tasyodhva paramaṃ śambho pakṣaṃ tu jagataḥ pṛthuḥtava caikākṣarā vidyā sā ca pañcaprakārataḥ kumārikākhaṇḍamerukarṇikayā jvālā śaṅkhamastakabheditā kuverāsanamūdhve tu visargāntamiti smṛtam eṣā sā bhagavatī devī nāmnā sā vahnivāsinī ekākārā parā mātā viśvamātā pratiṣṭhitā śambhumārge sthitā vidyā śāmbhavīsṛṣṭirūpataḥ tadadhaḥsthāsana mārga sūkṣmaṃ hṛdayavallabham tasyāsana paraṃ nātha tat śāktamiti kaulikam śāktaśāmbhavayormadhye āṇava nāma pakṣakam aetat trikaṇṭaka mūlaṃ nyastvā kṣobho vijāyate mālinyā śabdarāśestu etad vidyākramatrayam abdaikena tu abhyāsāt parāvasthā pravartate ye yoginīkule jātā teṣā tuṣṭā hyahaṃ purā te jñāsyanti trike bhedān śabdarāśisamāyutān  pañcāśadrudraracita sthānavarṇaparigraham etad deva paraṃ guhyaṃ nyāsaṃ tridaśapūjitam trīṇi vidyāstrisiddhāśca tripīṭha ca tridevatam trīṇi vṛkṣā guhāstrīṇi  triśaktirguṇamujjvalā trināḍimārgagaṃ jñātvā vidyātritayamāruhet ityādyāvatāre mahāmanthānabhairavayajñe anvaye saptakoṭipramāṇe merumārgavinirgatelakṣapādādhike vidyāpīṭhamārge vimalaṣaṭkanirṇaye kādibhede ājñāpārameśvaresvāminīmate śrīcaturviṃśatsahasrasaṃhitāyāṃ devyākramabhāṣitetrividyādhikāro nāmānandaḥ ekaviṃśānandaḥśrīvakrā uvācaathānya pravakṣyāmi aghorāṣṭakamuttamam gamāgamena kartavyaṃ śivena tu puṭīkṛtam padabhedakrama śambho idānīṃ kathayāmyaham aghoreti padaṃ pūrvaṃ aghoyīī dvitīyakam eṣā sā prathamā ghorā dvitīyā ca yathā bhavet paramaghoreti padaṃ paramaghoyīī param ghorarūpe havisarga ghorarūpā ī cāntagam tṛtīyāghorikā proktā caturthī tvathavā śṛṇu ghoramukhi ghoramukhā īkārasvarabheditam bhīmabhīṣaṇīti pada aparaṃ bhīmabhīṣaṇā gauryā caturthikā gauryā pañcamā ca maheśvara vama piva heti padaṃ vama piva hāyīsaṃyutaṃ ṣaṣṭhīyaṃ kathitāghorā aparā saptamā bhavet ruruśabda raraścaiva ruruśabda raraḥ punaḥ akārasthāstvime rephā gauryāyākṣaradīpitāḥ eṣā sā saptamā ghoyī aṣṭamā cādhunā bhavet phetkārī caiva phetkārya caturthasvarabheditā aghoryaṣṭakametad hi padaṣoḍaśabhedataḥ dvipadakramayogena kathitaṃ ghorikāṣṭakam kumārikākhaṇḍadīpanaistu vinirmukta aghoryādyaṣṭakoddhṛtam na tu siddhiprada deva bījahīnaṃ na sādhayet tasmāt sabījakaraṇa idānīṃ śṛṇu bhairava mātṛkākramaliṅgasya pūrṇimānalabheditam gauryāyāmalamākrāntaṃ ājñāvartisamujjvalam etad bījaṃ mahendrasya tathā prasādabhairavam tasyānte madhyagaṃ pātyaṃ mahendraśirabheditam śaktitomaramāviṣṭaṃ adhikārārṇabheditam tatpadastha visargasthaṃ vyomabījaṃ maheśvara bavilomāccaturtha tu toraṇaśirabheditam tasyādhasthastathā codhvaṃ candrāsana susasthitam tasyodhve tu punaḥ kṣobha saṃyogād rāvabījakam vakārasya makārasya antasthaṃ ca samuddharet kuberāsanamāviṣṭa bindubhinnagurūpari eṣaiva kaulinībījaṃ surasiddhanamaskṛtam  prathamādi caturthaṃ tu agnivedhakabheditam śaśāṅkāṃkitabindūdhve ṣaṭyāgāt saptame hitam eṣa kālāgnirudrastu proktaḥ sarvajanapriyaḥ kumārikākhaṇḍabhalamadhyamaka nātha bādyenāhata auśiram bindunādakalākrāntaṃ mahārudrapuroddhṛtam anya dhūmradhvajasyādyaṃ toraṇāsanabheditam toraṇa śiracandrā ānanda ca akhaṇḍitam yoginībījarājāna rāvāvasthottamottamam etad bījāṣṭakaṃ kuryād ghoryāyā aṣṭakasyatu padānāṃ ṣoḍaśānāṃ tu bījānyaṣṭau dvidhā kuru avasāne padānāṃ tu te bījā ṣoḍaśa smṛtāḥ bhaviṣyanti ca deveśa ādyantaśivayojitāḥ prasādasya tu jīvasya śiraṃ kṛtvā caturdaśam bhavate śivarājāna kṛtvā nyāsa samārabhet padābhyā jānujaṅghābhyāṃ ādhāre hṛdi maṇḍale kukṣibhyāṃ pṛṣṭhavaṃśe ca tathā bāhudvaye punaḥ vaktramaṇḍalamevaṃ tu aṣṭasthāneṣu vinyaset saṃhāra pūrvataḥ kṛtvā tataḥ sṛṣṭikramaṃ punaḥ  aghoyadyātmaka nyāsaṃ trikaṇṭāvaraṇoddhṛtam kathitaṃ tava deveśa puryaṣṭakasamāyutam śabda sparśaca rūpa ca raso gandhaśca pañcamaḥ amano buddhirahaṃkāra puryaṣṭakamiti smṛtam brahmāṇyādevatādyaṣṭau catuḥṣaṣṭistu saṃkhyayā evaṃ vyāptikrameṇaiva aghoryaṣṭaka vinyaset kumārikākhaṇḍaatha vidyākramaṃ nyāsaṃ siddhagāṅgasamāyutam karanyāsakrameṇaiva pūrva yat khyāpitaṃ mayā sāmprataṃ bījavinyāsa tathā vai pīṭhapañcakam visargādyaṃ mahāvarṇaṃ pañcadhā kārayet svaram mahadbhūtamataḥ  kṛtvā dīrghapaṅkajabheditam kalābindvaṅkitaṃ deva etad vai bījapañcakam  vinyastavyaṃ hi devyāyāstattvapañcakasaṃyutam pṛthivī śaktibījaṃ tu āpo vai somabījakam tejo vai sūryabījaṃ tu vāyurve bindubījakam ākāśaṃ nādabīja tu etad vai bījapañcakam teṣāṃ sthānāni vai pañca guruvaktre pratiṣṭhitāḥ pṛthivī kandacakre tu āpo vai yonimaṇḍale tejo vai nābhicakrasthaṃ vāyurhṛdayamaṇḍale ākāśaṃ ca bhruvormadhye bījasthānāni pañca ca bījabījāśramāḥ pañca kṛtvā ādyena saṃyutam labdhvā gurūpadeśaṃ tu nyastavyaṃ bījapañcakam anyathā na bhavevasthā bījahīnā ca sundara pṛthivyādiṣu tattveṣu bandha cāstamana bhavet kumārikākhaṇḍasadābhyāsena kaulesmin punarjanma kuto bhavet etadunmanīkaraṇa nyāseda bījapañcakam tattvānāṃ pañcakaṃ deva adhikārakrame sthitam upadeśe bhavedeva nyāseda pīṭhapañcakam uktā ye pūrvaṃ te pañca praṇavāni samabhyaset teṣāmagre tu pīṭhāni kṛtvā nyāsa samārabhet uttaraṃ pūrvapīṭhaṃ tu pañcamādyantabhūṣitam bhrūmadhye kṛṣṇavaṇabhaṃ tathā jālandharaṃ punaḥ dvitīyādyantarūpaṃ tu ārakta hṛdi maṇḍale tathā pūrṇagirinama tṛtīyādyantaropitam pītavarṇaṃ ca nābhistha kāmarūpa tathāparam prathamādyantamadhyastha himakundenduguhyataḥ tisrove pañcamaṃ pīṭhaṃ caturthādyantayojitam haritaṃ tanmahāraudraṃ kandasthāne prakāśitam udaya kāmarūpetu sthiti pūrṇagirya saṃhāra dakṣiṇe pīṭhe nirvāṇaṃ pañcame sthitam viśrāmamādyapīṭhe tu nyāsedaṃ pīṭhapañcakam yathā dhyānaṃ tu pīṭhānāṃ kāmarūpādi bhairava tathā krameṇa tattvānāṃ kuryād vai dhyānapañcakam yathā tattvāni bījāni tathā vai pīṭhapañcakam kumārikākhaṇḍasabāhyābhyantaraṃ jñātvā ko na muñcati bandhanāt pīṭhanyāse kṛte deva kiñcit paśyanti yoginaḥ adṛṣṭamaṇḍale deva akhaṇḍapuramaṇḍalam tatra sā kaulinī vidyā antaḥkaraṇabheditā tattvānāṃ cādhikāra tu pratyaya tu yadā bhavet tasmāt nyāsavaraṃ proktaṃ yat surairapi durlabham ākhyātaṃ tava siddhasya siddhamārge prasiddhakam ityādyāvatāre mahāmanthānabhairavayajñe anvaye saptakoṭipramāṇe merumārgavinirgatelakṣapādādhike ādyapīṭhāvatārite vidyāpīṭhamārge vimalaṣaṭkanirṇaye kādibhedeājñāpārameśvare svāminīmate śrīcaturviṃśatsahasrasaṃhitāyā avvākramabhāṣite tattvapañcakāravarṇane kramodayo nāmānandaḥ dvāviṃśānandaḥśrīvakrā uvācaataḥ paraṃ pravakṣyāmi nyāsaṃ tridaśapūjitam ṣoḍhā dvādaśabhedena nyāsaṃ kuryād gamāgame ṣoḍhā śakti samākhyātā parā ekākṣarā śubhā tasyāsana ṣoḍhāsaṃjñā ṣoḍhāśaktipuraṃ viśet tasya te ṣoḍaśo bhedā  śṛṇu mārgeṇa sundara jaṭāhāra gauryā sthāpya dvādaśadhā punaḥ bindunā bhedita kṛtvā candrārkaśirasāhatam tasyāṅgā dvādaśale khyātācchāyācchatramanukramāt siṃhāsanaṃ tu prathama cādyāsana dvitīyakam tṛtīyaṃ hyekavīra syāt caturthaṃ haramaṇḍale pañcamaṃ śaktibījaṃ tu makārāsana ṣaṣṭhakam saptamaṃ jilabhāgasya aṣṭamaṃ haramastakam haśiraṃ navamaṃ deva daśama tāraṇaṃ śiraḥ rājyamekādaśaṃ ceti dvādaśa tārakaṃ nyaset vedhake vedhayet sarvān ekavīreṇa bhūṣitān candrajyotikalāśuddhāḥ rudradvādaśabheditāḥ punareva hi deveśa gaurya dvādaśabhiḥ punaḥ rudraśaktisamāyogāt ṣoḍhānyāsaṃ mamākṛtiḥ na tasyā dīpanaṃ kiñcid gauryādvādaśadīpitā eṣā vai rudraśaktistu ṣoḍhāśaktirnapuṃsakā  kumārikākhaṇḍatasyā dvādaśadhānyāsaṃ ādau sṛṣṭikrameṇa tu paścāt kuryādaṅganyāsaṃ gamāgamamiti smṛtam kopasthāne ca netrābhyāṃ karṇanāsāpuṭāvubhau kaṇṭhe ca hṛdaye nābhau yonau ādhāramaṇḍale ṣoḍhānyāsa krameṇokta gauryākādirgamaḥ smṛtaḥ āga sṛṣṭibījādau indubinduvikāsitam makārādikrameṇaiva gamāgame padadvayam sadā nyastena deveśa maṇḍalāgre kramāgrataḥ varṣaikena ca abhyāsāt divyājñā saṃpravartate dvādaśābde tu saṃprāpte pāṣāṇānapi vedhayet cūrṇayet parvataśṛṃgān mudrāsphoṭānyanekaśaḥ kurute vividhāñścaryān ājñāveśaprabhāvataḥ yaṃ sovalokayejjantuḥ pāśānāṃ vajrapañjaram taṃ tu saṃśodhayet śaktyā kalisyā sādhayet priya vidyāsiṃhāsaneda tu nyastvā śakti pravartate kālāntarād guṇotpattimacirāllabhate dhruvam gurorvaktraṃ ca nirvāṇaṃ tathā dvātriṃśadakṣarā ājñā sā ca krame guroradhikāra samārabhet vidyātritayasaṃyukta maṇḍalaṃ devatākramam tathā ca dvādaśa ślokā ulitritayanirṇayam kumārikākhaṇḍajñātvā tu prathamaṃ deva citra damayate tataḥ mantrapādena caikena vidyāpādārdhameva ca mudrā caivāṣṭabhāgena gurupādaikasaṃjñaka nirvāṇe ca niraṃśe ca tadā siddhi labhennaraḥ etat pūrvakramaṃ jñātvā paścāt ṣoḍhā samabhyaset tacca dvādaśabhirbhedaiḥ siṃhāsana samuddhṛtam tasyaiva nāyakī vidyā parā caikākṣarā bhavet merumadhye va kauleśa  kapālāsanasaṃsthitaḥ tuadhaḥ sṛṣṭisamāyuktaḥ trayodaśavibhūṣitaḥ visargasthā parā hyeṣā plutasvaravivarjitā napuṃsakapadenaiva na strīkāraṇapuṃgavam tasyādhikāramāyāta śrīmaccandrapure gṛhe pāramparyopadeśa tu tasyādhyātmikanirṇayam ādau sā sakalā proktā kūṭabhūtā hyadhomukhī himakundendudhavalā śravamāṇā manonmanā kopānte vinyased deva siṃharūpakrameṇa  tu na cāsyā dīpanaṃ deya svabhāvenaiva dīpitā lakṣajāpād bhavet siddhistato yāti parāṃ gatim ityādyāvatāre manthānabhairavayajñe anvaye saptakoṭipramāṇe merumārgavinirgatelakṣapādādhike vidyāpīṭhamārge vimalaṣaṭkanirṇaye kādibhede ājñāpārameśvare svāminīmate śrīcaturviṃśatsahasrasahitāyā avvākrama bhāṣite ṣoḍhādhikāravarṇane kramodayo nāmānandaḥ śrīvakrā uvācatrayoviṃśānandaḥadhunā tadgrahaṃ vakṣye vidyātritayabheditam vargāṣṭakavidhānena amūlāt tu vinirgatam a ana a iti padaṃ pūrva ā tha gho tu dvitīyakam i ṝ re tṛtīyaṃ syāt ī ṝ hrī caturthakam u ḷ pa pañcamaṃ syāt ū lṛ ra ṣaṣṭha smṛtam ṝ ca ma saptamaṃ caiva aṣṭamaṃ ṝ dha gho iti lṛ ṇa re navame datta lṛ u hrauṃ daśamaṃ smṛtam e ū gho daśamekaṃ ca ai ī ramiti dvādaśam o baru trayodaśa au ka peti caturdaśam aṃ kha haḥ tripañcamaṃ ca aḥ ga gho iti ṣoḍaśaḥ ka gha ra saptadaśa ca khaṅa mu ca daśāṣṭakam ga i khi ūnaviṃśañca gha a bhī iti viṃśamam ṅa va ma ekaviṃśa ca ca bha bhī dvayaviṃśamam cha ya ṣa trayoviṃśaṃ ja ḍha ṇi caturviṃśakam jha ḍa va pañcaviṃśañca ña ṭha ma ṣaḍviṃśamam ṭa jha va saptaviṃśañca ṭha ña ma cāṣṭaviṃśam ḍa aḥ pi ūnatriṃśeti ḍha ṭa va triṃśamaṃ padam ṇa ra pi ekatriṃśañca ta ja va dvayatriṃśamam thapa heti trayastriṃśam de sa he catustriṃśakam dhaharu pañcatriṃśañca na ccha ru ca ṣaṭtriṃśakam pa la ra saptatriṃśañca pha ā ra aṣṭatriṃśakam ba ṣa vi ūnacāriṃśa bhakṣa cce catvāriṃśatiḥ kumārikākhaṇḍama ma aiṃ ekacāriṃśa ya śa hrī dvicatvāriṃśam ra a hūṃ tricatvāriṃśa la ta hrīṃ catuścāriṃśam va e aiṃ pañcacāriṃśa śa ai hrīṃ ṣaṭcatvāriṃśam ṣa o aiṃ saptacāriṃśa sa au kṣaṃ aṣṭacāriṃśam ha da hrī ūnapañcāśat pha hasrauṃ śatārdhakam pañcāśatpadasaṃyogāt saṃgraheṇa tu tadgraham śabdarāśikrameṇaiva nyāsaṃ kuryācca tadgrahe bhaved divyatanurmayo asya nyāsasya sevanāt ṣaṇmāsāt paṭhite siddhiḥ athavābdena niścayāt śastraghātairna bhidyeta acchidra vajrayoginaḥ kṛtvādau rāvabījaṃ tu padasyānte tathā punaḥ rāvabījapuṭāntastha vidyātritayabhedataḥ sudīpta tadgraha tasmād bījarikta parāṃmukham paradehād viniṣkrāntaṃ yoginīmukhasaṃcayam evaṃ tadgrahakṣetraṃ tu vidhānavadaśeṣataḥ evaṃ vai kulasaṃcāra kulācāre pratiṣṭhitam yasyedaṃ vaktragaṃ nyāsaṃ sopi śāntapade sthitaḥ pūrvābhyastaṃ na saṃdehoṃ anyāyaṃ na pravartate śrīvakrā uvācapunaranyaṃ pravakṣyāmi nyāsaṃ tu samayakramampadabhedakrameṇaiva vidyā pīṭheśvarī bhavet kumārikākhaṇḍacce vi ceti padaṃ pūrvaṃ ṇiki ṇiki ca dvitīyakam ccha ra ī ca sacandrārdha ccha ra ā sārdhacandramā ubhayostṛtīya regho virabhaiyemasa punaḥ gala ū saśaśi kṛtvā caturthapadamuddhṛtam kahaśabda dvirabhyāsa saṃyogāt padaṣaṣṭhamam sahaśabda dvirabhyāsa devatāṣṭapada smṛtam hara au candraśūnyasthaṃ dvidhābhūtaṃ navamaṃ smṛtam ṇikako dvipañca ca ṇikako daśaikādhikam haśakti  śūnyacandrārdhaṃ kalā rephaṃ ca candramā gauryā śūnyaṃ kramādekapiṇḍamevaṃ tu dvādaśam menaṇañaṅa padaṃ tu idameva  trayodaśam haragaurī śaśi śūnyaṃ harā śūnyaṃ ca maulinī caturdaśapadaṃ khyātaṃ khimurāgho a eva ca pañcadaśa  samākhyātaṃ rāva reghoa ṣoḍaśam reghora saptadaśa syāt re rā rā ca daśāṣṭamam kebjiku hasau viṃśeti śrīṃ hrīṃ aiṃ pada viṃśamam siṃhakrameṇa vākhyātaṃ aiṃkārādi anukramāt udaya sūryamārgeṇa somamārgeṇa rodhanam candrasūryakrameṇaiva varṇaiśca catuḥṣaṣṭibhiḥ samayākhyā kule kaule ādime nāma yojita ādyantena samāyuktā bījayuktā manonmanā sā ca pīṭheśvarī māyā samayā kulamālinī kumārikākhaṇḍaḥsā dīptā bījasaṃyuktā bījariktā  adīpitā mahāneṣādhikārī yaḥ sevyamānā sa siddhyati bījeścaturdaśai   proktā koṃkaṇā jvalabhūṣitā lakṣaikena tū tarpayet tataḥ samayalopād mucyeta tejaścāyu parākramam vartate jñānasadbhāva yoginīkulamelakam  labhate samayāyukto vīradravyaṃ caruṃ tathā prāśanād bhavate siddhiḥ anyathā maraṇaṃ bhavet nirviśaṅke guruvaktraprasādataḥ prāśanāt kaulikī siddhirnirvikalpasya nānyathā nyāsaṃ vidyādhunā vakṣye sṛṣṭinyāyena kaulikam ādyārṇasaptakarepha tṛtīyakaṃ cakṣuṣe kopā ca vinyaset rārākarṇaubhayordeva cibuke nyasya ñakāra kaṇṭhamekhalā mekāraṇakāra cakrakādyāhṛdayātmāna iti galamekhalā hūṃkāra prāṇamadhyataḥ koṃkaṇi stanayoretat trikamevānuvinyaset koṃkaṇa udare nyasya ikāra nābhimaṇḍalehrauṃ hrauṃ  karayoḥ kahau hasaśabda tu pṛṣṭhataḥ hasaśabdānvitaṃ caiva skandhayoḥ kaha vinyaset kahānyaṃ bāhuyugme tu glakāra yonimaṇḍale sahaśabda karābhyāṃ tu samayeti karāṃgulī bhairavīti tathāghore cchā ccha ūrukayugmake  kiṇīti jānujaṅghābhyāṃ kiṇi pādadvaye nyaset vicce pādāṃgulīprānte vāgbhavaṃ vaktramadhyataḥ yatra sthānāt samārabhya kṛtaṃ nyāsaṃ ca vidyayā pādāntāt punastatraiva uccāro yatra tallayaḥ udayāstamameva tu pu parigīyate eṣā sā samayā vidyā apasavyād vinirgatā tadgrahasya tu kṣetrasya eṣā evādhikāriṇī kumārikākhaṇḍaḥvidyānyāsena siddhyeta kūṭenaiva vidhānataḥ pañcopacārapūjāyāṃ maṇḍalāgre gurogrataḥvidyāpīṭhethavā cakre yatra kramāgrataḥkramāgrataḥ kṛtam tatra tasya mahāvasthāpratyaya kaulikaṃ bhavet tasya devyāśca kāruṇyaṃ kurute svapnadarśanam sarvadvandvavinirmukta acirāt khecaraṃ padam ityādyāvatāre mahāmanthānabhairavayajñe anvaye saptakoṭipramāṇe merumārgavinirgatelakṣapādādhike vidyāpīṭhamārge vimalaṣaṭkanirṇaye kādibhede ājñāpārameśvare svāminīmateśrīcaturviṃśatsahasrasaṃhitāyāṃ avākramabhāṣite tadgrahasamayavidyādhikāravarṇanakramonāmānandaḥ caturviṃśānandaśrīnātha uvācaśrutaṃ vakre mayā vākyaṃ kumārīkhaṇḍanāyike kathaṃ sā mātṛkā nāma ślokadvādaśabheditā  na jñātā ca mayā devi ślokārthaṃ kathaya sphuṭam śrīvakrā uvācamahānandavikāsena yat tvayā pṛcchitā hyaham tatsarvaṃ kathayiṣyāmi mātṛkākramanirṇayam yosau parāparonantaḥ vibhuḥ kāraṇamavyayaṃ praśāntamaparaṃ nāma śāntātītamanāmayam pūrvasaṃkṛtyamākāraṃ bhairavasya maheśvara kalpe parāmpare pūrvaṃ manvantaraśatairapi yugaiścaturaśītiḥ pāṣaṇavat yā tu saṃsthitā ekāhaṃ bhairave yajñe bhairava tvamahaṃ punaḥ na strī na puruṣākāraṃ nākāraṃ vi kvacit śūnyākāre tamaikatve ramaṇānandacetasam śamana kulasaṃkāśaṃ kiñcijjānāmyahaṃ hara na vācā śruticakṣubhyāṃ na ca buddhyāmyaha hara kaivalyānandamāhlāda saṃvatantaṃ śatārdhakam tasyecchā kiñciccinmātraṃ avyakta vyaktirūpiṇam tadāha  vismayamāpannā kimidaṃ śūnyarūpakam kumārikākhaṇḍaiti matvā gahana ghoraṃ bhītāhaṃ suptacetasā praviṣṭā bhairave yajñe sthitāhaṃ pararūpataḥ paramāṇusvarūpeṇa kiñcidrūpaṃ ca siṃhakam siṃhasaṃvartaka nātha vyāvṛtaṃ tamasākulam akulādikula caiva vyākulaṃ kulakaulikam kalanāt dhvaninādāntaṃ tannāda pañcadhāgatam tacca ca varṇāditattvaṃ ca kalānāṃ ca mahodayam kalāḍhya ca tathā śānta savisargādi cālayam mahogra kālika rāvaṃ rūpākhyaṃ ca tathāparam kulāvalitayogena vinyaset kulapaddhatim dvādaśāni tu ślokāni karṇāt karṇagatāni ca sadoccāraprayogena gṛhṇate sādhakottamaḥ tasya deyamida  jñānaṃ anyathā na kadācana pañcapraṇavasaṃghātaiḥ sāmānyaireva bhairava haṃsākhyairmahatairdivyaiḥ parāmūrtiradhiṣṭitaiḥ uddhared dvādaśa ślokān ṣaṭkūṭādhiṣṭhitān śubhān catvāraḥ ṣoḍaśairbhedaistathā ṣaṭ nabhāntare sṛṣṭimadhyagatā ye ca hakṣasthā dvayabhedataḥ kathaṃ yugmaṃ kathākhyaṃ ca anaṅgaṃ sṛṣṭisaṃyutam tadadho hanumān nātha rāvamārgasamanvitam kumārikākhaṇḍagajendraśirasākrāntaṃ bindunādakalāṅkitamājñājyotisamāyukta ślokadvādaśanirṇaye dvitīyamakṣara proktaṃ tṛtīyaṃ tu yathā bhavet vyomabinduśirobhinnanādaśaktikalāyuktaṃ mahogramiti kathyate amṛtaṃ sravamāṇa ca śāntayuktaṃ samuccaret dvirabhyāsa mahāśambho yāvad vai mātṛkākṣaram agnivedhakabheditam etad vinyāsavijñānaṃ paramaṃ devadurlabham kulāvalitayogena uddhāya kulapaddhatiḥ sahitārthamida satyaṃ akathyaṃ tava darśitam yosau parāparo devo bhairavo bhavacchedakaḥ tasya icchā hyanāmākhyā kiñciccetā cinoti yat sā ca vai vyāpakatvena saṃpūrṇa kaulinī parā amā sūkṣmā anāmā ca nirānande layaṃgatā  sā ca vai bhairavī śāntā anantena vibhājitā tasmānmanthānabhedena bheditaṃ ca parāparam evaṃ sṛṣṭigatānaṅga anaṅgaṃ kāmanāśanam tacca haṃsa mahātmāna jvalanādamṛtodbhavam kumārikākhaṇḍadvāvetau śivaśaktyākhyau otaprota jagatrayam etad rahasyamākhyātaṃ mahāmanthānasaṃjñayā śrīnātha uvācakathaṃ nāthe kā me saṃjñā kutrotpattau nirāmaye vyākulohaṃ samutpanno niḥsaṃdigdha vadasva me śrīvakrā uvāca sarahasyaṃ kṛtaṃ praśna amoghājñā kuleśvara kathayāmi na saṃdeho icchā kāmadugdhāṃ kalām yathāhaṃ cidghanānandā ānandatanutāṃ gatā tena tṛptiḥ purāsmāka bhavate pṛthivī hara pṛthivyāha tva mahacchabda śabdabrahmākṣarāṇi ca sā ca śrīśāmbhavecchākhyā suśāntamiti lakṣaṇam ahaṃ kācit kalā kālī vikalā kulaśāmbhavī icchā hyahaṃ parotpannā avyaktā vyaktarūpiṇī kulālī kulakauleśī akulādvyāpakī bhavet vyāpakatvena rūpeṇa saṃyogādupajāyate saṃyogena tu saṃvatī nirāvartīt pravartitā prathamaṃ ca anāmākhyaṃ nityaṃ ca śiraśekharam mahābhairavajyotiśca vyāpakaṃ paścime gṛhe eva ṣaṭkakrama tva hi vidyā vyomena veṣṭitā kumārikākhaṇḍaudaya vimalaṃ nāma amṛta bindubhairavam saṃyogena samutpannā tadānte dvādaśa  smṛtāḥ mama mūrtigatā kuryāt sṛṣṭihetūpalakṣaṇām ahaṃ sā ca parā caikā aparā siddhisāgaresāgara manmatha nāma kulākulakulāntagam  trikulaṃ trīṇi tattvāni tridhā mantrī ca śaktayaḥ trīṇi siddhāstrayastrotastritattva tripathāntaram tatparaṃ ca mahāsthānaṃ mayā vyāptaṃ tu sāgaram sāgara śaśisūryantaṃ akhaṇḍamiti maṇḍalam akhaṇḍamapara caiva anantaścākṣayaṃ tathā akulaṃ pañcamaṃ nātha vijñeyā kulabhūṣaṇā evaṃ nādaḥ samutpannaḥ pañcadhā tu kramāgataḥ kramāt sṛṣṭi sthitā yonau ekā eva hyadhomukhī sadbhāva sā mahāmūrtijyotirūpā manonmanī unmanā manavegena śakti kuṇḍalinī kalā amā nāma kalā kālī sthitāhatāca bhairava asyāścaivāsana pātraṃ iḍānāmena gīyate iḍā sā bhairavī śāntā  śaktipātramudāhṛtā udaya śaśibimbasya sūryaṃ muñcati bhāsvaram tacca bindu ghana ghoraṃ ghargharāmṛtasaṃbhavam śāmbhavaṃ ṣaṭkabhedena kalā kalati kaulinī maphrekhasaharāveṇa sthitāgniprakṛtirūpiṇī kumārikākhaṇḍasattvarajatamaikatve sthitā vyomāntavartinī vyomyāditattvasaṃghāta  tattvād varṇā hyajāyanta ākrāntāśca kalairjñeyā pañcakādisvabhāvataḥ pañca bhūtāḥ svarāḥ pañca sūkṣmaśāmbhavasaṃbhavāśāmbhava  sarahasyeda rephakhasahakārakam tasyaiva vaktramādyaṃ ca anāmānāmasaṃyutam yathā sṛṣṭikrameṇokta tathā śṛṇu maheśvara vyoma jīvasamāyuktaṃ vahnirardhīśasaṃyutaḥ anugrahaśirākrāntaṃ sūkṣmanādena bheditam binducandrakalākrānta akṣara bhairava hara śūnya khecarasaṃyukta pharamante samāśritam ekapādena saṃbhinnaṃ nādabindukalāṅkatam eṣā sā khecarīvidyā trailokyākarṣaṇī parā yasamadhyagataṃ devaṃ hadhamadhyagataṃ punaḥ ṇaṭamadhyagataṃ gṛhya tadantaragataṃ viduḥ gaurīśikharamākrāntaṃ indubindukalānvitam kathitā śāṅkarī vidyā tṛtīyā kulanāyikā caturthī māyayā nāma hara vyomāsanasthitāagnidhāmena saṃbhinnā i u  madhyagatena ca bindu  ardhakalāyuktā raudrarūpā ca ambikā kumārikākhaṇḍaakathyamātṛkā śakti  hasaphrekārabheditā nādabindukalāyuktā vāgbhavākārarūpiṇī kaulinī kulanāthānāṃ siddhānāṃ jñānabhūmikā śāmbhavāḥ praṇavāḥ pañca ṣaṣṭhaṃ caitanyamuttamam ṣaḍaṅgavaktrasaṃyuktā pūrṇā devī parāparā ṣaḍbījānukrameṇaiva uccared gurūpadeśata dviṣaṭkadivyayogena ślokadvādaśapaddhatim yo vetti mahatīṃ śambho ślokārthapadasaṃyutām sopi ekena janmena kaulikājñādharo bhavet yaṃ yaṃ spṛśati hastena yaṃ yaṃ paśyati cakṣuṣā yaṃ yaṃ smarati bhāvena sarva saṃpadyate kṣaṇāt duṣṭānyanekakrūrāṇi bhūcaroragarākṣasāḥ tasyālokanamātreṇa palāyanti daśo diśaḥ iti satyaṃ mayā proktaṃ ślokārthamatamuttamam ye nyasyanti trikālajñāste yānti paramāṃ gatim śrīvakrā uvācaatha cānyakramaṃ vakṣye ślokadvādaśake sthitāḥ dvādaśa siddhayoginyo abhidhānena tāḥśṛṇu kumārikākhaṇḍanandā bhadrā jayā kālī karālī vikṛtānanā kroṣṭukī bhīmabhadrā ca vāyuvegā hayānanā gambhīrā ghoṣaṇī caiva yoginyo dvādaśa smṛtāḥ kṛtvādau vāgbhavāstrīṇi ante tepi vilomataḥ saṃpuṭena yutā devyo dvādaśāṅgaprasiddhayenandā śirasi vinyasyā bhadrākhyā ca lalāṭake jayā ca dakṣiṇe netre kālī caiva ta vāmake tukarālī dakṣiṇe karṇe vāme ca vikṛtānanā kroṣṭukī  nāsikāgre tu bhīmarudrā tathā mukhe vāyuvegā gale caiva hṛdayasthā hayānā gambhīrā nābhimadhye tu ghoṣinyā guhyamadhyataḥ evaṃ nyāsaṃ tu devīnāṃ divyadehakaraṃ param etadāvaraṇaṃ nyāsaṃ dvādaśāṅgamudāhṛtam samayasya tu siṃhasya yoginyo dvādaśa smṛtāḥ etanyāsa purā kṛtvā yatra yatra vrajennaraḥ tatra tatra mahālābhaṃ jñānaṃ labhati puṣkalam melakaṃ yoginīsā guptānāṃ ca maheśvara dvādaśāṅgaprabhāvena jñānaṃ tāḥ kathayanti hi dadanti carukaṃ divyaṃ prasannāstvaritāṃ gatim divyarūpadharo yogī yadi gupto maheśvara punaranyakrama vakṣye nyāsaṃ kṣetraparigraham amṛtādi ca jīvāntaṃ hakṣasaṃjñāsamāyutam tāvannyāsa prakartavyaṃ śabdarāśikrameṇa tu upadeśa pravakṣyāmi paraṃ devyāḥ parigraham dīpanaṃ ca prakartavyaṃ varṇe varṇe pṛthak pṛthak hakṣa saṃjñādvayaṃ sthānaṃ prāṇa krodhaṃ ca khe balamkumārikākhaṇḍatābhyāṃ na dīpanaṃ deyaṃ svabhāvenaiva dīpitāḥ varṇadīptātmaka piṇḍaṃ ādikādikrameṇa tu ādikādikrama kṣetraṃ parādevīparigraham dīpamānandayoga ca śakterjñeya parigraham ādau vai svaracakraṃ tu tattvaṣoḍaśanirṇayam ye ca uktā kakārādyā jīvaṃ te  sarvadehinām visargeṇa tu niṣpatti etat kṣetraparigraham  krodhaḥ prāṇakalā coktā rudraśaktyā ca veṣṭitā tābhyāṃ saṃyogakaraṇa guruvaktrāt samabhyaset sṛṣṭinyāyena mūrdhādinyāsa kṣetraparigraham kṣetraparigrahe hīne matyaiḥ sādhyaṃ na siddhyati teṣāṃ tu sādhanāthīya ākhyāta ca parigraham anenābhyasite deva ājñāyāmabhiṣecanam abhyāsād hi māsaikena pratyaya pravartate na śṛṇoti na paśyeta tadā kṣetraparigraham ataḥ paraṃ pravakṣyāmi adhikāra punastrayaṃ yena vijñātamātreṇa adhikāra  pravartate ulīnā tritayaṃ deva jyeṣṭha madhyaṃ kanīyasam bālakramaṃ tu kaumāraṃ vṛddhameva kramatrayam teṣāṃ kūṭatrayaṃ śambho parādehād vinirgatam kumārikākhaṇḍaḥprāṇātmādyantanikara ādisthaṃ ca nitambakam vāmastanaṃ tathā kaṇṭhaṃ daṇḍaṃ ca skandhadakṣiṇam punaḥ prāṇaṃ punardaṇḍa kṣīramekatra piṇḍitam evamekādaśā rudrā ekatra viniyojitāḥ rudrakūṭaṃ samākhyātaṃ khaṃ candrārdhavibheditam dīpitaṃ chinnamuṇḍena etad vṛddhakramoddhṛtam tadeva kṣīranirmuktaṃ nāsikayā vibheditam kaumārakramakūṭedamākhyātaṃ tava sundara taccaiva caiva nāsayā rikta vāmakuṇḍalabheditam tṛtīyaṃ ca kaniṣṭhaṃ ca bālakramamudāhṛtam olitritayavinyāsa kuryāt kūṭatrayaṃ guruḥ jyeṣṭhaṃ ca vinyaseccakre bhrūmadhye kopamaṇḍale  madhyamaṃ nābhideśe tu kaniṣṭhaṃ kāmarūpataḥ tribhiraulikrame jātā ye śiṣyā  siddhasantatau teṣāṃ tu trividhaṃ nyāsaṃ ākhyātaṃ satataṃ hitam krameṇānena deveśa ityājñā pārameśvarī tatkṣaṇāt tatra tacchāpa kramaṃ tatra parāṃmukham svatulyāṃ guruḍadyaṃ    tu nirbījaṃ pūjayanti ye saṃsāre vartate bhūya saṃsārānna nivartate na teṣāṃ dīpanaṃ kiñcit śāmbhavakūṭadīpitāḥ tasmāt kūṭasthavinyāsa tridhā mantrakramoddhṛtam viparyāyakrameṇaiva te ca siddhāstribhiḥ punaḥ okāraśca ṣakāraśca mikāraśca triulikāḥ nāyakāstatra vinyasya teṣāṃ piṇḍa svarūpataḥ kumārikākhaṇḍaupadeśena vinyāsaṃ karotyāveśamuttamam  kaniṣṭhaṃ madhyamaṃ jyeṣṭhaṃ madhyamaṃ yonimadhyataḥ aparaṃ yat kaniṣṭhaṃ ca yonimadhye tṛtīyakam evaṃ krameṇa vinyāsaṃ na kuryādapi cānyathā adhikāratraya śambho jñātvā yajanamārabhet ratnapañcakavinyāsa vakṣyāmyāhamataḥ param siddhasaṃketasiddhānāṃ prokta sarvatra pañcakam tṛtīyaṃ daśanaṃ devyāstasyātmānaṃ hṛdi punaḥ nitambaṃ ca śikhā tasyā dakṣastanavibheditam  vāmakuṇḍalasaṃpūrṇa khaśaktiśivabheditam  ratnapañcakamākhyātaṃ proktaṃ sarvajanapriyamoṣamaitracasiddhānāṃ siddhaṃ hyamarikākramam lābhya tena ca gūḍhārthaṃ prakaṭaṃ kulakaulikam karmakṣayānmahādeva vidyeya pañcadhā bhavetsevyā santāne satataṃ tataḥ kamariho bhavet  ratnādyaṃ yat paraṃ piṇḍaṃ tacca ādhāramaṇḍale caturthaṃ kaṇṭhadeśe tu pañcamaṃ turyamaṇḍale kumārikākhaṇḍabekavīrān nyaset pañca na teṣāṃ dīpanaṃ kvacit aiṃkārāntarayogena bhagamadhye layaṃgatāḥ kṣetrasthā vinyaset pañca svabhāvena ca dīpitāḥ cirāyunyāsamātreṇa acchidro bhavate naraḥ divyapīṭhapurakṣobhaṃ vīrasiddhimavāpnuyāt prāpnoti vividhān bhogān vīraiḥ pañcāśadbhiḥ saha yadyāvartayate deva smaraṇāt paṭhanādapi sarvasiddhyālayaṃ tasya yoginastu pravartate divyadṛṣṭi purakṣobhaṃ siddhiḥ pañcāśritena tu daśalakṣakṛte jāpye tīvrājñā saṃpravartate pañcaratnena saṃsiddhi nirvāṇaṃ prāpyate padam matārthaṃ pūrvato jñātvā mantrapada sphuṭam etad vai kaulikaṃ sūtraṃ ṣoḍhānyāsena veṣṭitam  ṣoḍaśānvayamantraughaṃ kramaṃ ṣoḍaśarūpiṇam etad vimalavijñāna  kulamārgavinirgatam kulaṃ ca ṣoḍaśairbhedaiḥ santāna ṣoḍaśai punaḥ ṣoḍaśājñāprasūtistu nyāsamañjūṣakoddhṛtam gopanīyaṃ prayatnena tāntrikānāṃ na darśayet evaṃ prabhāvamākhyātaṃ ṣoḍhānyāsasya sundara kumārikākhaṇḍagurūpadeśato jñeyaṃ saṃhitārthasamuccayam vistaraṃ pūrvamākhyātaṃ lakṣapādādhike mate atra saṃkṣepataḥ prāptaṃ caturviṃśatsahasrake ṣoḍhānyāsasya sūtraṃ tu ākhyātaṃ tava sundara ityādyāvatāre mahāmanthānabhairavayajñe anvaye saptakoṭipramāṇe merumārgavinirgatelakṣapādādhike ādyapīṭhāvatārite vidyāpīṭhamārge vimalaṣaṭkanirṇayekādibhede ājñāpārameśvare svāminīmate śrīcaturviṃśatsahasrasahitāyāṃavvākramabhāṣite ṣoḍhānyāsamañjūṣākramavarṇanekramodayo nāmānandaḥ pañcaviṃśānandaḥśrīnātha uvācakulaṃ ca ṣoḍaśairbhedairmayā jñātaṃ maheśvari viparyāyeṇa apara svābhāvikakula katham ṣaṭcakraṃ ṣoḍaśādhāraṃ trilakṣaṃ vyomapañcakam saṃsphuṭa ca na me jñātaṃ  kulamārgakrameṇa tu idānīṃ kathyatām devi kulabhedaṃ yathā bhavet śrīvakrā uvāca etat praśna mahāśreṣṭhaṃ devadevāvatāritam vicāraṃ tasya vakṣyāmi kulapañcāśikākramam kulamūlakrama śambho śṛṇu vakṣyāmi bhairava adhomukhaṃ tu prathama kandanālasamudbhavam guptaṃ ta kandacakraṃ tu adhomukhavyavasthitam caturdalasamāyukta padmarāgasamaprabham catvārastasya bhedāśca ādhāre cakranāyakāḥ piṇḍaṃ tasya prasādaṃ tu himakundendunirmalam tasya ūdhve dvitīyaṃ ca yogarājamadhomukham vahnikapilasaṃkāśa jvālājvalitavigraham tasya bhedāḥ ṣaḍirjñeyā cakreśa svādhiṣṭhānakam tasya piṇḍa mahārāvaṃ ārakta śuddhavāsanam kumārikākhaṇḍatasya ūdhve tṛtīyaṃ tu cakraṃ nābhihutāśanam mahāratnaṃ mahādīptaṃ tasya bhedāni vai daśa svaraṣaṣṭhasamākrāntaṃ bindusaṃsthaśaśāṅkadhṛk dāḍimīkusumaprakhyaṃ jvalanta bhairavānalam ta piṇḍaṃ maṇipūrasya siddhasya iti niścayam cakranāyakavikhyāta surasiddhanamaskṛtam caturthaṃ tasya ūdhve tu hṛdi cakramadhomukham varṇaṃ taddvairikābhāsaṃ tasya bhedāni dvādaśa cakranāyakavikhyāta tatrānāhatabhairavam khecarīhṛdayaṃ tasya piṇḍa dvādaśavarṇakam dhyāna tasya bhaved raktamīṣadśyāmavimiśritam atova saṃpravakṣyāmi aparaṃ cakranirṇayam himakundendudhavala tasya bhedāni ṣoḍaśa viśuddhaṃ bhairavaṃ tatra kathitaṃ cakranāyakam tasya piṇḍa bhaved vāha tripadena vibheditam haritaṃ tasya varṇaṃ tu nīlajīmutasannibham tasyodhva paramaṃ cakraṃ turyasthānagataṃ pṛthu gokṣīrasadṛśānanda tejorūpaṃ bhagākṛtiḥ tasya bhedadvayaṃ proktaṃ ājñācakreśvaraṃ prabho vāgbhavaṃ tasya tat piṇḍaṃ sindūrāruṇasannibham ṣaṭtyāgāt saptamaṃ ūdhva ākāśe śūnyamaṇḍale turyātīta tu tat proktaṃ tasmāt ṣaṭka vinirgatam sṛṣṭikrameṇa ūdhvāddhi cakraughaṃ tat vibhāvyate kumārikākhaṇḍaḥdvirāra turyacakraṃ tu kaṇṭhe vai ṣoḍaśārakam hṛdayaṃ dvādaśāraṃ tu nābhi daśabhiḥ smṛtaḥ ṣaḍāraṃ yonicakraṃ tu caturāra gudadaṃ smṛtam punaḥ siddhakramaṃ teṣāṃ viśuddhādikrameṇa tu viśuddhaṃ ṣoḍaśairbhedaiḥ dvādaśaistu anāhatam daśabhiśca maṇirbhinnaḥ svādhiṣṭhāna ṣaḍātmakam ādhāre bhedāścatvāra ājñā bhedadvayaṃ viduḥ akārādivisargāntā bhedāni ṣoḍaśa smṛtāḥ kakārādiṭhakārāntā dvādaśāni anāhate ḍakārādiphakārāntā bhedānāṃ daśakaṃ maṇau bakārādilakārānta bhedaṣaṭka krameṇa tu svādhiṣṭhāne  mahādeva ādhāre tu yathā śṛṇu vakārādisakārāntā bhedāścatvārādhāragāḥ ṣaṣṭhaṃ cakraṃ bhrūvormadhye hakṣadvayavinirmitam hakṣadvayavinirmuktāḥ ślokāni dvādaśaḥ smṛtāḥ ṣaṭtyāgāt saptame muktistatrānanda vyavasthitam aparaṃ ṣoḍaśādhārā lakṣatritayameva ca amṛtādivisargāntāḥ kalādhārāṇi ṣoḍaśa teṣāṃ ca yoginīsiddhāḥ svaśarīre vyavasthitāḥ ananta caiva ākāśaṃ induḥ īśvarasaṃjñakam udayaṃ ūrjanāthaṃ ca ṛkṣakarṇaṃ ca ṛṣabham liptāṅgaṃ lūlihaścaiva ekapādaṃ maheśvara tathā vai rāvaṇo nāma ovalī nāma aumuniḥ ambunāthaṃ ahvavāha ādhārā ṣoḍaśa smṛtāḥ kumārikākhaṇḍaete caiva mahāsiddhā ādyante aisamāyutāḥ etaistu vyāpitaṃ piṇḍaṃ teṣā sthānāni ṣoḍaśa prathama ghaṇṭikāyā tu dvitīyaṃ tālumaṇḍale majje mede tathā śukre anyaccaiva tu kuṇḍalīsnāyvasthitvacaromāṇi kesara ca tathāmṛtam māṃsa ca rudhiraṃ caiva vāḍavānala mārutam ākāśaṃ ca tathā deva evamādhāraṣoḍaśa teṣāṃ olitrayaṃ deva sattvarajastamastrayamlakṣatraya samāsena mano buddhirahaṃkṛtiḥ teṣāṃ vai trīṇi siddhāśca kūṭasthā oṣamitraeteṣā tu laya deva pañcavyomastu bhairava ādhāre hṛdaye caiva tathā kule kapāṭake pañcavyomagataṃ lakṣa bhittvā caiva tu khegatiḥ somamaṇḍalamadhyasthaṃ aparaṃ sūryamaṇḍalam vāyumaṇḍalamadhyasthaṃ aparaṃ vyomamaṇḍalam ākāśaṃ pañcadhā proktaṃ adho madhye ca mūrdhani eteṣāṃ vyāpakāḥ pañca bindumārgaprabhedakāḥ śivādyantasamāyuktaṃ teṣāṃ vai siddhapañcakam pṛthivyāpastathā tejo vāyurākāśameva ca ete pañca mahābhūtā nirmitā sṛṣṭikārakāḥ śrīkaṇṭhaḥ śaṅkaronantaḥ sādākhya piṅgalastathā pañcaite sṛṣṭikartāra siddhāḥ pañcakule tathā śrīkaṇṭhaḥ pṛthivī jñeyaḥ śaṅkaroṃ āpa ucyate tejonanta iti proktaḥ sādākhyo vāyurucyate ākāśa piṅgalo jñeyaḥ pañcaite sṛṣṭikārakāḥ kumārikākhaṇḍaetad vai kulamārga tu tavākhyātaṃ rahasyakam guptā kulavadhū yadvat tadvad gopyataraṃ kulam uddhāraṃ pūrvato jñātvā paścād yajanamārabhet etat kulakramācāra bindumaṇḍalabheditam tatra lakṣe mati kṛtvā rudraśakti pravartate adho madhye ca ūdhve vā ātmatulyādhikārakam kuryāccaiva svadehasya cittaṃ damayateṃ tataḥ bahirantarabhāvena tadā cotpadyate sukham tatkulākulamādāya  śarīraṃ ṣaṭkabheditam  navasaṃjña punarbhūyaḥ kulabhedārṇavaṃ bhavet śaṅkha śaktistathā yoga mahāgṛha caturthakam pañcamaṃ ca prabhu proktaṃ pādaṃ tu ṣaṣṭhamucyate atītamāvalī caiva uttarau parikīrtitautasyottamaṃ mahādeva ānanda navamaṃ kulam kulaṃ tu navadhā bhinnaṃ vikhyātaṃ sarvatomukham uḍḍāmara siddhakaula gaṇākhya khecarīmatam candrākhya rauravaṃ deva vīrākhya bhūtaḍāmaram navamaṃ tu mahākaula pratyayaṃ svādhikārakam tenāvatāritā cājñā lakṣapādādhike mate tasmāt tat siddhakaula  tu tadā kaulasya pratyayamavasthā unmanī bhāva etat kaulopadeśakam kulakaula samākhyātaṃ ādyānta tamanāhata kulamekaṃ vijānīyāt  vyomapañcakabheditam  āsanaṃ bhedanaṃ teṣāṃ kulapañcāśikākramam kumārikākhaṇḍaityādyāvatāre mahāmanthānabhairavayajñe anvaye saptakoṭipramāṇe merumārgavinirgatelakṣapādādhike ādyapīṭhāvatārite vidyāpīṭhamārge vimalaṣaṭkanirṇaye kādibhedeājñāpārameśvare svāminīmate śrīcaturviṃśatsahasrasaṃhitāyāṃ avvākramabhāṣitekulapañcāśikādhikāravarṇane kramodayonāmānandaḥ śrinātha uvācaṣaḍviṃśānandaḥkiṃ kula kiṃkramācāra kā pūjā kramamaṇḍale kathayasva maheśāni prasādād vada me prabho śrīvakrā uvācakramādyaṃ mūlasūtra tu vṛttādhyuṣṭapramāṇataḥ tasyārabhya kramāt sṛṣṭi ityā  khecaram yā sā śaktirbhagākhyā trividhagatiyutā tryakṣarā triprakārātasyā śrī oḍḍiyāṇa parakalasahita madhyasthaṃ sudīptam tacchrījālandharākhyaṃ prakaṭitanilaya dakṣiṇe caiva koṇevāme śrīpūrṇapīṭha paśujanabhayakṛt kāmarūpaṃ tadatasyodhve tisrapīṭha paramakalayutaṃ candrapīṭhaṃ lalāṭetrikoṇānte samastaṃ paramaśivakalākṣobhita divyamatanmadhye vakraliṅga paramasukhakara bindurūpaṃ tribhinnanityānandasvarūpa taduparimathanāt  ṣaṭprakārādhikāram apūrvāmnāyakramaugha tadupari aparaṃ vṛddhakaumārabālamevaṃ vyāptaṃ samastaṃ sthitilayajananī rudraśaktistribhedaiḥ kumārikākhaṇḍaciñcājñā kādibhedairakulakulamayānandadā bodharūpā guvajñā ṣaṭkārā paśubhayaharaṇī candrabimbasya madhye nityaklinnā suraktābhayamuditaparānandaśakti prasiddhākurvantī śāmbhavauṣa kṣubhitavaratanuḥ śrīkujā divyaliṅgam mayāvatārita  tubhyamādyasūtramadhomukhamyā sā śakti parākhyātā sā ca devī bhagākṛtiḥ tasyānte sā parā devī pīṭhānāṃ pīṭhadevatā yā sā śaktirbhagākhyātā gatistasyāstridhā punaḥ ādikādithakārādibrahmaviṣṇumaheśvarāḥ jyeṣṭhā vāmā ca raudrī ca dvādaśaślokabheditāḥ parā sā rudraśaktistu tribhiḥ sthānaivyavasthitā lalāṭe hṛdaye yonau kṣarate triṣu kāriṣu śukraṃ ca śoṇitaṃ kṛcchra nāḍītritayasandhiṣu iḍā ca piṅgalā caiva suṣumnā madhyamā trayaḥ evamānandayogena triśakti svādhikārikā tasyāyāta kramaṃ deva bālakaumāravṛddhakam pīṭhapañcakasaṃyukta kramameka trayoliṣu ānandānandabinduśca akṣara  paramā kalā pīṭhānyete kramāt pañca antaraṅge pratiṣṭhitāḥ kumārikākhaṇḍabahiraṅge ca te kūṭā ojāpūkā ca tisrakam samastaṃ ca kula kaulaṃ śivaśaktikalāvṛtam ānandāvṛtavṛndastu ānande tu pravartate udbhavānandacittasya samatvaṃ ca pravartate tanmadhye sūkṣmaliṅga tu divyaliṅgamadhomukham paramākāśamadhyastha candramaṇḍalamadhyataḥ tadā tat suṣira yāti lakṣitenāntarātmanā paśyate tu samādhistho bindurūpaṃ nabhastalam cidānandasamutpatti āveśa saṃpravartate tadrūpaṃ ca svarūpaṃ ca ityāśrāvaṇapratyayam mathite cittacaitanye mathitaṃ karmasaṃśrayam  mathanādapi cakrasya yogāveśa muhurmuhuḥ ārakta tatkule cakraṃ tatrasthaṃ bindumaṇḍalam bheditaṃ drāvita yasmāt mathitaṃ smaraṇena tu ṣaṭprakārairvibhinna tu bhedaiścaivāṣṭaviṃśatiḥ catuṣkaṃ pañcaka ṣaṭka catuṣkaṃ pañcaka catuḥ ṣaṭprakārakrama hyetat yo vetti sa ca kaulikaḥ  ādau pīṭhacatuṣkaṃ tu catvāraḥ pīṭhadevatā  siddhapañcakamanya tu jñānaṣaṭkasamanvitam mahantārīpañcaka ca olitrayakulakramam aṣṭāviṃśatibhirbhedaiḥ prakārāṇi ṣaḍi smṛtāḥkumārikākhaṇḍaetairbhinna kulātmāna tadā ānandasantatiḥ kalisyānte ca kāmākhye samīpasthaṃ ca pañcakam avasthā ca kule kaule tisrākhye jāyate hi ca sa cāṣṭāviṃśamo bhedo bhaviṣye ca bhaviṣyati evaṃ te pañcabhiḥ pīṭhā pūrvasūtre visarpitā tathā ca devatādīni sṛṣṭinyāye ataḥ śṛṇu gajajihvā agnijihvā taḍijjihvā tṛtīyakā śukrajihvā ca amarā rasajihvā ca pañcamī teṣāṃ siddhī kramāt pañca idānī pravadāmyaham candrārkānalabimbastha bindau ca gaṇapañcakam āveśa ghūrṇirānandaḥ ūṣmā kroṣaṇaśoṣaṇam etad vai jñānaṣaṭkaṃ tu prakṛtisthaṃ prameyataḥ māyā ca śāmbhavī śakti icchā jñānī kriyā tathā etaccatuṣkamākhyāta pañcakaṃ mahantārikā śabdā spaśī rasā devī rūpavyāpī ca gandhinī ete vai tvadahaṃkāryā pañcaka parikīrtitam vimalāntaramātmāna evaṃ olitrika smṛtam eva te kramabhedāni kathitānyaṣṭaviṃśatiḥ etairbhinnaṃ mahāliṅgaṃ divyamaṇḍalasaṃjñakam teṣāṃ vidyānvaya yacca parā sā paramā kalā kumārikākhaṇḍanityoditā susūkṣmā ca nāsāgre saṃvyavasthitā ūrṇatantunibhākārā gokṣīrahimaśītalā tayāsau jīvate jīvo divyaliṅgaṃ maheśvara tasya siddhānvayaṃ sarvaṃ bhedāñcaivāṣṭaviṃśatiḥ tayā prāśitamātrā yā antarbhavaḥ pravartate trināḍisaṃgama sthūlaṃ ekatra yatra tiṣṭhati tena ta tripuraṃ pīṭhaṃ tribhiḥ srotapravāhakam tisrākhya ca lalāṭastha brahmagranthiradhomukhīlalāṭasuṣira cakraṃ pratyaya jñānaraśmayaḥ evaṃ vyāptaṃ krama meroryoginī ca adhomukhī sā śakti paramā tatra sthitā viśrāmakāriṇī dakṣiṇottarayoḥ pārrave jananī calate pure bhagamadhyamaśṛṅgasya tasyāgre tu layaṃ punaḥ evaṃ sā rudraśaktistu tribhirbhedaiḥ pratiṣṭhitā ādisthāne sthitā tatra devadevī kulecchayā dadate jñānasadbhāvaṃ kuṭilāṅgī svatantrataḥ tadānandaḥ pravarteta  mokṣamārgamahotsava ājñā gurumukhād labdhvā rudraśaktiḥ pravartate vaktrād vaktragatā ājñā bandhubhūtā kulakrame vācāsiddhi kule kaule bhavanāt saṃpravartate kumārikākhaṇḍakarmaṇā manasā vācā triśuddhirbhaktivatsale tasyājñā vartate śiṣye bhāvahīno na siddhyati paśupāśabhaya  śiṣye anyathā ca bhaved dhruvam rudraśaktirmahādevī amoghā ca jagatsutā divyājñāyā svarūpā sā siddharūpā tvanekadhā nityaklinnāprabhāvena atiraktasvarūpataḥ udayaṃ labhate śiṣya paramānandalakṣaṇam pratirūpā ca yā śaktiḥ prasiddhā cchāyajā parā kurvantī nitya karmāṇi manecchayā  yathā sudhīḥ mocayecchakticakrastho  divyaliṅganurdharaḥ candrādityajale cchāyā agnisomārkadarpaṇe tathā sā tārakānte ca parā devī susūkṣmagā paśudharā yathā paśyet kuṭilā ca adhomukhīmsā ca devī hyahaṃ mūrtiḥ kubjikā kulakaulinī tasyāḥ sūtrakramaṃ coktaṃ kramaogha vinirgatam prajñārthaṃ saṃgataṃ paśyenmūlasūtropadeśakam  ityāgamaviśuddhasya prajñāsūtramaya hara malasyaivopaghātārthaṃ nirṇītāmiha saṃhitām anena sūcitaṃ sūtra mūlasūtraṃ tu mūlataḥ prajñāsūtravinirmukto yonyathā avadhārayet na tasya sūtraṃ na mūlaṃ tu na jñānaṃ jñeyarūpataḥ na kulaṃ ca kramaṃ naiva nācārya naiva putrakam tasmāt sarvaprayatnena mūlasūtraṃ samāyet śrīnātha uvācakramaugha mūlasūtraṃ tu prajñāsūtreṇa bodhitam tvanmukhācca mayā jñātaṃ siddhohaṃ nātra saṃśayaḥ divyānandaprakāśoyaṃ kumārikākhaṇḍakālī tvaṃ caiva ujjainyā ardhapīṭheśvareśvarīṃ tvaṃ ca pīṭhopapīṭheṣu tvamādyā kramamaṇḍale pañcapraṇavamadhyasthe pūrṇānte kulamātare mātṛcakrasthite devi ṣaḍyoginiparāvṛte tvaṃ ca sā vāyuvege manāntasthe parāparavisarpite śūnye śūnyāntarāvasthe māruti siddhasevite nirālambe gate devi ākāśe duratikrame jñānavijñānagambhīre jñeyarūpe ca kevale sthitilayakarīdevi janani tattvamaṇḍale tattvānā kṣobhaṇī śakti ajñānatamabhedanī mātarī sarvadevānāṃ mama prāṇapriye ume viśveśvarī jagaddhātrī saṃpradāyapradāyinīnamaste paranirvāṇe jagadyonimahāmbike smara tvaṃ samayaṃ pūrvaṃ snehena manavigraham tuṣṭā bhava paresmākaṃ mātā  tvaṃ tridaśairapi iti māyāstava  proktaṃ yogīvāṇīkramāgatam tasyāvatāraṃ kurute vakrikā pīṭhadevatā kumārikākhaṇḍasukhamārogyasaṃpattimavasthā labhate naraḥ sarvapāpavinirmukto bhavate tatkṣaṇādapi na tasya punarāvṛttimīyāstavamudīraṇāt ihaiva prāpnuyād bhogān lābha pūjāyaśa śriyaḥ avasthā kramayuktasya pāramparyeṇa tasya ca samayācārayuktasya tīvrājñā saṃpravartate ityādyāvatāre mahāmanthānabhairavayajñe anvaye saptakoṭipramāṇe merumārgavinirgatelakṣapādādhike ādyapīṭhāvatārite vidyāpīṭhamārge vimalaṣaṭkanirṇayekādibhede ājñāpārameśvare svāminīmate śrīcaturviṃśatsahasrasaṃhitāyāṃ avvākramabhāṣite mūlasūtrādhikāravarṇanemāyāstavādhikāro nāmānandaḥ saptaviṃśānandaḥśrīnātha uvācadevi siddhe jagatsvāmi ādināthe kulodbhave brūhi jñānopadeśaṃ tu yat sāraṃ paścimānvaye prakaṭaṃ kuru kaulīśe pūjāāgamamaṇḍalam śrīvakrā uvācasāraṃ śaivasya jagato bhuvanākṛtimaṇḍalam bāhyasthaṃ ca svadehasthaṃ antaraṅgaṃ cidātmakam tadahaṃ saṃpravakṣyāmi gurumaṇḍalakaṃ yathā yosau anādiravyakta  śivaḥ paramakāraṇaḥ mantramūrtirabhūnnātha lokānugrahahetunā avatīrṇastu bhūloke anugrahakaraḥ paraḥ pūjyosau maṇḍale deva navātmānandabhairavaḥ pañcamūrtidharo nātha ṣoḍaśāvayavānvitaḥ navadhāmūrtimāśritya avatīrṇaḥ kalau yuge pañcāśadrudramūrtisthoṃ yathā pūjyastathā śṛṇu tasyoddhāra mahādeva ślokaiḥ pañcabhiḥ sūcitam  akāre catvare madhye pañcamaṃ ca tathā punaḥ lakayakṣatana ramaḍakha ceti viparyayet ḍa ḍha ṭha ṭa daparyantaṃ sṛṣṭyā merorvinirgatam maṇḍalaṃ taṃ smṛtaṃ deva dvitīyaṃ cādhikārayoḥ kumārikākhaṇḍaindra āpastathā tejo vāyurākāśameva ca jñānogya  kuṇḍalī koṭi tṛtīyā varavarṇini hṛdaya samaya caiva sarvajñaṃ ca kadambakam khagīśaṃ gurunāthaṃ ca ratnabījaṃ caturthakam kadamba vimalaugha ca samayaṃ bhairavāvalī pādukānte manu smṛtvā pūjayed gurumaṇḍalam vidyāpīṭhāgrato deva gurumaṇḍalapūjanam pūrvakrama yathā coktaṃ pañcāsanasamanvitam prasādatrayasabhinnaṃ arcayet guru pañcadhā īśakoṇāt samārabhya yāvanmadhyaṃ tu pañcamam maṇḍalaṃ cādhikāra ca siddhāḥ samaya yoginī pañcadhā pañcabhirbhinna pañcadhākaulinīyutam vāgbhavaṃ māyayā sārdhaṃ lakṣmīprasādabheditam navātmānandasaṃyuktaṃ pañcabhirgurumaṇḍalam pādukāntaṃ mahādeva pūjayet satataṃ varam antaraṅgagatāḥ pūjyā maṇḍalāni tathātmani ādhāre prathamaṃ proktaṃ dvitīyaṃ yonimaṇḍale tṛtīyaṃ nābhicakre tu caturtha ca anāhate pañcamaṃ kaṇṭhadeśe tu ādināthaṃ tu mūrdhani śrīkaṇṭhādi piṅgalānta pañcadhā pañca kalpitam prabhāte caiva madhyāhne sandhyākāle tu sundara vidyāpīṭhāgrataḥ kuryāt guroragre tu pañcadhā ārādhanaṃ tu kartavyaṃ saṃpūrṇa siddhidaṃ bhavet na rikta maṇḍalaṃ kuryāt gurora kadācana kumārikākhaṇḍayathāvittānusāreṇa kṛtvā saṃpūrṇapūjanam ārātrī candanaṃ dīpa vīradravyasamanvitam nivedana prakartavyaṃ sāṣṭāṅga ca namaskaret tridhā ca pañcadhā caiva sāṣṭāṅga daṇḍavat sudhīḥ pradakṣiṇaśataṃ kṛtvā pūjayed gurupādukām etadācārasamaya pālayet satataṃ budhaḥ pālanād bhavate siddhiḥ anyathā narakaṃ vrajet oliparveṣu sarveṣu nityanaimittikeṣu ca maṇḍalakramapūjāyāṃ sarva saṃpūrṇatāṃ vrajet ataḥ paraṃ pravakṣyāmi śṛṇu bhairava tattvataḥ śrīkramaṃ tu tataḥ pūjya yathoktaṃ śrīkulāgame tasyāvatāraṃ saṃkṣepāt paryaṅke satataṃ kuru mṛgājine tu saṃkalpya āsane vāgbhavaṃ śubham śrīkhaṇḍacandanaṃ śuddha kaṃkumaṃ cālimiśritam abhimantrya ca vidyāyāḥ kramaṃ likhya tridhāvidham ādyakramasya vṛddhasya yogapīṭhaṃ tridhoditam tadbāhye likhya ṣaṭkoṇa aiṃkāreṇa tu veṣṭayet aṣṭāraṃ padmaka bāhye mekhalātritayāvṛtam catuṣkoṇa tu tadbāhye likhya ca susūtritam ṣaṭkoṇacakrasaṃyukta  kaumārasya kramaṃ likhet aṣṭārapadmasaṃyukta  krama bālakramasya ca evaṃ te kramabhedoya maṇḍalasya prakāśitam kumārikākhaṇḍanyāsabhedaṃ yathā  deva vṛddhakaumārabālake prathama śabdarāśistu dvitīyā mālinī tathā vidyātritayamevaṃ tu tadaṅgāni caturthakam aghoryaṣṭakamevaṃ tu tathā siddhāṅgapañcakam ṣoḍhānyāsamidaṃ kṛtvā paścād yajanamārabhet vṛddhakramasya jyeṣṭhasya nyāsāvaraṇamuttamam atha madhyamasiddhasya kaumārasya yathākramam prathamaṃ tadgraha kṣetraṃ dvitīyaṃ bījapañcakam dvādaśāṅgaṃ tṛtīyaṃ ca siddhāṅgaṃ ca caturthakam pañcamaṃ tu ṣaḍaṅgaṃ syāt pīṭhanyāsaṃ tu ṣaṣṭhakam khecara saptamaṃ nāma kṛtvā yajanamārabhet atha tṛtīyakaṃ vakṣye kramasyāvaraṇa punaḥ prathamā samayā vidyā siddhāṅgaṃ ca dvitīyakam tṛtīyaṃ tu ṣaḍaṅgaṃ syāt ślokāni tu caturthakam pañcamaṃ cādhikāra syāt ṣaṣṭhaṃ kṣetraparigraham saptamaṃ ratnavinyāsaṃ vidyānyāsaṃ tathāṣṭamam evaṃ nyāsakramaṃ nyasya paścād bālakramaṃ yajet kramāṇāṃ maṇḍalaṃ jñātvā ekacakre tu paścime siddhāṅgaṃ ca ṣaḍaṅgaṃ ca dvāvetau tu viśodhayet kumārikākhaṇḍaviśvāmitrakapālaṃ tu susiddhaṃ yogināṃ śubham pīṭhāgre dravyasaṃpūrṇa vratīnāṃ nṛkapālakam koṅkaṇāstreṇa saṃśodhya kavacenāvaguṇṭhayet mūrti praviśya hṛdaye netre tridhā japtvā sānnidhyaṃ kramamaṇḍale aparaṃ dvitīya pātra candanāmṛtapūritam pañcakādyena saṃsthāpya punastenābhimantritam atha tṛtīyakaṃ pātraṃ sthāpita ratnapañcake tena yaṣṭvā punastatra dakṣiṇottaramadhyataḥ evaṃ pātratrayaṃ pūrvaṃ kṛtvā pūjā samārabhet candanena tu vinyāsaṃ vidyāyā ātmasantatau bhakārādicakārāntaṃ sthāne sthāne pṛthak pṛthak ātmānaṃ dhūpitaṃ kuryād vinyāsaṃ mūlavidyayā aṅganyāsa samārabhya sva  olyā tu yathākramam kumārikākhaṇḍatilatailāṣṭadīpāni pañcādyena pradīpayet digvidikṣu ca pīṭhasya adhivāsamanantaram candanaṃ dhūpasaugandhakuṃkumākṣatasaṃyutam mūlamantrasya siddhasya kuryād dāna ca santatau mudrātritayaṃ kṛtvādau tataḥ pūjāṃ samārabhet pūrvakrameṇa kartavyaṃ dehasthaṃ kramapūjanam paścād bāhye tu pīṭhasthaṃ sabāhyābhyantaraṃ kramam candanākṣatasaṃmiśrairādau kuryāt kramārcanam śvetapuṣpaiḥ sugandhaiśca taistu pūjyaṃ kulakramam abhāvād raktapuṣpaistu tathā pītaiḥ sugandhibhiḥ sumanācampakaiḥ padyaistathā nīlotpalaiḥ śubhaiḥ deśācāreṇa labdhaistu taistu pūjyaṃ kulakramam nirgandhaiśca sakaṇṭakairbhagnai saṃkucitairdumaiḥ kramapūjā na kartavyā manasāpi sureśvara dhūpārcanaṃ punaścaiva pṛthak ājñākramaṃ punaḥ alipūjā tataḥ kāryā vaiṣṇavīpadamātrataḥ pratyaya vyākulaṃ tatra mahārāva pravartate sānnidhyamatulaṃ cograṃ paśūnāṃ ca bhayāvaham mūlamantreṇa vidyāyā vāmapāṇyakṣasūtrakam sphāṭikaṃ putrajīvaṃ vā mātrā aṣṭottaraṃ śataṃ dvimātrāṃ vā trimātrā vā icchayā vā manīṣiṇām sthūla vā sūkṣmamaṇi vā na meru laṅghayet kvacit kumārikākhaṇḍaaṃguṣṭa varjayitvā tu yathā prāpta catuṣṭayam madhyamau dvau tathā varjayau vāmāvartaparibhramāt etat pāṇikṛtaṃ japyaṃ akṣasūtreṇa vā kṛtam cūlāgramamalaṃ śuddhaṃ uparisthamakṣamālayā taṃ ca meruṃ vijānīyāllaṅghanānnarakaṃ vrajet vāmāvartakrameṇaiva sadyojātaṃ vidhīyate tadārūhya paraṃ dhyānaṃ mantra vāpi ca muktidam svaolyāmātmapīṭhasya ātmānamaṇḍalepi vā mantratriṣkoṇamadhye tu athavā pūrṇavidyāyām dvicatvāriṃśatsaṃjñāyā japyaṃ dhyānaṃ trikoṇake kuryāt tanmānasaṃ japyaṃ ātmakūṭamathāpi vā mudritaṃ yonimudrāyāmamānāmāṅkita śivam ādau tanmūlavidyāyā agnikuṇḍasya madhyataḥ dhyānamāraktakṛṣṇaṃ tu kuryāt karmānurūpataḥ ūdhvamadhyamadhaḥ kuryāt saṃskāraṃ ca tathā puna mama yonigataṃ dhyāyenna bāhye viniyojayet ityādyāvatāre mahāmanthānabhairavayajñe anvaye saptakoṭipramāṇe merumārgavinirgatelakṣapādādhike ādyapīṭhāvatārite vidyāpīṭhamārge vimalaṣaṭkanirṇaye yathākramam adhunā śrotumicchāmi kramamekaṃ tridhā kathaṃ śrīvakrā uvācaaṣṭāviṃśānandaḥśṛṇu nātha pravakṣyāmi kramamekaṃ tridhā yathā olitritayabhedena bālakaumāravṛddha vṛddhakramaṃ tu prathamaṃ jyeṣṭha  olikramāgatam mantriṇātu yathā deva āyātaṃ jñānanirṇayam pīṭhānāmādyavarṇāśca ojāpūkācatuṣṭayam te yugāni catvāraste pīṭhāni aihikībhuvi te ca pañcamahābhūtāścatuvyāpakasaṃyutāḥ oṃ puruṣaṃ viduḥ pūkāraṃ vāmadevaṃ tu kākāra sadyarūpakam antaraṅge sthitā devyo bhrūmadhye hṛdi nābhigāḥ yonimadhye samākhyātāsteṣu devyācatuṣṭayam kakārādiṣu catvāraḥ strīnapuṃsakabheditāḥ pīṭheśvarya samākhyātā pīṭhadhyānasamāyutāḥ teṣu siddhāñca catvāraḥ pūjyā pīṭhacatuṣṭaye haraśabdaścatunyāsa haraśabdaścatuṣṭayam ādyadīrgheścaturbhinna ājñāyā śikharāṅkitam pīṭhabījāśca catvāraḥ dhyānaṃ teṣāṃ ca pūrvavat ataḥ paraṃ pravakṣyāmi vyomapañcakanirṇayam vyoma tu pañcadhā sthāpya śaktyādhastejabṛṃhitam dīrghapañcakasaṃbhinnaṃ bindunādairalaṃkṛtam vyomapañcakametaddhi dhyānaṃ teṣāmaghoravat ājñāsaṃkrāmaka deva tasya mantrakramaṃ bhavet ye coktā  vyāpakā pañca tejorūpā mahābalāḥ teṣāṃ sthānāni vai pañca asmin śāstre pracakṣmahe śrotre nāsāpuṭe vaktre jñātavyaṃ vyomapañcakam pṛthivī cāpatattvaṃ tu tejo vāyuḥ khasaṃjñakam śaktitattvaṃ tathā ṣaṣṭhaṃ teṣāṃ caivādho raviḥ kumārikākhaṇḍatathā tad vāyutattvaṃ ca nādākṣaravibheditam bindusthaṃ nādaśaktisthaṃ ājñākūṭaṃ maheśvara gude yonau tathā nābhau hṛdi kaṇṭhe bhruvontare eteṣāṃ kathitaṃ ṣaṭkaṃ saṃketena ca ṣaḍvidham śvetā ca prathamā vartirdvitīyā pītarūpinī tṛtīyā nīlavaṇī ca caturthī haritā bhavet pañcamā gairikābhā ca śveta pītaṃ ca āraktaṃ harita gaṇapañcakam dhyāna vai pañcadhā teṣāṃ trikamadhye  yathā bhavet trikaṇṭakaṃ samākhyātaṃ vidyātritayamabhyaset ādhāre hṛdaye tūrye teṣāṃ sthānatraya bhavet ārakta upadeśavaśenaiva pīṭhadevyāḥ samarcayet vyomapañcakamevaṃ tu mantrayuktaṃ samabhyaset teṣāṃ vai devatā   pañca pūjākāle pracakṣma vyoma tu pañcadhā kuryāt teṣāṃ pañcādhikārakam kāsirephasiye madhyamolyā kramārcanam teṣāṃ nāmāni varṇāśca tattvayuktā manīṣiṇām śaktyādhiṣṭhitacatvāra haramāyāsanasthitāḥ ā  īū aisvarairbhinnā nādabindukalāṅkitā evaṃ pīṭhāni catvāri  pīṭhadevyāścatuṣṭayam vṛddhasya mantrakrama samuddhṛtam vidhānaṃ ca mahādeva yathā kaumāravṛddhakam tathā saṃketabhāṣā ca nāmasaṃketasūcanam kumārikākhaṇḍaojāpūkāñca catvāra  kāpūjāocatuṣṭayam mā vi sajja samu ceti saṃketakamida punaḥ ete guptatarā pīṭhā guptāśca pīṭhadevatāḥ pīṭhasiddhāśca catvāraḥ saṃketa susūkṣmakam kulapañcakamanya tu tasya saṃketa pañcadhā aku saku sakuśceti aṃku caiva aku punaḥ kulapañcakametad hi ambhāṣaṭkamataḥ param aṃbhā ca ṣaḍvidhāṃ kuryāt catuḥsvaravibheditām  tasyāgre cādhikārāṇi vṛddhadevyāḥ ṣaḍirbhavet āpa iti ma aṃkāra ma avvā krama tathā makha a ced  bhakārāvvā ambhāṣaṭkamitietad vai kaulabhāṣāyāṃ mantrakramamudāhṛtam yogapañcakameva tu tasya saṃketa pañcadhā asā sasa vayogeti saku īsasaka iti guptaṃ prakaṭasaṃyogāt pūrvakramasamāyutam siddhatrikaṃ trikasyaiva teṣu saṃketa tridhā si siddha iti siddhāstu sarve mantrakramoditāḥ kṛtvā pūrvakramācāra prakārāṇi samabhyaset upadeśavaśenaiva kaumārakramamuddhṛtam adhunā madhyamolyāyā krameda caiva
