vyavasthitāḥ kujīśasya tanuścaiva parāśāntād vinirgataḥ jagadyonīti  vikhyātā sṛṣṭirūpā mahāmbikā sā yoni sarvabhūtānā varṇarūpā vyavasthitā ye varṇadevatāḥ sarve vīrāśca bhairavāstathā rudrā siddhāśca tepyevaṃ varṇarūpā vinirgatāḥ kālāgnyādiśivānte ca sā yoniḥ saṃvyavasthitā evaṃ divyaṃ mahādivyaṃ divyādivyairna gocaram tadevamanvaya tattva gocarācāramelakam kathitaṃ te mahāśaṃbho rahasyamatidurlabham divyeda vimalaṃ jñāna uddhṛtaṃ saptakoṭitaḥ ye vindanti narā deva te muktā nātra saṃśaya kumārikākhaṇḍavinā vimalabhedena dīkṣā śikṣā ca yo dadet na dīkṣā naiva śikṣā ca ahutīnā nirarthakā mātṛkā viditā hyeṣā siddhajñānena saṃyutā na deyā kasyacid deva viśeṣād bhaktivarjite kramapūjārate śānte rāgadveṣavivarjite teṣā deyamidaṃ deva nānyeṣā tu kadācana pāpiṣṭhā nindakā krūrā rāgadveṣasamanvitāḥ na te yogyā kule kaule vicaranti narādhamā na te yānti paraṃ sthānaṃ niṣiddhāste mayā purā śvānena tu yathā śvāno dṛṣṭoṃ buddha  pravartate  tathā ca niṣphalā ceṣṭā ajñānatamasāvṛtā saṃsārārṇavagambhīre ye magnā bhuvi mānavāḥ dīkṣitāpi na mucyanti krodhalobhaparāyaṇāḥ viṣṭhāmadhye kṛmiryadvadamedhyamupajīvati evaṃ te kulavibhraṣṭā patanti narakārṇave bhajante mepratiṣṭhā ye ahaṃkāravaśānugāḥ na teṣāmaihikā siddhi  paratra ca na vidyate pāramparyakramārūḍhā dīkṣitāḥ siddhaśāsane abhiṣiktāstathā śaṃbho vinayena vivarjitāḥ nayahīnā na siddhyanti ihaloke paratra ca vinayāt prāpyate sarvaṃ tasmād vinayamācaret evaṃ vinayahīnā ye pāpiṣṭhā bhuvi garvitāḥ na te yogyā kule kaule bhavanti jñānavarjitāḥ kumārikākhaṇḍavinayāmṛtatṛptānāṃ śāntācāraparāyaṇām mukhanāmapi yā siddhirna sāhaṃkṛtapaṇḍitām idaṃ jñānodaya nāma śaivasāra tu kaulikam kathitaṃ devadeveśa satyena tu mayā tava tat khyāta jñānakhaṇḍa nihatakaliripudhvasitaḥ pāparāśiyonau saṃgṛhya vegāt kramati ahaniśa tattva sandhyākṣareṇa taṃ nāda citsvarūpaṃ praṇamata satataṃ vandanīya surāṇāṃdātāra bhuktimukti namata guruvaraṃ śrīmahānādinātham mokṣārtha jñānahetoḥ prakaṭitanilaye siddhaśabda amoghavighnavyāghātadakṣa sthitamamalamajaṃ maṅgalānāṃ nidhānam jñānabhāvaiḥ prapannaṃ bahuvividhaphalaṃ divyamānandabhūtaṃśrīmadoḍīśanāthaṃ vyapagatakaluṣaṃ pādapadmaṃ namāmi yasyānanta na dūraṃ na ca divasaniśā kālavelā na caivajāgratsupte suṣupte gaganamatirataṃ mokṣakāmānuraktam matyānā tāraṇārthaṃ bhavabhayaharaṇaṃ tīvramājñādhara calīlābhāvai prapannaṃ namata guruvaraṃ śrīmahātūṣṇinātham ājñāsiddhairamādyaiḥ kalikaluṣaharai  tarpate divyapānaiḥdṛṣṭaṃ cādṛṣṭarūpaṃ patati  śuddhakāyo bhavet saḥ paścāt krīḍāsvarūpaḥ susamavidhiparo jāyate divyayogīsarveṣāṃ vandanīyo jayati sa bhagavān pātu māṃ caryanātha kumārikākhaṇḍayenedaṃ siddhamārgaṃ prakaṭita  bhuvane kīrti kollāpure vābilvasphoṭaṃ vidhāya punarapi ca gataḥ saṃsthitaścandrapuryām  tribhuvanaviditāṃ yasya kīrtirbabhūvaciñcāmālokayitvātīvrājñāyā varo yo kalikaluṣaharo naumyahaṃ vṛkṣanātham ityādyāvatāre mahāmanthānabhairavayajñe anvaye saptakoṭipramāṇe merumārgavinirgatelakṣapādādhike ādyapīṭhāvatārite vidyāpīṭhamārge vimalaṣaṭkanirṇaye kādibhedeājñāpārameśvare svāminīmateśrīcaturviṃśatsahasrasaṃhitāyāṃ avvākramabhāṣite śrīkramasṛṣṭyadhikāro nāmānandaḥ pañcacatvāriṃśānandaḥśrivakrā uvācaataḥ paraṃ pravakṣyāmi trikabhedavinirṇayam parāparamanuttamam paraṃ caiva tu bījasthaṃ nirbījaṃ paramaṃ padam advayaṃ paramaṃ jñānaṃ mantrātītamagocaram  evaṃ trividhabheda syāt satam kṛtā yena mahācaryā pratyayaṃ prakaṭīkṛtam pratyayājjāyate muktirmukterbandho na vidyate evaṃ sṛṣṭikramaṃ proktaṃ trikabhedasya nirṇayam  divyāmnāyakramājjāta paścime parameśvara prathamāvatārasaṃketa ukta kulakramodayam yaścāvadhārayet śrīmānśrīkujākhyāmahāmatam sa mukta sa kulācāryaḥ paramānandananditaḥ evaṃ śaktisvarūpoyaṃ avyaktaṃ ca bravīmyaham avyaktājjāyate siṃha siṃhāt saṃvartavibhramaḥ vibhramājjāyate śaktiḥ śakte  kiñjalkabhairavam bhairavādakulaṃ jātaṃ akulād vikula tathā kumārikākhaṇḍavikulāt puṃkula caiva puṃkulāt khakulaṃ punaḥ khakulāt pañcadhā hyātmā akulāt kulasantatiḥ bhaviṣyanti na saṃdeha kalisyānte mahātapa siddhajñānamidaṃ divyaṃ kulāmnāyamudāhṛtam ādyāvatāra yo vetti sonvayī kulaśāsane idaṃ sṛṣṭikramaṃ jñānaṃ siddhasantatinirṇayam na kasyacinmayākhyātaṃ tvadṛte parameśvara rakṣitavyaṃ prayatna aprakāśya tu kārayet ityādyāvatārasūtraṃ tu pāramparyavinirṇayam yo jānāti varāroha tasya ājñā catuṣṭaye prathamaṃ tu kulāmnāya kramāmnāya dvitīyakam dvīpāmnāyaṃ tṛtīyaṃ tu pīṭhāmnāyaṃ caturthakam siddhāmnāyaṃ pañcamaṃ ca devyāmnāyaṃ tu ṣaṣṭhakam etadāmnāyaṣaṭkaṃ ca anvaye parikīrtitam prathamaṃ divyapuṣpa tu yugmasaṃjñamataḥ param ekamevamida guhyaṃ puṣpasaṃketapañcakam puṣpapañcakametaddhi kule ca prakaṭīkṛtam kaumāramūvato divyaṃ śirastha yo hi dhārayet kaulika sa ca vijñeya  ācāryamatabodhakaḥ khecaratvamavāpnoti siddhistasya karasthitā kumārikākhaṇḍakavimukha puṣpasyeda paścime tu vinirṇayam pāramparyakramāyāta divyametat kulodayam ādyanta smarate yo hi kaumāre tu pare pade kulasiddhirbhavet tasya khegatiśca na saṃśayaḥ khegati khecarī caiva khegatavīravandita labhate nātra saṃdeho ānanda svādhikārakam khecara khecarīsiddhiḥ gamanāt khecarasya tu khecarīsiddhisiddhasya siddhiścaiva tu khecarī etat te khecaraṃ mārgaṃ divyājñā nātra saṃśayaḥ kulāmnāyamidaṃ hyeṣā kaulabhāṣā udāhṛtam athātaḥ kramabhedaṃ tu kulāmnāye vyavasthitam ojāpūkācatuṣka tu devīcatuṣkabhūṣitam khasamatāsamopeta sārdhaṃ vidyācatuṣṭayam mioṣaceti catvāraḥ sarvavidyāyutāḥ pṛthak gasapamanāntare ratnaṃ saṃjñā ratnaṃ ca pañcakam ratnottha pañcakopetaṃ vinivivisasaṃjñakam yoginībhirḍakārādyaiḥ ṣaṭkaṃ saptamasaṃyutam aparakartarī vidyā tathā  saptasamasteṣu  asaṃyovisamadhye tu vidyāyuktaṃ ca pañcakam triyugma ca trikūṭaṃ ca asikta trikasaṃjñakam kumārikākhaṇḍakramabhāṣā iyaṃ deva bhedāni saptaviṃśati yogamārgeṇa siddhyanti dhyāyamānāścaturyuge evaṃ kramamida deva yugmanāthena dīpitam bhāṣā caikākṣarā vidyā purā vai yā samākhyātā kakhasvagurustattvamālā tu tathā pañcāśikākramam samayā mālinī vidyā tathā tu bhairavāṣṭakam tataḥ kulāṣṭakaṃ divyaṃ aṣṭāṣṭakasamanvitam evaṃ pūjākrama prokta kaumāraṃ tu yuge yuge āmnāye paścimāmnāye divyametat kulakramam dakṣiṇataḥ śatātīte śatābdaśatakena tu tato dakṣāntakeśeṣa siddhināthasya bhāṣitam na likhet pustake deva kramaughamidamuttamam  karṇākarṇagata jñeya matārtha vimala kramam pūjanāt prāpyate mokṣo janmasaptavimocanam divyametat kramāmnāya saptāviṃśat kulājñayā evaṃ vai vindate yo hi sa bhavet kaulabhājana sa muktaḥ sarvapāpebhyo gatvāsau paścime gṛhe kailāśasyopari divye vicareta yathāsukham jarāmaraṇanirmukta siddhatulyo bhavatyasau yamopi vañcitastena yenāmnāya  prapūjitaḥ kramikaḥ sa ca vijñeya  paścime yoginīgṛhe sodhikārī kulakaule deśika  sobhidhīyate kumārikākhaṇḍaanyathā vindate yo hi kramabhedān pṛthak pṛthak na mukta sarvapāpebhyo narakānna nivartate dāridrya vardhate tasya svalpāyu saṃprajāyate anyathā tu kriyācāraṃ mudrāmaṇḍalaka yathā pīṭhaṃ ca pādukāṃ devyā saṃjñāmantrārṇava yathā yo vadet siddhasantāne sa pāpiṣṭhataro bhavet divyakramamida deva bhuktimuktiphalapradam etad deva tavākhyāta kaumārakramanirṇayam śrīnātha uvācaetad vai kramakaumāra divyabhāṣāsamanvitam jñānasādhya sphuṭaṃ bhadre katha pīṭhānvaya bhavet vistareṇa mama brūhi yadi tuṣṭāsi vakrike śrīvakrā uvāca athānyaṃ kramasaṃdeśa vimalārthaṃ yathā sthitam pīṭhādikramacatvārastathā bālakramodayam bālakramasya saṃyogāt kaumāraṃ kathitaṃ tava kaumārakramasaṃyogād bhavate khecaraṃ kramam khecarakramasaṃyogāt vṛddhakrama sphuṭaṃ bhavet ṣaṭprakāramidaṃ kaula guhyasaṃketaka kramam gurukrama navātmāna māyācakrasamanvitamdevyāṣṭakakramaṃ caiva aṣṭāṣṭakamatāntaram evaṃ tu kramaśo jñātvā tathā vai khecarīkramam kumārikākhaṇḍasiddhakrama nirācāraṃ mālinīkramarājakam śabdarāśikramaṃ cānyaṃ tathā vīrāvalīkramamvīrāvalīkrama caiva mātṛkākramanirṇayam yoginīkramamādyaṃ ca tathā vai samayākramam ratnamālākrama divyaṃ maṇḍalakramanirṇayam gṛhabhedakramaṃ cānyaṃ divyakramamataḥ paraṃ merukramaṃ śivamebhiḥ saptāviṃśatkramodayam evaṃ vai kramasaṃjāta jñātvā muktirna saṃśayaḥ ataḥ kramottara nāma mantrāṇā mātarīgṛham pūrvapaścimamadhyaṃ ca vāmadakṣiṇakaulikam yoniṣaṭkaṃ ca śṛṅgāṭa ādikṣānta kuleśvaram evaṃ vai yo vijānāti sa sākṣād bhairava svayam evaṃ kramārthatastattvaṃ saptakoṭyād vinirgatam idaṃ matamida jñeyaṃ idaṃ tattva kulārṇavam kuloyaṃ krama  ogha ca jñānaugha ca tathottamam pūjanīyaṃ prayatnena nindate na kadācana pañcaśrotātmake śaive ṣaṣṭhe kulaviniścaye ākhyātaṃ tu kramāmnāya idaṃ tatsārasaṃgraham  siddhasantāna  subhagaṃ pratyayājñāviśāradam nāmnā kramodayaṃ jñānaṃ śrīkujeśīmahāmatam sadyojātamidaṃ kaulaṃ sadyaḥ sṛṣṭikramodayam sadyo  ādiḥ smṛtaścaiva asadyodbhavakāraka   khegatiṃ kurute sadyo sadyo kaulasya nirṇayam khegati kurute sadyo saṃgho śekharabhāṣitam kumārikākhaṇḍasatyaṃ kulāśrama śreṣṭhaṃ yoginīpaścimaṃ gṛham sarvānandaṃ smṛtaṃ sadyasadyo vai saptakoṭikam saṃpradāyamida sadya  sadyonugrahanigraham pāramparyakramaṃ sadyaḥ sadyo śaivasya nirṇayam sadyo hi bhavate sarva śrīmataṃ paścimaṃ gṛham evaṃ sadyovihīnā ye paścimāmnāyavarjitāḥ na teṣāmabhiṣeka tu deśikatvaṃ na vidyate kulānvayena hīno yo nādhikārī śivāgame dīkṣitāstena ye deva na te mokṣasya bhājanā prakaṭaṃ na likhed deva kramārthedaṃ mukhodgatam guruvaktre sthitaṃ nityaṃ guruvaktrāt tu labhyate evaṃ sadya samāyukta kaulikastu yadā bhavet paśusaṃgād vinaśyeta yadi sākṣāt sadāśiva  asatsaṅgaṃ na kartavyaṃ asatsaṅgād vinaśyativiśuddhaṃ kāñcana  yadvannāgasaṅgād  vinaśyatievaṃ śuddhavataḥ sopi asatsaṅgād vinaśyati paśusaṅgānna mukti syādabhiṣekānna mucyati kumārikākhaṇḍaityādyāvatāre mahāmanthānabhairavayajñe anvaye saptakoṭipramāṇe merumārgavinirgatelakṣapādādhike vidyāpīṭhamārge vimalaṣaṭkanirṇaye kādibhede ājñāpārameśvaresvāminīmate śrīcaturviṃśatsahasrasaṃhitāyāṃ avvākramabhāṣitekramamañjūṣādhikāravarṇane kramodayo nāmānandaḥ śrīvakrā uvācaṣaṭcatvāriṃśānandaḥathā pravakṣyāmi tattvapīṭhodaya  śubham kāmākhye pṛthivī jñeyā tejo dakṣiṇapīṭhake āpaḥ pūrṇagiristhitaḥ vāyuroṃkārasaṃsthitaḥ ākāśaṃ sarvapīṭheṣu pīṭhabhūtāni me smṛtāḥ śabdo vijānīyāt sparśa tasyaiva cāgrataḥ rasa taduttare mārge rūpaṃ dakṣiṇakoṇake kailāśānte tu gandhatvatanmātramiti pañcakam ākāśe saṃsthitā tu vā pāṇiścāgre sadāśivaḥ pādau dakṣiṇapīṭhe tu pāyuścottarakoṇagaḥ upasthaṃ tisramadhye tu pañcakarmendriyāṇi me śrotraṃ jālandhare pīṭhe tvacokta pūrṇagiryake cakṣurmadhye vijānīyājjihvā kāmākhyamaṇḍale nāsikā tisrapīṭhe tu evaṃ jñānendriyāṇi tu kāmākhye tu manaḥ proktaṃ buddhiścodyāṇamaṇḍale dakṣiṇasthamahaṃkāraṃ prakṛti paścime viduḥ puruṣo madhyame pīṭhe pañcaite kulabhūṣaṇāḥ kumārikākhaṇḍapañcaviṃśatitattvāni yogapīṭhe udāhṛtāḥ jñātavyāstu prayatnena guṇatrayasamanvitāḥ sattvamagre vijānīyād rajamuttaramaṇḍale tamaṃ tu dakṣiṇe mārge pañcaratnamataḥ śṛṇu kāmarūpe sthito brahmā viṣṇuścottarapīṭhake rudro jālākhyasaṃjñe tu īśvarastisrapīṭha sadāśivastayormadhye pañcaite sṛṣṭikārakāḥ guptā saṃjñā pravakṣyāmi yathoktā saptakoṭiṣu śakaronanta śrīkaṇṭhaḥ piṅgalaśca caturthakaḥ sādākhya pañcamo deva pañcaite amarakārakāḥ pūjanīyāśca satataṃ siddhiṛddhipradāyakāḥ yonimudrā tu kāmākhye karālā dakṣiṇe viduḥ padminī pūrṇagiryāyāṃ ghaṭamudrāntarālake kadambinī tisrapīṭhe mudrāṇāṃ pañcakodayam caturvidhaṃ smṛtaṃ dhyānaṃ śyāmavarṇoḍḍiyāṇakam  rakta jālandharaṃ proktaṃ pīta vai vāmagocare śvetaṃ tu cottara dhyānaṃ kāmākhye tu vijānataḥ niścalaṃ madhyamaṃ dhyānaṃ calaṃ dakṣiṇataḥ sthitam uttare dvisvabhāvaṃ tu susthiraṃ dhyānamagrataḥ kumārikākhaṇḍamadhye kṛtayuga deva tretā dakṣiṇakoṇagā uttare dvāparaṃ jñeyaṃ agrataḥ kalirucyate evaṃ caturyugaṃ prokta mudrācakre maheśvara vṛkṣatrayaṃ trikoṇasthaṃ kadamba cāgrato viduḥ dakṣiṇe kathitaṃ bilva ciñcākhya tu tathottare evaṃ tattvavibhāgena yogapīṭhamudrāhṛtam kulavṛkṣatrayaṃ vakṣye kulamārgeṇa sundara tejamadhyagatā buddhiścittavṛttirubhāvapi advaitavāsanāyāṃ tu tridhā trīṇi vyavasthitāḥ samarasaṃ tatra vidyeta bhagāhlādena ciñciṇī kalāśeṣaṃ mano gatvā bhramate tu kadambakam maṇipūrṇakalādhāre jāyate mriyate  sadā ātmā ca vadate nityaṃ virute tu kadambakam bilva ca jāyate binduḥ ūdhva ūdhvavighaṭṭanāt dṛṣṭādṛṣṭavibhedena ciñciṇīvṛkṣasaṃjñakam vṛkṣopadeśamākhyāta kulavṛkṣatrayaṃ bahiḥ yo jānāti mahādeva matārthī sa nigadyate śrīnātha uvācapīṭhānāṃ kīrtanaṃ jñānaṃ yena siddhyanti sādhakā anyad me saṃśaya devi kathayasva prasādataḥ śrīvakrā uvāca kumārikākhaṇḍana kasyacinmayākhyātaṃ tava deva vadāmyaham brahmādidevatādīnāṃ na mayā saṃprakāśitam  yathāvatāritaṃ tena devena parameṣṭhinā tat tehaṃ kathayiṣyāmi ātmāsavittikāraṇam yādṛśaṃ pūrvavṛttāntaṃ tādṛśaṃ kathayāmi te śrīkaṇṭhaḥ śaṅkaronantaḥ sādākhya piṅgalastathā pañcaite vyāpakā loke bhūtagrā caturvidhe śrīkaṇṭhaḥ pṛthivī jñeyaḥ śaṅkara āpa ucyate tejonanta iti khyātaḥ sādākhyo vāyurucyate ākāśa piṅgalo jñeyaḥ pañcaite sṛṣṭikārakāḥ evaṃ pañcātmaka deva nigrahānugrahe sthitam ciñciṇīnāthadevoyaṃ ājñāsiddhimahātapaḥ vidyāt sarvajñabhāvena lolībhūtena cetasā unmattacaryacāreṇa caratyevaṃ carācare yaduktaṃ piṅgalaṃ nāma siddhanāthamanāmayam sarvajñaṃ sarvagaṃ nityaṃ avatīrṇa dharātale kṣīrodasyottare kule hemaratnamayottame vicitramaṇiśobhāḍhye ratnakūṭāca śubhe mahākṣīrodakallole nitya dhautaśilātale siddharṣigaṇagandharvasurāsuraniṣevite kumārikākhaṇḍaḥumā dākṣāyaṇī kanyā tatra tena anugraham kṛtvā tu bhārate varṣe caturmūyāvatārakam trailokyanagare sarvalokānā tārakaṃ param bhavārṇavanimagnānā gotrabhedakṛta priya prathamaṃ mitranātha  vai caryānātha dvitīyakam tṛtīyaṃ ṣaṣṭhasaṃjñākhya oḍḍīśākhya caturthakam ādyametaccatuṣkaṃ tu caturyuge mukhāmbuja catuḥpīṭhādhikārārthamavattīrṇa dinotta śrīmadoḍḍīśanāthoya tūṣṇīśākhyena viśrutaḥ tadekaṃ svecchayā dehamālambya navadhā punaḥ śiṣyatvena svayaṃ deva bhaviṣyatyātmanaḥ kalau anugrahārthaṃ jagata saṃjñābhedamihocyate gaganendro mahākubjo ratneśaḥ padmabhāskaraḥ devavaktrāmṛtaścānyo bhairavābjaśca pañcamaḥ kamalārka śivāmbhojo rāmatattvātmā eva ca kṛṣṇamārtaṇḍanāthaśca navaite siddhanāyakāḥ pauṇḍrākhye ca ahicchatre pure śrībhogavardhane pāṭalīnagare ramye māyāpuryā varānana kanyakubje alampure ayodhyā vardhamānake sthāneṣveteṣu deveśa divyamānuṣayonijāḥ jñānayogabalopetā svādhārā kaulikānvaye anugṛhītā  deveśa devenājñārkabimbaje kumārikākhaṇḍadivyaraśmikarairbhuktimuktidaistrividhaiḥ  kramāt śrāvaṇāṣāḍhavaiśākhacaitrakārttikapañcabhiḥsaṃpūrṇadivasairdeva avatāraṃ krameṇa tu gaganeśādināthānā pañcānā tattvatoditam kaumāramṛgacaitrasya  śuklāyāmaṣṭamī tathā dvādaśyāṃ cārkasaptamyā bhūtā phālgunasya ca caturṇā kamalādīnā siddhīśānāmudāhṛtam nākhyeyametat sahasā rahasya bhuvi durlabham prathamaṃ ca dvitīya ca vyatyayenāṣṭama tathā traya te pare dhāmni līnā santānavarjitāḥtṛtīyaṃ pañcamaṃ yacca ṣaṣṭhaṃ caiva tathāparam munīnā svāminādiṣṭā kṛpayānugraha prati kalpagrāma gatā hyete trayogrā ūdhvaretasaḥ navama saptamaṃ vātha caturthaṃ tāni pūrvavat śrīsantānakule trīṇi jyeṣṭhaṃ madhya yavīyasam krameṇa gaditā sṛṣṭināthādyā  siddhanāyakāḥ tīkṣaṇājñā  sukarā vyagrā nigrahānugrahe ratāḥ carācarasya viśvasya bhuktimuktyamṛtapradāḥ jñānāsavamadonmattā ānandalalitekṣaṇāḥsvarūpānandasaṃtṛptā ājñāsiddhikarā smṛtāḥ sarve sarvajñabhāvena lolībhūtena cetasā saṃbhāṣaṃ na kuryāt kuladeśikaḥ bhavate yoginīdroho ājñābhaṅgaḥ pravartate madyaṃ nāma paraṃ prokta samaya pārameśvaram asamayināmida deva gopanīyaṃ prayatnataḥ samayabhaṅgeṣu dāridrya maraṇaṃ dīpakaṃ carukaṃ bhakṣaṃ kṛtvā pānaṃ pibet tadā kumārikākhaṇḍapuṣpaṃ dhūpaṃ pradatvā tu svagotra sahitaikataḥ samayapātraṃ prakartavya nirvikalpena sundara ekata sarvavarṇāni sadā cakre upasthitāḥ cakrād bahirviniṣkrāntā sarve va pṛthak pṛthak vaṇītarjanyā tarpaṇaṃ kṛtvā antarikṣe kṣamaṇḍale sandhāne tarpitā yānti tṛptā siddhiṃ dadanti ca madhyamātarpaṇaṃ kṛtvā antarikṣe khamaṇḍale pitara punaḥguruṇā  sthāpayet tatra gurureko hi pañcadhā kumārikākhaṇḍaḥatha caitad dvayaṃ yuktaṃ sāmānyaiḥ pañcabhiḥ kṣipet puṣpaṃ sthaṇḍilamadhye tu paścimābhimukhaṃ karam sahitaṃ vāmahastena vāmāvartaparibhramāt pañcapraṇavamuccārya tanmadhye puṣpapañcakam sāmānyairāsanapakṣaṃ muṣṭau cāṅguṣṭhamagrataḥ akhaṇḍādi kramāt pañca pūjayeta vidhānavit paścānyāsa tu navadhā amṛtādivibhāgaśaḥ uttare vinyaset soma sūryamīśānamaṇḍale nairṛtye vinyaset kūṭaṃ binducakra tu dakṣiṇe pūrve purandara deva varuṇa paścimādiśi vahnikoṇe nyasedagni vāyukoṇe cala nyaset tato hastaṃ samuddhṛtya kaniṣṭhāṅguṣṭhamadhyamāḥ mudrātritayayogena mekhalātritayaṃ kramāt karayoradhaḥ kartavya navamaṃ bījanāyakam śrīnāthaṃ pūjayenmadhye puṣpāṃjalibhiḥ pañcabhiḥ dakṣiṇe tu tathā vāme alinā maṇḍaladvayam vāmāvartena kartavyaṃ nābhyā bījadvayaṃ nyaset prāṇabījaṃ nyased vāme nābhidakṣiṇato nyaset āsanaṃ tu samākhyātaṃ vaṭukeśvarayoginī mudrāmaṇḍalasyāgre tu maṇḍala ca pṛthak pṛthak pañcādi vinyased bījān itīṣṭau kārayet sadā tatraiva paścime mārge pañcāṅgule ca maṇḍale kumārikākhaṇḍaḥbindunā saha śaktyākhya kūṭaṃ madhye vinikṣipet evaṃ kūrmāsanasthena navamaṇḍalamaṇḍitam gurumaṇḍalamevaṃ hi ākhyātaṃ ca trayoliṣu toyaṃ gandhamali puṣpaṃ piśitaṃ cārghadhūpakam saṃpūrṇaṃ kārayet pātraṃ dakṣahastena tvanagha dakṣeṇa daṇḍamudrāṃ tu kṣetrapālasya dakṣiṇe uttare yoginīnā tu vāmahastena sundara pātraṃ dakṣakare kṛtvā sthāpya maṇḍalamadhyataḥ balitrayamidaṃ datvā ācamanaṃ ca tataḥ punaḥupaviśyāsa badhvā śambhuśaktiṃ tu vinyaset karābhyā pañcadhā nyastvā śuddhayarthaṃ dahanaṃ tathā taḍidvidyutsvarūpeṇa kārayet karasaṃpuṭam āpyāyanaṃ karābhyāṃ tu uttānābhyāṃ samabhyaset savisargeṇa candreṇa mantrapādena kārayet kālānalasamaprakhyaṃ paścāstra tu bhrāmayet āgneyā ciñciṇīmudrā ciñciṇyājñādharā   dharmādharmo parityajya adhañcoṣva prapīḍayet adhomukhaṃ tu yat padma raktaṃ vikasitaṃ smaret tatra madhye mahālakṣaṃ candrakoṭisamaprabham vidrumākārarūpeṇa mahāvahniśikhā iva  kumārikākhaṇḍamadhyanāḍīpravāhena śaktyūve nīyate pare śanaiḥ śanairdahyamānā yāvat samarasa  padam dahanaṃ tāvadākhyāta dagdhe dehe layaṃ vrajet punarāpyāyana mūna śamanāntāt parā kalā śravantī paramā sūkṣmā mṛṇālatanturūpiṇīṃ cintayennāḍimadhyasthāyāvad vai janmamaṇḍalam tāvadāpyāyanaṃ śambho kṛtvā nyāsamataḥ param karamadhye mūrtipakṣa ājñā muṣṭidvaye nyaset  karāgre ūdhvavatra tu mūrdhamaṅguṣṭha nyaset tarjanī pūrvavakā tu madhyamāyā tu dakṣiṇam uttaronāmikāyā tu paścimaṃ tu kaniṣṭhike aṅguṣṭhe hṛdayaṃ nyasya uttamāṅgaṃ tu tarjanī śikhā vai madhyamāyāṃ tu kavacaṃ tu anāmike netra vai kanyasāyā tu astra tu karapṛṣṭhataḥkaranyāsamida proktaṃ mūrtipakṣāditaḥ kramāt hṛdaye vinyasenmūrti mūrdhādicaraṇāvadhimājñātattvaṃ samākhyātaṃ śaktyante ūdhvamānanam mastake mūrdhavakā tu pūrvavatra mukheṃ nyaset kumārikākhaṇḍaḥdakṣiṇaṃ hṛdi madhye tu uttaraṃ guhyamaṇḍale pādābhyāṃ paścimaṃ vaktraṃ daṇḍanyāsaṃ prakīrtitam purodhve ūdhvavatra tu mū mūrdhani vinyaset pūrvataḥ pūrvavaktraṃ tu dakṣiṇe dakṣiṇānanam uttare cottaraṃ nyasya paścime paścima nyasethṛdaye hṛdaya nyasya śira śirasi vinyaset śikhāyāṃ tu śikhā nyasya sarvāṅgeṣu tanutrakam netraṃ vai netrayonyasya astraṃ tu karapṛṣṭhataḥ kujānyāsamida kṛtvā paścāt pātra  tu vinyaset dhūpaṃ caiva tathādhāre argha śrīkāramaṇḍale prasādena bhaved gandhaṃ rāvasya kusumāni ca sauṃkāra maṇḍalasyānte varuṇe tu samuccaret astreṇa śodhayet sarvaṃ kavacenāvaguṇṭhayet āpyāyana tu netreṇa kārayed dhenumudrayā mālinyādi nyased paścād yathā bhavati tacchṛṇu mālinī śabdarāśiśca trividyāghorikāṣṭakam dvādaśāṅgasamudbhūtaṃ ṣaḍaṅgaṃ ratnapañcakam ślokadvādaśikā mālā pādādau śikhayāvadhiḥ mekhalāyā nyased deva vilomenopadeśata kumārikākhaṇḍaḥbrahmasūtrojjvalā śambho skandhobhau tadgrahānvitau ṣoḍaśagranthisaṃyuktaṃ navātmānandananditam mukhakośaṃ ca vinyāsa iṣṭaṃ caiva paṭārgalam ṣoḍhānyāsa samākhyātaṃ bhedaiḥ ṣoḍaśabhiḥ sthitam ṣoḍhānyāsamidaṃ kṛtvā kramamaṇḍalamuddharet gurumaṇḍalamevaṃ hi ākhyātaṃ paścimānvaye śrīvakrā uvācagurumaṇḍalanirmukta kārayet gurumaṇḍalam triḥkāla kūṭanāthena tatra pañcakamāruhet yugmabhedaṃ tato nātha antaraṅgesamadhyaset mahābalaviniyukta balidvaya samuddharet mudrābandhasamāyukta prasāda tava khaṇḍitam labdhvā kāruṇyamudaya paścād dehe parigraham antaraṅgeṇa sūtreṇa jñānasūtreṇa bheditam sūtrajñānavinirmukto bhedayet kūṭamaṇḍalam kūṭa japtvā lakṣameka mantrajāpasamāhitaḥ purāveśaṃ tato dehe gahvarasyāpi vartanam kumārikākhaṇḍatat gahvaraṃ tathā dehe svātmanaḥ bahi kārayet paradehe samuttīrṇa paradehāt samuddharet samūrte ca pare tattve padaṃ padaṃ dvikaṃ dvikam trikaṃ trikaṃ catuṣkaṃ tu catuṣkaṃ ṣaṭkameva ca ṣaṭkaṃ ca apara bhittvā bhittvā sthāne pṛthak pṛthak kuṭilā pūrvamāsthāya   kareṇa pañca ca pūrṇimāntyasphura kṛtvā amāvasyā pravartate pakṣadvayavinirmuktā madhye pratipadā smṛtā ājñāmṛtapravāhena sakalīkṛtavigrahaḥ pañcacakrāṇi vai hitvā ṣaṣṭhaṃ pūrva nirāmayam vinyaset jñānamāsādya tasyaite pañca vyāpakāḥ sṛṣṭikrameṇa satataṃ saṃhāreṇa tu yoginām tatrāṅgāni samutsṛjya upāṅgāni tu vinyaset olitritayabhedena mudrātrayaṃ tu vinyaset mudrātrikaṃ purā nyastvā kramamaṇḍalamuddharet  gahvaraṃ cālikhet pūrve gahvareṇāpi bhedayet ūdhvato gahvareṇāpi vṛttarājena veṣṭayet caturviṃśatitattvaiśca saṃbhṛtaṃ kārayet tadā dalānyaṣṭau krameṇāpi diśāsu vidiśāsu ca mekhalātritayaṃ bāhye krameṇa parivartayet kumārikākhaṇḍaḥcaturastra puraṃ kṛtvā vibhajya tadanantaram madhye khapuṣpaṃ saṃsthāpya upadeśena gahvaram ityukta maṇḍalaṃ nātha tatra lakṣmī samuddharet paścāt pātratrayaṃ deva purasthāne samuddharet pañcabrahmavibhāgena ādau vāme prakalpayet tatra manthānabhedena upadeśa tu pañcadhā tatrānandapure madhye samayaṃ tasya vinyaset hṛṣṭi tuṣṭiṃ tadā kṛtvārṣapātra tu dakṣiṇe arghapātravinirmukto gāyatryā bheditaṃ tataḥ arghaṃ paramabījena śivena saha arcayet puṣpadhūpādi yat kiñcit svavidhiṣu yathākramam sarvasaṃbhārametaddhi antaryage samuddharet gurvoghaṃ olipīṭha tu puṣpasaṃketaka smaret teṣvadhaḥ pūjayedātmā olipīṭhāditaḥ kramāt yāvat pīṭhacatuṣkaṃ tu teṣāṃ deśacatuṣṭayam catvāro nāyakā  siddhā olipīṭhāditaḥ kramāt oṃkāre pañcamaṃ nāthaṃ ājñāṣaṭka krameṇa tu agrakoṇa samārabhya pūrvādau yāvanmadhyamam puna siddhāstu catvāraḥ pūrvapīṭhāditaḥ kramāt yoginīgaṇamevaṃ hi siddhasthāneṣu pūjayet trikaṃ triṣu ca koṇeṣu pūjayedupadeśataḥ saptāviṃśatibhedāni vaktraṣaṭka krameṇa tu kumārikākhaṇḍaūdhvavaktra koṭimadhye mū codhvamātrataḥ pūrvaṃ tadastrakoṇe tu dakṣiṇe dakṣamānanam uttare vāmavaktraṃ syāt madhye paścimamānanam hṛdayaṃ kāmarūpe tu śiraḥ pūrṇagirau smṛtaḥ śikhā jālandhare pīṭhe kavacaṃ tisrapīṭhake netraṃ caivārdhacandre tu astraṃ vai bindumaṇḍale madhye ājñā prapūjyā ca dvātriṃśāṇī kurūpiṇī daleṣu pūrvamārabhya vāmāvarte kulāṣṭakam mekhalāyā puruṣaugha bhedaiśca pañcaviṃśatiḥ upadeśena vai jñātvā maṇḍalānyaṣṭaviṃśatiḥ tṛtīyamekhalāyā tu catuḥṣaṣṭistu devatāḥ sarvogha prathamaṃ sāraṃ kramaugha tu dvitīyakam vidyaugha ca tṛtīyaṃ syāt kulaugha tu caturthakam pañcamaṃ puruṣaugha tu ṣaṣṭhaṃ divyaughamuttamam vidyaugha ṣaḍvidhābhinna jñātvā yajanamārabhet oghānyeva diśānyaṣṭau pūrvādārabhya tu kramāt kṣetrāṇyāṣṭau yajed deva prayāgādikrameṇa tu samayā ca tribhirbhedairyajet koṇatrayeṣu ca stutyagre mātaro dakṣe mantrakhaṇḍottare bhavet kumārikākhaṇḍakoṇatraya samāsādya dvānavatyā śatadvayam trikhaṇḍābhairavīdevīṃ yajed yatnānmaheśvara upadeśatrayaṃ bhittvā aṣṭadhāsiddhiriṣyate tanmadhye devatāliṅgaṃ tithyodayaṃ pravartate yajet tadgatacittātmā sṛṣṭinyāyena bhairava yasya yā bhavate vidyā tasya sā śrī  oḍḍiyāṇake yāvat dvātriṃśasaṃkhyayā tāvat saṃśodhayet puram pure śuddhe sarvaśuddhirityājñā pārameśvarī samayalopāni sarvāṇi śuddhyante ca caturyuge koṇatraye tadante ca jñātvā vidyārthino mahatadhikāra ca kartavyaṃ śrīmaccandrapure gṛhe antaryāgamidaṃ śambho olitritayaśāsane śāmbhavājñāviniṣkrāntaṃ yo jānāti sa yoginaḥ ityupadeśasūtra tu bhāvitānāṃ pade pade devatājñā prakurute pāśastobhādipratyayam sūtropadeśanirmukta kramaṃ yotrāvatārayet parāṅmukhaṃ bhavet tasya paratra  nānuvartate aprakāśyaṃ jagannātha  hṛdayānandakārakam guptād guptataraṃ kārya śāmbhavājñāprakāśakam ityādyāvatāre caturviṃśatisāhasre kramasūtrādhikāraḥ  ūnapañcāśānandaḥśrīkaulīśa uvācaantaryāga na me jñātaṃ mānasaṃ yad vyavasthitam tasya dhyānaṃ ca sakala divyapiṇḍaṃ salakṣaṇam kāruṇyād vada devadeveśi yadi tuṣṭāsi kubjike śrīkubjikā uvācaatigopyataraṃ praśna tvayogīta sureśvara rakṣet prāṇavad rudra sarvaṃ gopyaṃ suyatnataḥ samayamudrā gṛhṇīyāt padmakaṃ svastikāsanam prabhāte samaye snātvā paścimābhimukhasthitaḥ mṛdvāsanopaviṣṭastu ekacitta samāhitaḥ ākramya sutalasthānaṃ adhova vighaṭṭitam recaka pūrakaṃ kṛtvā kumbhake manarodhanam svakīya pīṭha saṃsmṛtvā tanmadhye śaktimaṇḍalam tejorāśisamaprakhyaṃ dyotayantaṃ nabhastalam tanmadhye vedhayed binduṃ jvālājvalanasannibham akhaṇḍamaṇḍalākāraṃ vāyupañcakabheditam svarūpaṃ paśyate bimbaṃ candramaṇḍalavartulam tatra pūjā prakartavyā antaḥsthānubhavena tu kumārikāṃkhaṇḍaḥkandasthānāt samutthāpya spandakuṇḍalinīṃ parām nādena sahajā bodhyā ādhāre ravimaṇḍale dīptakāñcanasaṃkāśā tamadhvaṃsavināśinī taḍidvalayacakrātmā lohacūrṇavinisṛtā sānusvāreṇa mantrajñaḥ praviśeccandramaṇḍale māyā bindustathātmā vai nāda śakti śivastathā krameṇa kramaśo yojyā krama bhittvā hyanukramāt susūkṣmaṃ kalitaṃ rāva avyucchinnaṃ pravartate tad gatvā ramate yogī kaulinīṃ kulanāyikām tatra madhye sthitaṃ divyaṃ haṃsākhya parameśvaram adehe dehasaṃsthaṃ tu cicchaktyādhiṣṭhitaṃ kramāt tasyopalabdhimātreṇa kramabheda pravartate bhagnakāṃsamaya śabda śrūyate jñānakarṇena ghaṇṭā śabdamiti proktaṃ tena sūrye ca maṇḍale  nāyikā samayā ghaṇṭā ghaṭitā viśvakarmaṇā antaraṅge smṛtā ghaṇṭā sā dūtī sarvakāmadā bahi kāṃsyamayā dūtī sthityarthaṃ samupāgatā dīpa cakṣūnmanībhāva avasthā iti pratyayam dvādaśānte smṛtaṃ toyaṃ patate yonimaṇḍale malaya ceti kailāsa śamanamiti candanam kumārikākhaṇḍayā kalpā śukrasaṃpūrṇa triṣkoṇākhye tu maṇḍale sā ca kāmāturā deva śamanena vibhedayet tenāmṛtena mānasā kṣībonmattāśca yoginaḥ tanmadyāmṛtamāsvādya naiva madyaviḍambanā āgopālāṅganā mlecchā śūdrāḥ prākṛtakāstu ye pītenaiva va madyena kṣībonmattā samantataḥ tumadyaṃ tu kṛtrima bāhyaṃ sāmānyaṃ sarvajantuṣu lohitaṃ padmarāgena tri koṇe paṭṭa rājate tameva piśitaṃ prokta etad grāhyaṃ kramārcane juṣṭhacaṇḍālinī nāma vidyākhyā ca tavānvaye vidyābhūtakhaliṅgena sakalaṃ dhyānamācaret mama tu yoktavidyā yā ākhyātā tava sundara olitraye trikoṇāṃnte adhomāgavalambinī vāḍavena tu rūpeṇa dhyātavyā kubjikā hyaham trinetrā ṣaḍbhujākārā ṣaḍvaktrā ca mahābalā śyāmā raktā ca vakrā ca sarvaratnaistu maṇḍitā kaṭakeyūrahāraistu kuṇḍalai sumanoharā karṇapūrī tu candrā bālendukṛtaśekharā mastakābharaṇā śaktirmaṇimālāsuśobhitā barbarā keśabhārā tu tanvaṅgī cārulocanā nagnā muktaśikhā devī nagnavāsā digambarā capalā candrapūrṇa ca netrābhyāṃ vartulānanā kumārikākhaṇḍatriṣkoṇānanasaṃdīptā vidyutpuñjasamaprabhā sphijai śailai  susaṃpūrṇa jarjarā siddhavanditā caraṇau nupūrasaṃlagnau kaṭikā pūrṇamaṇḍitā mañjarī ratnakhacitā vāmahaste pratiṣṭhitā dakṣiṇe śūlahastā ca vāmahaste kapālakam dakṣiṇe khaḍgavidyeya dakṣahaste sadoditā vāsukīhāranicayā sarvābharaṇabhūṣitā raktānanā ca hrasvā ca garjantī meghaśabdavat kruddhadṛṣṭirmahāsiṃhā siṃhāsanasamāśritā aṭṭāṭṭahāsavadanā nṛtyantī vahnimaṇḍale sarvāvayavasaṃpūrṇa nānāvidhairalaṅkṛtā kuṭilāṅgī tathā stabdhvā vakrarūpā bhayaṅkarī mātaṅgī madirānandā madonmattātilālasā amoghamoghavarṣantī amṛtarūpaṃ vicintayet mahāvyome samālīnā brahmarandhrapravāhinī āpyāyet sarvabhūtānāṃ bhairavī bharaṇātmikānitambagrīvasphijau gāvau kiñcitkuñcitalocanā śaktyante vedhayellakṣya mahāvyoma nirīkṣayet tatra nagnavasā devī paripūrṇa suśobhitā devai parivṛtā devī mahāyonau paristhitā paśyantī sādhakān vīrān sarveṣāṃ ca phalapradā kaulinī kathitā tubhya atigopyā gurūpamā yat kiñcid vāñcchita kāma tat sarva kathita mayā kumārikākhaṇḍaetat divyaughasūtra tu nirṇaya pīṭhadevyāstu mudraiṣā ṣaḍbhi pīṭhaistu dhyānalakṣaṃ niyojayet paścāt ṣaḍvidha vinyāsaṃ dhyānasūtraṃ ca ṣaḍvidham saṃjñākramasamāyukta yogaṃ pujītanantaram sākṣāt mama kramāmnāya sūcitaṃ na vicāritam hemapuṣpaiśca vividhaiḥ sugandhaiśca sukalpitaiḥ candanairalipātraiśca naivedyaiḥ phalguṣādikaiḥ nivedya vidhivad bhaktyā devyāgre tu subhāvitā dīpakā vividhākārā godhūmādivinirmitāḥ athavā yavacūrṇena saṃkhyayā kuladevatām dviraṅgulocchrayeṇaiva cchatraṃ kuryād dviraṅgulam bhagākārā prakartavyāḥ pramāṇena tu dīpakāḥ kṛtvā rātrau paṭhet stotraṃ mālinīdaṇḍakaṃ śubham devyāvṛtāṣṭaka vāpi tathā olitrayeṇa vā pūjānte tu namaskāraṃ vidhānena namaskaret tryaṅgena triraṅgaṃ tu praṇavatrayapuṭīkṛtam pañcapraṇava  tato nyastvā  pañcāṅgena namaskaret atha vargān tato nyastvā aṣṭāṅgena namaskaret tryaṅga caiva tu pañcāṅgaṃ aṣṭāṅgaṃ ca tṛtīyakam namaskāratraya kṛtvā daṇḍavat tu punaḥ punaḥ namaskaret kumāryaṣṭau catvāroṃ dve ca ekā vākulavidyā japitvā tu naivedyaṃ tu nivedayet kumārikākhaṇḍaḥtilakānukrame kṛtvā naivedyaṃ tu nivedayet mudrābandhairvisarjitvā bhairavīṃ samayāṃ yajet yaṣṭvā namaskared deva mūlasūtreṇa bhaktimān tilakānukrame kṛtvā svagotre samayānvitam kūrmāsanopaviṣṭe tu mudrābandhakaradvaye caruka kaulikaṃ śreṣṭha devānāmapi durlabham prathamaṃ kuladīpāni alidravyamataḥ param caru piśitasamiśraṃ nirvikalpena prāśayet saptākṣarā mahāvidyā sarvasiddhikarī smṛtā saptajaptena pūtoya vaṭuka siddhidāyakam na dvaitaṃ sādhakaiḥ sārdhaṃ guruṇā ca mahādvaitam viruddhaṃ bhrātṛbhijyeṣṭhai viruddha pūrvadīkṣitaiḥ śuvedhi  caiva jyeṣṭhānāṃ mantriṇāṃ matabodhakām nocchiṣṭaṃ carukaṃ dadyāt puṣpaṃ jyeṣṭhopi yo bhavet anyathā kurute deva ājñābhaṅgaḥ pravartate prāśayitvā vidhānena carukaṃ piśitāsavam ācamya ca śucirbhūtvā vidyāṃ ca samayāṃ yajet tadatirikta yat kiñcit śuddhyate nātra saṃśayaḥ śire kṛtvā tu nairmālya maṇḍalaṃ tu visarjayet ākarṣayet tataḥ paścād vilomānmūlavidyayā kramārcanamida proktaṃ parvakāle tu kārayet ye yoginīkule jātā labhante śāśvataṃ padam kumārikākhaṇḍaanyā jāti kriyā cānyā kāla mantropi cānyathā maṇḍalaṃ pādukā devyāḥ  pūjā āgamamanyathā yo vadet siddhasantāne sa pāpiṣṭhataro bhavet satyaṃ satyaṃ punaḥ satyaṃ trisatyaṃ kathitaṃ mayā nāśiṣyāya pradātavyaṃ na ca putrasya bhairava bhraturapi na dātavyaṃ abhakteṣu viśeṣataḥ uparodhānna dātavyaṃ na caivārthasya lobhataḥ gurubhaktā krame bhaktāḥ samayācārapālakāḥ teṣāṃ deyamidaṃ sūtraṃ yasya tuṣṭo bhavet kila akrameṇa gurorājñā yo dadati ca gṛhaṇate yāvadāyutasaṃplavāubhau tau narakaṃ yātauiti śrīcaturviṃśatisahasre antaryāgamūrtidhyānasūtram śrīvakrā uvācapañcāśānandaḥdhyānaṃ kuryād yathāvasthaḥ abhyased yonimudrayā krama pūjya śarīrasthaṃ yathā sūtre prakāśitam śrīkaulīśa uvācasvaśarīre mahādevi kramapūjā yathā bhavet yeṣu yeṣu ca sthāneṣu mantroddhārasamanvitā caturvidyā tathā devi sucitā na prakāśitā kāruṇyād vada deveśi mama bhaktasya bhairavi śrīvakrā uvācatataḥ pūjākramaṃ sarvaṃ vartate tu yathākramam mastakeṃ gurupaktistu kāmarūpāgrato yajet ātmā nāma ca hṛdayeṃ pīṭhaugha mastake sthitam agrakoṇe tathā vāme dakṣiṇe madhyataḥ kramāt yajet pīṭhacatuṣkaṃ tu pañcakaṃ vaktramaṇḍale vaktramadhye vāmacakṣurbhūmadhye dakṣacakṣuṣi nāsikāgre tathā pūjya jñānaṣaṭkamataḥ param kumārikākhaṇḍaḥhṛdaye vāmamārge tu vāmaskandhe tathāparam bhrūmadhye dakṣiṇe skandhe dakṣamārge trikaṃ bhavet ṣaṭka devyā idaṃ cakraṃ sṛṣṭinyāyena pūjayet tataḥ siddhacatuṣkaṃ tu tatrādhastāt prapūjayet janmacakre  tu vai pūjya yoginīgaṇapañcakam upadeśa tu vai pūjya svapīṭhe tu maheśvara tuaṣṭāviṃśatibhedāni pāramparyasthitāni tu ṣaṭkārāṇi pūjyeta ājñācakrānukramāt pādādau jānuparyantaṃ samastavyastaśāsanam yaṣṭvā sakalakāmāni pratyayāni bahūnyapi ityāśrame susaṃpanne mūrtipakṣaṃ tu vinyaset aājñātattva   tu tatraiva savaktrāṅgāni kalpayet vaktrairvaktrāṇi  vai pūjya aṅgairaṅgāni pūjayet kulāṣṭakaṃ mahāśambho pādād pūjya yathākramam brahmāṇī pādayoḥ pūjyā jānudeśe maheśvarī kaumārī guhyadeśe tu vaiṣṇavī nābhisaṃsthitā vārāhī jaṭhare pūjyā indrāṇī hṛdimaṇḍale kumārikākhaṇḍatṛtīyaṃ maṇipūre tu caturthaṃ pañcamaṃ tathā punarādhāre saṃpūjya ṣaṣṭhaṃ vai svādhiṣṭhānake saptamaṃ navamaṃ yāvat turyātīte prapūjayet nava siddhāḥ samākhyātā  ṣoḍaśāpyathavā śṛṇu aṣṭau kapālamālāyāṃ navamaṃ nābhimaṇḍale dvipañcāt ṣoḍaśaṃ yāvat bhagamālā prapūjayet maṇḍalāni yathā deva svaśarīre vyavasthitāḥ hrīṃ śrīṃ pūrvakrameṇaiva tathoccāra samabhyaset prathamaṃ dakṣiṇe cakṣurgaṇḍe karṇe tataḥ punaḥ śikhare ca bhuje dakṣe bāhau madhyakare tathā kukṣau sphije jānujaṅghe pāde caiva tu dakṣiṇe vāme pāde ja jānusphije vāme ca cakṣuṣi kare vai bāhumadhye tu vāmaskandhe ca karṇataḥ tathā kapole vaktre ca lalāṭe ca kṛkāṭikām pṛṣṭhamadhye  tathādhāre hṛdaye vaktramaṇḍale eteṣu maṇḍalā  pūjyā aṣṭāviṃśatisaṃkhyayā aṣṭāṣṭaka yajed deva diśāsu vidiśāsu ca catuḥṣaṣṭirmahādevyāḥ pūjayed  vidhipūrvakam etat te kathitaṃ śambho kṣetrāṇi kathayāmyaham kṣetra nāma paraṃ śānta śarīre tattvasaṃyutam kṣetrajñaścarate tatra sthānāṣṭakagatisthitaḥ tenedaṃ devadeveśa kṣetrāṣṭakamudāhṛtam kumārikākhaṇḍaḥye pīṭhāste ca vai kṣetrā kṣetrā pīṭhā udāhṛtā nāmaparyāya vai teṣā śāstre śāstre pṛthak pṛthak prayāga nābhideśe tu varuṇā hṛdi saṃsthitā kaullagirya tu vai kaṇṭhe bhīmanādaṃ tu tāluke bindusthāne jayantyākhya nādākhye tu caritrakam ekā śaktimadhye tu jñātavyaṃ viditātmabhiḥ guruvakāgataṃ prokta koṭivarṣa tathāṣṭamam ete sthānā mayā proktā aṭane paunale sthitāḥ samākhyāya yajed deva tribhirbhedairanukramāt khyātaṃ mūrdhni stutikhaṇḍaṃ mātṛkhaṇḍa hṛdi yajet mantrakhaṇḍa tu vai guhye yajed deva maheśvara etat kramopadeśa tu bhuktimuktiphalapradam na syādataḥ paraṃ kiñcidityetat paramārthataḥ ye kecit śāstrasaṃghātā pāramparyakramāgatāḥ asya śāstrasya deveśi kalā nāhanti ṣoḍaśīm kramaugha ṣaṭvidha jñātvā dehasthaṃ pūjayet sadā maṇḍalasthaṃ tathā pūjya yathāvihitatatkramāt ityādyāvatāre mahāmanthānabhairavayajñe anvaye saptakoṭipramāṇe śrīkramasūtrādhikāra  ekapañcāśānandaḥsiddhānte pañca sāraṃ catuṣka vāmagocare dakṣiṇe trikamityāhu  pūrvānāpaścimolikramāmnāyeṃ gurureva kulānvayeṃ m ṣaḍantaṃ saptamānta ca rudrasya cāṣṭamolikam vyāpakasyādimaṃ deva tṛtīyaṃ ca caturthakam dvitīyaṃ cañcalādya ca nādākhya sūkṣmapañcakam navātmānandayogīndra śāsane vṛkṣanāyakam ciñcānātha tribhedastha ekāśītipadairyutam kalābhiḥ ṣoḍaśairdīptaṃ bhinnaṃ siddhestu ṣoḍaśai anulomavilomena pañcapraṇavadīpitam vidyātritayamāviṣṭa padavidyāsamāyutam sandhyātrayānvitaṃ śvetaṃ ārakta kṛṣṇapiṅgalam brahmasūtradhara deva mekhalānūpurānvitam pañcārūḍha bindumadhye caryaikādaśakānvitam nṛtyadvādaśasaṃyukta vādyadvādaśasaṃyutam vidyāvratadhara vīra sūtradvādaśagocaram navadhājñādhara śrīmān śāsane tu kramādhipam kumārikākhaṇḍaḥdaśasaptakalāntastha hrasvadīrghavibheditam  gurupaktitraye nātha ādināthaṃ trayoliṣu tena sārdhaṃ krama pūjya yo jānāti sa deśika   anyathā naiva jānāti saṃbhāṣa naiva kārayet caryākramasya deveśa bhojanaṃ śayanaṃ tathā guruvaktre tu samaya na tena saha kārayet ādināthakrama yastu gurumaṇḍalaka kramam yo vijānāti tattvena sa bhavet kulanandanaḥ tridhā jyeṣṭha namaskuryāt kaṇṭhe bāla samāśrayet hṛdaye dhātara kuryāt gotrajaistu karadvayam anyathā ācared yastu prayaścittī bhaved dhruvam lakṣajāpād viśuddhātmā gotramadhye punarbhavet vṛkṣanāthasya  sūtreda pāramparyakramāgatam candradvīpād viniṣkrānta gumnāyasya nirṇayam kumārikākhaṇḍakāmarūpa haṣkaḍḍokaṃ nepāla puṇḍravardhanam purastīra kanyākubja pūrṇagirya tathārbudam āmrākeraikā trio kāmakoṭṭikam kailāsa bhṛgunagara kedāra candrapūryakam śrīpīṭha caiva ekoṇa jālandhara ca mālavam kulūta devikoṭṭaṃ ca gokarṇa marukeśaram aṭṭahāsaṃ ca viraja rājaveśma mahāpatham kollagirya kollāpura sopāra tu jayantikā ujjayinyā caritraṃ ca kṣīrikā hastināpuram udakeśa prayāgākhyaṃ pīṭhaṃ māyāpurī tathā urasā malayaṃ caiva śaila bheruṇḍaka tathā mahendra varuṇā caiva hiraṇyapurameva ca mahālakṣmī tathodyāna cchāyācchatramataḥ param ete pīṭhā samākhyātā  pañcāśat parikīrtitāḥ sṛṣṭinyāyena saṃjātā vāmāvartaparibhramāt  vāmādinavaśaktīnā madhye traikūṭamaṇḍale udayaṃ svaravarṇānā ukta pīṭhavigraham mudrāmaṇḍalamadhye tu māyayā gahanīkṛtam svaravarṇavibhāga tu meruśrīgahvarakramam ādyaprastāramākhyātaṃ santāne siddhaśāsane adha  kālāgnirudraṃ tu tadūdhve tu trayodaśadaṇḍayañca samākhyātā bhagādyā ūdhvagāvadhi  kumārikākhaṇḍapurodhvaikādaśa rudrā santāne adhikāriṇa navasiddhāstadū dhve tu purodhve sapta yoginya  evaṃ maṇḍala ūdhve tu akhaṇḍādya krameṇa tu śaktitrayaṃ tadūdhve tu tatrodhve nāthaciñciṇī kālāgnyādi hi nāthāntamukta vai gahvara kramam gahvaranyāsanirmukta siddhasantānavarjitam na pūjyaṃ paścimācāryairityukta kādibheda iti gahvarakramam iti śrīkādibhede pañcāśatpīṭhameruprastārasūtra  dvipañcāśānandaḥnavadhākalitaṃ nāthaṃ pūjanīyaṃ pṛthak pṛthak kulanāthamanantākhya kandarpaṃ vimalastathā advaita tūṣṇamāna samayaṃ śiraśekharam śāmbhavājñāvara devaṃ navama parikīrtitam navanāthaivātmā navamūrtidharaṃ bhavet iti kādibhede śrīcaturviṃśatisāha ādināthasūtram śrīvakrā uvācatripañcāśānandaḥsūtrasantānaka prajña gūḍhārthena bravīmyaham santāna dvitīya puṣpa meruvijñānabhairavam nādiphanta smṛtaṃ mārga anvaye devatāḥ ṣaḍiḥ nirgata dvādaśa ratna khamapuṣpadvayena  tu saṃvartamaṇḍalodyāna śūnyaṃ guhād vinirgatam mi  osiddha tatra guhātūṣṇīsamādhiṣu pratyayājñā bhavet tatra vṛkṣa caiva kadambakam siṃhavat tiṣṭhate vidyā śāpānugrahasiṃhakā kuṭilājñā adhomārgeṣaṭprakāra gṛhaṃ śāktasaptāviṃśatibhirbhedairbheda manthānabhairavam śivaśaktisamācāra advaitāmaragotrakam  vakrikenugrahālayegṛhaṃ candrapurodayam kumārikākhaṇḍaḥsiddhā śuṣkā mahācchāyā trikūṭe cāpare pade kalpanākalpita yat tu paścimāmnāyakalpitam ūdhvaśaktiradhaḥ śaktirāma kalpana viduḥ sā ca haṃsaśca mālinī pratyaya bījasaṃgamam trayaḥ siddhāḥ koṇāyā anuṣṭhānādhikārakāḥ cittavṛttiparityāgādadhikāra tu kaṇe divyā saptaśilā śuddhā janmani nāmarūpikā brahmā tu kaulikāmnāya vāsanā śuddhacetasā dvandvatyāgāt prasādastu janmabrahmaśilā śubhā yatra yatra vrajedicchā samādhisthe  varānana sthitiryogasamāyoga sthitirvai kāmarūpake bhagamadhye mana kṛtvā kīrtayamānā samāviśet cittāhlāda manastuṣṭi kīrtiściñciṇivṛkṣake kumārikākhaṇḍasiddhaṃ yasya mahārthaṃ tu ṣaṭprakāramahārṇavam bhrāntijñānaparityāgāt siddhicaiva tu sāgare tasya tuṣṭā hyaha deva yo jānāti kulakramam prajñāsūtramida jñātvā ko na mucyeta bandhanāt unmanādikrameṇaiva  yāvat śrīnāthaciciṇī  punarnavakrame nātha siddhistu gahvare krame iti śrīkādibhede caturviṃśatisāhasre pañcāśadbhedabhinnaṃ santānasūtrādhikāram  śrīvakrā uvācacatuḥpañcāśānandaḥvāgbhavaṃ praṇava nāma himakundendunirmalam sphuratpāvakasaṃkāśaṃ yonau madhye vicintayet kāmarūpaṃ mahāpīṭhaṃ ādau kṛtayuge sthitam lakṣajāpāt pratyayājñā śarīre kṣobhamāviśet dvitīyaṃ praṇavaṃ caiva pīṭhe jālandhare hara bālārkamuditaṃ dhyātvā siddhagandharvasevitam niśācāre caikavṛkṣe japellakṣamatha dvayam pāśastobha karotyāśu devīnāṃ melaka mahat vīrasiddhimavāpnoti parapurapraveśanam ityānanda mahābījaṃ praṇavaṃ ca tṛtīyakam pītarūpa mahākānta nābhimadhye vyavasthitam pūrṇāgiryā mahāpīṭhaṃ sasurāsuravanditam lakṣatritayajāpena niśācāre catuḥpathe ghūrmipratyayavijñāna vartate sādhakasya tu purakṣobha na saṃdeho nirvikalpasya siddhyati kumārikākhaṇḍabhinnāñjananibha raudra kaṇṭhamadhye vicintayet tisrapīṭhe bhaviṣye tu kalerante bhaviṣyati śūnyadevakule rātrau japellakṣacatuṣṭayam nityānanda sadā śiṣye adṛṣyatva prajāyate dravyākarṣaṇasiddhiśca vaśyāveśamanuttamam eṣa bhairavarāja tu raktālaktakasannibham bhrūmadhye tu vijānīyāt pīṭhodyāna prakalpayet svayambhūliṅgapūrvato niśācareṇa pañcabhiḥ japairlakṣairyoganidrāpratyayaṃ  jāyate tataḥ atītānāgataṃ caiva vartamāne pravartate pañcapraṇava  uccārāt lakṣamekaṃ japed yadi śūnyadevagṛhe rātrau aṇimādiguṇāṣṭakam evaṃ te praṇavā pañca prathamaṃ śrīkujānvaye mantrāgrenukrameṇaiva ante tepi vilomataḥ amāvāsyā bhavet pūrṇa kalikāle tu muktidā iti śrīcaturviṃśatisāhasre pañcapraṇavasūtram śrīvakrā uvācapañcapañcāśānandaḥantarikṣ parānande unmane vyomapañcake parā devī parādehe śuddhanirvāṇamaṇḍale pañca vyomāni jātāni parā devī jagāntare binducakre viśuddhākhye hṛdaye yonimaṇḍale kandādhāre kramāt teṣāṃ pañcake vyomanāyaka vyomacakrasya madhye ta sthitā sā vyomapañca tuevaṃ vyomāni jātāni parā devī kṛte yuge sthānasaṃketakaṃ jñātvā jyeṣṭhoṃ bhrātā tadā bhavet athavā pitṛdaivatya bhavate vā pitāmahaḥ prapitāmaheti saṃjño vai vṛddho vai yādṛśo bhavet teṣāṃ maṇḍalakaṃ kṛtvā sāṣṭāṅgena namaskaret na rikta maṇḍalaṃ kuryād yadīcchet siddhimātmani cintābhāvena ātmāna vinivedya prasannadhīḥ tatrāpi maṇḍalaṃ kuryāt kūrmāsanasamanvitam dakṣiṇe vīradravyaṃ tu dakṣiṇā madhyamottare tucatuṣkaṃ kārayet śreṣṭha susūtraṃ ca suśobhanam kumārikākhaṇḍapātraṃ pūrva samāsādya sarvalakṣaṇasaṃyutam kambugrīvocchrita svarṇa bālabālukavarjitam vāmahastayutenāpi madhye śrīnāthapādukā vāgbhavena prakartavyaṃ vṛkṣatritayamuttare ciciṇī pūrvato jñeyā dvitīyaṃ ca kadambakam tṛtīyaṃ bilvamityāhuvīgbhavena samanvitam mātarīṣaṭkamagre ca ḍakārādi vidhānavat krameṇānena ṣaṭka syāt bījaṃ tāsā ca ṣaḍvidham svayonimiśrita kṛtvā vāgbhavena vibhūṣitam ambāpādānta sarveṣāṃ svasthāne olināthakam tasmin sthāne guroḥ paṃkti sṛṣṭinyāyena sundara vāgbhavādi tataḥ pañca ūdhvakoṇādi āruhet madhyasthāne tataḥ kṛtvā diśāsu vidiśāsu ca jyeṣṭhamaṇḍalamityukta gurūṇāṃ siddhihetave evavidhivihīnastu ārādhya yo na manyate yoginyastasya sīdanti bhakṣayanti vasāmiṣam kumārikākhaṇḍaihetyarthaparibhraṣṭaḥ paratra siddhyate kutaḥ tasmāt sarvaprayatnena jyeṣṭhānāmabhinandanam vratīnā ca yatīnāṃ ca yogīndrāṇāṃ viśeṣataḥ puruṣāṇāṃ striyāṇā vā ācāryāṇāṃ gurojñayā ye jātā  koṃkaṇe pūrve ye sthitā jarayanti ca  teṣā maṇḍalakaṃ kuryād dravyahīnamasiddhidam na kuryāt putrakānāṃ tu samayācāramelake iti śrīkādibhede ārādhyamaṇḍalavidhānasūtra viśvākarṣaṇayogena samyak sarvaṃ nirāmayam svānandaṃ svasvarūpaṃ ca śrīcandrapūryeti saṃjñayā anāhatasamutthānaṃ śūnyaṃ śūnyālayaṃ vrajet nirāśrayaṃ paraṃ bhittvā śrīgulmanātha dvitīyakam nijapadasamudbhūta candrasyārdhanirodhitam svakramodayavijñānaṃ śrīstambhadeva tṛtīyakam ṣaṭpañcāśānandaḥtrikoṇacakrasalīna ekanāḍyā samutthitam dvādaśārkasamaprakhyaṃ śrīkapīsākhya caturthakam ghaṇṭikāntarasaṃlīna drava vahnimaṇḍale ciccakra  sarvasusthāna śrīmapuraṃ bhavet bhedadvayaṃ gatosau vai dvādaśānte layaṃ gataḥhṛdvyomobhayamadhye tu virajaṃ deva ṣaṣṭhakam kulapañcakamudrāyā vyomavaktraṃ tu dīpayet bindusthānaṃ tu sabhittvā śrīprayāgaṃtu saptamam  mahāpralayanirghoṣaṃ vyomavako tucālayet dīpyamānaṃ tu sarveṣāṃ śrīkāṃsākhyaṃ tathāṣṭamam kumārikākhaṇḍaḥmahāvyomni pratiṣṭhosau viṣṇuliṅgāṅgadhāriṇaḥ mahāvajrapade līno bhogadeveti saṃjñayā khasthāne tu pare prāpte vahnau sūrye layaṃ gate tatra ājñā bhavet tasya bimbadeva dvipañcakam avarṇarasamākṛṣya śūnya vyomaṃ samāśrayet mahānāde praviṣṭosau śrīkhaḍgadevaṃ tu siddhyati tiraskāra tiraskṛtvā lokasya vañcanam bhavet manonirodhana kṛtvā dvādaśa rudrameva ca rasānande prabuddhātmā brahmatattve layaṃ gataḥ nirvāṇapadasaṃprāptā dhārā śiveti saṃjñayā mahānāde praviṣṭosau avasthāśāmbhave sthitaḥ ekākārasvarūpeṇa śrīmudrāsphoṭaścaturdaśaḥ  jyotirūpastathā nāda ekībhāvaṃ gatāvubhau paravyoma prabuddhasya śrīvaṃkāpurasaṃjñayā mahāśūnyālaya gatvā samarasatvena sasthitaḥ prabuddhastiṣṭhate tatra bhurjadeveti ṣoḍaśaḥiti ṣoḍaśasiddhānā sūtram śrīvakrā uvācasaptapañcāśānandaaṣṭādaśakramāmnāya bhūmikārthena kathyate khacakre kulajānanda khasukha khapracoditam khasthā nivartitākārā tasmāt  sā unmanā parā unmanākhyāmanākhyā  ca anāśrayapadotthitā nistaraṅgā nirābhāsā mokṣalakṣmī maheśvara sarvī sarveśvarī sūkṣmā nistattvā saṃvṛtālayā ālaya  sṛṣṭivargasya unmanāha nirāmayā mahatī sarvamantrajñā mātaṅgī cāntyaje kule manamekāgrataḥ kṛtvā dvādaśārcisamākulā mālinī meghanādena pārayet parakaulike manonmanapade jñeyā aṭate sā aśaṅkitā ṣoḍaśānte cidākāśe vikāse guptamaṇḍale kumārikākhaṇḍaḥtatrasthā yā purā bhāti ānandabodharaśmibhiḥ samaneti kalā sūkṣmā śāśvatā bodhavigrahā samanānte vijānīyāt śāmbhavājñā svarūpataḥ tattvahīnā avicchinnā ciddhanābharaṇodadhiḥ ūdhvasthā kulanāthaṃ ca vyāpayantī svayambhuvā tena sā vyāpinī proktā paradehād vinirgatā śodhanī śivatattvasya antaḥkaraṇayojanī yajñakoṭisuvistīrṇa nityānandā maheśvara antyajā maṇḍale kṣīṇā avyaktā paramāvyayā tasyotpattilaya nāsti saṃcareta mahāpathe nistaraṅge nabhe vyāptirnandinyā kulakaulinī saptakoṭistu mantrāṇāṃ prastāre ye ca bhāṣitāḥ  merumadhyād viniṣkrāntā mantratva saptadhā bhavet manthāna śivaśaktyādau ubhābhyāṃ ravisomayoḥ tryakṣaraṃ ta mahātmāna manthāna saptadhā bhavet kumārikākhaṇḍaḥṣatyāgāt saptame muktirnirdhūmā nirmalā dyutiḥ sā yoni paramākāśe tryākhyā caiva paścime helayā krīḍakāraṇe saṃsparśe ca anukramāt divyaratnakujāmbikā ālaye sarvasiddhānā trikūṭe paścime gṛhe kumārikākhaṇḍagṛhameka purārabhya kālakarṣī ca devā himavantagṛhe jātā saṃvatī paścime gatā gatasya punarāvṛtiricchārūpā maheśvarī siddhirbhāvakā abhāvajñānakhaḍgoya triśūnyādhārakandaram hanti kalirikruddha cchedayet pāparāśikam abhāvavimale dīpepaśyate jñānacakṣuṣā tamamāyātmamūrkatvapaśupāśavimocanam yad gṛhītaṃ svabhāvena khañjīnāthāvalīpūrṇa triśūnyānte layodayam trivallīvalayākāra trikaika ṣoḍaśādhikam tribhireko bhavet śrīmān  tri ulyākramanirṇayam aṣṭādaśaprakāreṇaabhāva khamahānanda divyaughamatanirṇayam kumārikākhaṇḍaḥsvabhāvodayakāraṇam abhāvagirimeruṃ ca durgandaravartinam līlayā kramate siddhaḥ krama divyaughabhāvanāt svabhāvasaṃbhava jñāna sarvagaṃ śāśvatamajam paktikrameṇa divyena guṇātītaṃ nirañjanam prāpya siddhiṃ khamārgeṇatriśuddhikramamārgeṇa ko na mucyati bandhanāt acirācca gurojñayā bandhamokṣakarī vakrā sālambāprasarobhayamadhyasthā devadevī parāparā ca nirāśrayāāmūlāt prasara tasyāḥ kramavṛkṣasamāśritāmūlamājñākrama vṛkṣaṃ triśākhaṃ nābhisaṃbhavam vartijñānāṃkurācchannaṃ abhimātrālatāvṛtam cchāyābinduvicitrāḍhya patrendukarabhūṣitam puṣpamekamanaṅgākhya gandhaṃ jyotiścidātmakamphalānandara ājñā tṛptiḥ kālasya vañcanam āhlādakaraṇa yogaṃ mokṣājñāsiddhisāgaram tadgata conmanāvastha suṣuptigatacetasam sarvabhāvaparikṣīṇaṃ paśyate jñānacakṣuṣā kumārikākhaṇḍasabāhyābhyantaraikatve adhodhve kandarandhragā nirānande samutpanne muktirdivyaughaśāsane sahajayogodbhava kaula kulapiṇḍaṃ tridhātmakam ekastrīṇi tathā pañca ṣaṭ trika kramanirṇayam sā vakrātu pragīyate vikāsānandasaṃyogāt sā vikāsaratā sadā paramāmṛtanirvāṇaṃ śāmbhavī jñānabhūmikā bhūmikā bhuvanāntasya unmanādikramasya ca tanmayājñāprabhāveṇa divyaughakulanirgatam sāmarasyapada divyāśramāmanaskākhya kalāśeṣākṣara  param tanmadhye mahadākāśa  ṣoḍaśasvarabhūṣitam visargahṛdayāntasthā sā śakti padmagarbhagā karṇikānāyakī sā ca sa liṅga śivātmakam amṛta sarvayogīnā kubjīśa bindubhairavam bhairavaṃ bindunādākhya trivalīdarasannibham tatra madhye bhagāhlāda mahāhlāda bhagodbhavam udbhava kaulika yoga liṅgodhāṇa ca devatākumārikākhaṇḍasvayambhū mātṛpakṣasya sabāhyābhyantarasthitam bāhyastha ca svadehastha  bhedaiḥ ṣoḍaśa  bheditam ṣoḍhāśaktiḥ parā khyātā viśuddhi  kāmarūpake ṣaṭkamadhye kramapadaṃ utkaṭa mātṛbhairavam mudrākūṭamiti khyāta kūṭaika mudrakūṭakam mudrākūṭa parasthāna taccākāśaṃ padottamam dakṣiṇakoṇasaṃsthāne kṣetranāthāmbarīśakam kalāṃ candrasya sūryasya vikāsvarā vicintayet karaṇa kṣetraliṅgasya vidyā ca mahantārikā bhagaliṅga ḍāmarīmūrtistadā kṣobhobhijāyate mālinī mahatī vāmā anāmākṣarapaṃktyayoḥ traiguṇyākṣaravinyāsairbindvakṣaraparākalā nirakṣarā parā māyā durvijñā trivalīkṛtā trividhākṣarabhedena sā ca devī kumārikā nistaraṅgaśivecchayā parajñānaprabhāveṇa anvayaṃ ṣaḍvidhaṃ bhavet oṃkārakulamānanda uḍḍiyānāmaragolakam śuddhasphaṭikabhāsaṃ ca mātṛbhairavaśekharam śaśimadhyāntarāvalī trivallī cāṣṭadhā kalā mūlāṃbjagolakopari kumārikākhaṇḍatasya bhedastridhā śaktirbhūteṣu devi sasthitā vilīnā sarvabhedānāṃ kramaṃ tasyā ca ṣaḍvidham vikāsaḥ paścimāmnāye nirāśīkṛtavigra kūṭaṃ pīṭhā kūṭa śakti kūṭa siddhāḥ parāparāḥ mathanāt kulavṛkṣasya tadā mūlobhijāyate ānandaḥ piṅgalo hyātmā eko hyekaprakāśakaḥ maṇḍalasthamabhedyatvāt tadā vindyācchiva jagat jagadvidyā mahāmātṛ samayavratacāriṇī mudrāśakti  paraṃ tattvaṃ kṣobhaṇāt paścimamaṃ gṛham gṛhamekārṇavā yoni sā cāṣṭādaśabhedataḥ samudrajñānakallolaṃ kallola bhairavāmṛtam nābhikośa mahāratnaṃ prasuptaṃ yadi bhāvitam aākrāntaṃ pūrvakaraṇaistadā pūrṇaśilā bhavet ekā nāḍī parā māyā trikoṇakūṭabhūṣitā saptāviṃśatibhi kūṭaijayate śuddhavāsanā tripuraṃ tat tadā ṣaṭkaṃ saptamātarabhedataḥ dakṣiṇasthaṃ vibhāvyeta tadā mantropadeśakam ahipūrṇā tadā kālī rudradehāt samudbhavā avasthā ṣaḍguṇā yasmāt tasmālliṅgodbhavānalam kūṭaikadamanā śakti  bindumaṇḍalamaṇḍitā kīrtidevaḥ kaṣākhyaśca tadā kandarpabhairavam śilāśekharapūryastha ṭaṃkaṭaśataśobhitam niḥspandagatiruddhāṃ tu tadā jñānopajīvanam saṃsāradamanākhyā tu pañcapīṭhāntanāyakīprasūtivyāpinī śāntā guṇabhedakramādapi saṃvatīṃ triguṇīkṛtvā madhyasthā ca manonmanā ājñācatuṣkabhedena bhūṣitaṃ śaśimaṇḍalam ekānekavibhedena ākāśaṃ pañcadhāgatam śikhāśivaikabhāvena paripūrṇanabhodyutiḥ pañcāśītyātmako hyātmā triguṇāvalibhūṣitaḥ kumārikākhaṇḍaārṇavaṃ saṃyatātmā vai sadā tejasamādyutiḥ mālinyaṣṭaparivṛtaḥ manovākkāyakarmasyaparakāyapraveśena bodhisattvaparāgatiḥ gatirāgatibhedatvād  yā nāḍī sūkṣmavāhinī saptaskandhaparityāgād bījāṃkura prapadyate mātṛmaṇḍale tadā bhedaḥ svamantrasya svakāyadamanādapi pīṭhe pīṭhādhikārasya sūkṣmā adhyātmikā kriyā bindusthā ghūrmaṇī nāma anāmā hyapi cinmayīṃ buddhitattve parākāśe kubjikā rudradevatā dakṣāvartaparākāśe  aparārkaviśodhana kumārikākhaṇḍanirodhasthānamādāya śavarī jñānadevatā rudrajñānaprabhāvyāptiḥ śaktirādyā svayaṃbhuvā koṃkaṇā vāmadevatā saṃpūrṇaśaśimadhyasthāvāmadakṣiṇasaṃyogāt sā bhāti śāṃkarī kalā udbhavānandarūpeṇa maṅgalā nāma ciñciṇīṃ catuḥ kīrtiparityāgāt caturmātrākṣarāṇi ca viparītākriyāśaktimataṅgī trisvarūpataḥ udānapreritā śaktiḥ kuṇḍalī yakṣarodbhavā anāmākṣarayogena koṃkaṇā koṃkaṇe gṛhe gṛhaṣaṭke ṣaḍi pīṭhā divyaśaktiprabhāvata sabāhyābhyantaraikatve yukterasyopadeśikā divyaughamida pīṭhānā pīṭhogha kulaṣaḍvidham guruvaktraṃ parāśakti jñātvā pīṭhān samarcayet siddhaughamapara teṣāṃ svādhikāraṃ tu ṣaḍvidham kumārikākhaṇḍaḥughajñānaprabhāvyāpti jñātvā siddhānvayaṃ bhavet śrīsamudrataṭāntastha kaulīśa khāmalambaram sa coḍḍīśo mahāsiddho bhagānā svādhikāraka kulaparvatarājasya vahnervai tat vibodhanam khamantro jñānacaryā ca jālākhye caryabhairavam bharitānandamadhyastha taruṇāruṇapīṭhajam śaśāṃkena dhṛtānanda pūrṇasthaṃ ṣaṣṭhabhairavam bhuvanāvalimadhyastha māyayā saṃpuṭīkṛtam devyā ājñāprabhāveṇa avasthānandabhairavam samudraśailamadhyasthā mahājñānaparivṛtā madanonmattamātaṅgī mātaṅgī śaktiravyayā kumārikākhaṇḍavimalajñānamadhyasthaṃ koṅkaṇa ca kriyātmakam bharaṇādapi cittasya vimalā śakti  koṃkaṇā ṣaṭ siddhā pīṭhaṣaṭkaṃ ca pīṭhadevyotha bhairavāḥ bhairavājñāprasādena ekasthānodayātmakā siddhakramavicāroya oghajñānakramodayam ṣaḍvidhārthaprayogena ciñciṇīnātha  ṣaḍvidham khamadhyasthaṃ khakāraika khatrikaṃ khaparāparam vijñānaniratoḍīśa vāyunākāśapūritam pūrvākṣarakṣakāreṇa trimātrapadapūrakam caryākāśāmṛtavyāptiḥ caryā ciñciṇicetanam ūdhvādhomadhya prāṇa ghaṭodaravighaṭṭinam ghaṇṭikāparvata ṣaṣṭhoṃ hṛtpadme tu vikāsakaḥ amṛtamṛtayormadhye yā mitrāmitrakalpanāvikalpakṣīṇacittasya siddhākhyā madanodbhavā kumārikākhaṇḍaḥmattamātaṅgagāmadhye madanoṃ jīvanāṃśakaḥ varṇagrāmaprabhedena yā vyāptistanmadāṅgagā vilomād nirmalānandaḥ kamalastha hutāśanam vilīna ṣaṭpadāntastha vimala kūṭapuṭam ṣaṭsthānanirato yogī svādhikāramanāmṛtam ṣaḍyogabharitātmāna ṣaṭsiddhānvayapīṭheṣu siddhaṃ siddhakramācāra siṃhakasiṃhikobhayoḥ mathanādapi cakrasya tadā jñānaṃ ca ṣaḍvidham ṣaḍvidhaṃ karaṇopāya ṣaḍvadhaṃ kulanirṇayam ṣaḍvidhārthaprayogātmā ṣaṭpīṭhamupacaryate caryācaraṇakartṛtva kartṛtva paramātmanaḥ bahirbhāvagatātmānaṃ tadātmāna ca ṣaḍvidham ṣaḍiṣaṭka parā cchāyā ṣaḍiṣaṭka parā kalā vimala kamalonanta kamalonantaḥkamalāmṛtasaṃgrahaḥ sarvopa aikāramiti ṣaḍvidham siddhānandavikāsajñaḥ bhuvanabhūtikuṇḍalam kuṇḍalī ca kapālaṃ ca virāmaṃ ca kapālakam vibhavānandakailāsa kailāsamupadeśakam kūṭāntastha ca kailāsa caturbheda kramādapi kumārikākhaṇḍatrimātrabinducakrastha tricakraṃ ca parāparam na doṣo vidyate yasmāt pīṭhānā siddhabhairavam tadā caikā parā vyāptivyāpaka parama śivaḥ tadā candrodayaugha  tu sūryasyātmani saṃsthitam candrasūryanipātena candrikā ca vijāyatecāndrakaraṇakartṛtve svakārye karaṇādapi indriyajñānabodhena tadā śambhūpadeśakam evaṃ taccandrapuryasya puraprakāraraśmayaḥ vikāsajñānamāṇikyabharaṇāccandrapuryakamsa caiva prakṛtānanda kāra kalanātmanihakṣasthā paramā kāntirjagasyāpyāyakārikā āpyāyayaṃ parameśasyaardhacandrakalā kācid akāra surasattamatayā jīva pravardheta koṃkaṇe kāmarūpake  śivasya kulajīvanam vṛkṣatrayaprabhedatvājjīvākhya labhate naraḥ evaṃ jīvaparāśakti prāṇāpānādipañcake kumārikākhaṇḍaḥprāṇasya ca apānasya samāna jāyate padam samānamayacandrasya siddhi prāpnoti kaulikīm ākāśa paramaṃ tiṣṭhet suśāntamupadeśakam ūkāraśca ukāraśca cakāraśca tṛtīyakaḥ ardhacandrakalājyotsnā  ekībhūtaḥ paraḥ śivaḥ ra iva ukāraśca ṛ ṝ riva ṝ vantarā ḷkāraśca lukāraśca hakāraścāntamakṣayam ūkārasvaramekatra uradvayapuṭīkṛtam candronmīlananādākhyaṃ akārasvararañjitam ārubharitarūpeṇa kukudvayapuṭīkṛtam apuṭa puṭaṃ kṛtvā udayāstamanāvubhau puṭaikakaraṇo rāri virāvi  kalpasaṃjñayā  rā rirarirānanda rā rivarṇastu ṣaḍvidhaḥ tadā śaktyudbhavānanda vaiṣṇavākhyaṃ tribhedataḥ cicchaktipreraṇād haṃso haṃsodarakulakramam kulaṃ kaulakalāntaṃ tu vikāla  kalanātmakaḥ kalanāt kālikā kālī kālakaṃkālakaulikī udayeta kule kāla kālojjhitamanākulam kaulīśa kulamadhyasthaṃ kaulīśaṃ kulavācakamkapālaṃ kalābhiryukta tadā kākīmukhā kalākālikākulasiṃhastha kālikāśaktyalaṃkṛtaḥ kṛtakṛtyavibhedena kālikākramapaddhatiḥ saṃkocaśca vikāsaśca prakāśaḥ paramātmanaḥ ullāsacinmayajyotirniṣkrāntamiti golakam kumārikākhaṇḍaḥkākākāro makāraśca kukārākṣaraḍambaram āḍambara gaṇeśaśca gagana ca hakārarāṭ āṭaśca maṭahaścaiva  īṭapati anādimam antasthaṃ bhavanākāśaṃ   ṭakāraścaṭhakārayoḥ tadā sā śāvarīśakti śaśāṃkakṛtaśekharā mahācinmātrarūpeṇa mahākālī prakāśikāudayaśca kaṭāhaśca haṭamadhyaśca vāṭayoḥ kaṭahavikhyaṭopa  virāma koṃkaṇaṃ gṛham āḍharūpaka māṭaṃ ca paṭalaṃ paṭalāmṛtam atrāmṛtataraṅgasya  ahicchatraṃ parāmṛtam avatārodayaṃ īśaṃ īśaśca mitiṣobhayoḥ cikopāṭayamūlaśca amṛtaścandrapuryakam candracāndrī parā chāyā candra candrārdhaśekharam ardhaśekhara nāda śilāśekharasaṃjñayāravicandrakalāśeṣa ṣoḍaśasvaramaṇḍalam nirmalagatimārūḍhā parā saptādaśī kalāja ṣatyāgāt saptamaṃ sthānaṃ viśrāma cāṣṭamaṃ layam ālayaṃ paramānanda akāraakāra śivacinmayaḥ kumārikākhaṇḍaḥtadā kālakṣayā śakti amāvāsyā tathāmbikāhaṃsasthānanirodhena haṃsākhyā paramā kalā  haṃsādihasamadhyasthā haṃsinī nāma devatā parāparavibhāgena padānāṃ śivabodhakī merumadhyagaṃta prāṇa prāṇamadhyagataḥ śaśiḥśaśiḥ śaśeścāntargato bhānurmeruśaktivisargayoḥ visargadvayamadhyasthaṃ visargamudayātmakam ekastha ca visargasthaṃ ekāneka visargayoḥ visargātītanādākhyaṃ ninādapadarūpadhṛk tripadaḥ ṣaṭpadavyāpī tadā kṣubhyati koṃkaṇe koṃkaṇaṃ kamalasthaṃ tu  kamalādapi koṃkaṇam koṃkaṇa  śaśinādākhyaṃ nādākhyaṃ koṃkaṇaṃ śivam śivamadhye śivo bindurbindumadhye śivaṃ ca vihaṅga prāṇaśaktigaḥ kumārikākhaṇḍaśaktimadhyagatastūṣṇī tūṣṇīmadhye kadambakam kadambānte bhaved bilva bilvānte cittaciñciṇīciñciṇī paramā śaktirbhagasthā tu bhagātmani antaḥstha  mahimānanda mahimājñā kulakrameṃmahimā ca parā śakti mahimā ca anāmikā mananā ca manādyā ca anantā sā anāmikāanāmāntargatā jyeṣṭhā sā ca bhinnakaloditā svapakṣajñānakatīra  pakṣāpakṣavibhedaka parānandaṃ ānandaṃ bhairavātmakam tryakṣaraṃ tripathātīta  tryakṣaraṃ ca tridhāgatam kṣara sarvamaśeṣasya śṛṅgāṭākṣaramelakam kailāse  meruśṛṅgasya meruśṛṅgāṭabhairava   manthānabhairave yajñe anvaye kriyāyoga samāsena pañcaratnāni pañcasu brahmā viṣṇustathā rudra īśvara sadāśivaḥ  śivakaraṇa caikatra cirāyurbhavate tadā pañcaitāni kalāyuktyā pañcaratnānvitāni ca pañcamudrāprayogeṇa kāraṇaṃ ratnapañcakam ratnaika ratnamadhyasthaṃ ratnodarapuṭīkṛtam ratlikāratnamāsādya ratnavajjāyate manaḥ manorana samaikatve sthiraprakṛtibuddhimān tadā ratnoditāmnāya jñeyavṛttiḥ prajāyate tu vikalpastvamane sthitaḥ vikalpasya kṣayaṃ kṛtvā tadā siddhirna saṃśayaḥ cāndrayogamaśeṣātmā prakṛtiḥ svātmapañjaram guṇatrayanirodhena dṛśyate candravat padam cāndracārakṣaya lakṣa ravilakṣa ākāśaṃ vimalānanda samudrādabhiṣecana vibhavānandayogena tadā mukto digambaraḥ bharaṇādapi ratnasya virajasya abhedanam yāvaccotpadyatevasthā sā cājñā ratnapañcakam nirāśīkṛtacittasya nirodhakaraṇāmbhasā jñātvā ratnopadeśaṃ tu ratnājñā siddhyate dhruvam ratnaika ratnamadhyasthaṃ ratnodarapuṭīkṛtam ratnākṣaraṃ tu kaulīśa kaulika ratnapañcakam evamādyāvatāraṃ tu śrīmaccandrapuroddhṛtam ādyaṃ tava mayā prokta pañcaratnaṃ rasāyaṇam ratnodaraparānanda  vikāsa caiva cinmayam manoratnakalāḍhyaṃ ca ratnameka parāparam kumārikākhaṇḍaguhāntastha mahāratnaṃ eka ṣoḍaśadhā sthitamṣoḍaśākṣarabhedatvād  aiṃkāraṃ ratnamakṣayam ṣoḍaśabhiśca saṃtiṣṭhed bhavabhedaṃ manottaram yonyārṇavaṃ ca aiṃkāra īkārākṣarabhūṣitam kaliyuge sthitāḥ sārdhaṃ kumudasthasutejasa a ā i ratnodayeṣu ca aḥkāra pañcamo hyete pañcaratnapradīpakāḥ candrapūryakramāyātāḥ pañcaite pañcaviṃśatiḥuddhṛtā daśabhirbhedaijñatvā parapadaṃ labhet sāṭaka paṭakañcaiva sāvaka paṭahastathā ṭaṭahaḥ maṇiratnakam maṇiralosya ratnasya ratnasya maṇibandhakammaṇiratnaprayogena ratnayogamudāhṛtam ratnasya tu vicitrasya maṇiratnaprakāśaka viparītakramādeva maṇiratnaṃ ca kāñcanam kāñcanaṃ ca hiraṇyasya hiraṇyaṃ brahmabījakam brahmanāḍīvibhedena brahmajīvopadeśakam upadeśopavargasya virajasya ca golakam brahmāṃśakaviśuddhena brahmavedhaṃ sadoditamsadoditacidā bhāti unmattabrahmacaryakam brahmacarya ca vimala vratametacca pañcakam evaṃ brahmākṣarākāśaṃ ākāśamitipañcadhātmāsamāyukta pañcātmana prakāśakamkumārikākhaṇḍaḥākāśa pañcadhā bhittvā vyoma bhittvā tu pañcadhā pañcadhājñānamekatra pañcapañcopadeśakam  pañcapañcātmikā śakti pañcapañcātmikā kriyā pañcapañcakalāvyāptiḥ pañcaratnāni coccaret pañcadhā visargasthaṃ yadā ratnaṃ turyasthaṃ ratnapañcakam mudrāpañcakayogena adhvāna ratnapañcakam prakāśakam nāḍīratnatraya śodhya ekā nāḍī viśiṣyate śuddhāśuddha puraṃ kṛtvā viśuddhijayate tadā vrataṃ cayī vrata śaktivrataṃśivīkaraṇacittasya śivā nisaṃgatāsthirāṃ piṇḍagatiṃ labdhvā tadā vaivapuḥ brahmacaryakam caikatvatāṃ gatam sugatividdhacittasya caitalliṅgagatirbhavet evaṃ ratnopadeśaṃ tu yatrasthaṃ ratnapañcakamevaṃ pañcopadeśaṃ tu vṛkṣe tu paścime gṛhe kumārikākhaṇḍaḥpaścimagṛhanāthasya vṛkṣamūrtirbhagodare bhagasyodaravṛ tu yatrasthaṃ ratnapañcakam vṛkṣāntabhavitānando ratnavṛkṣaṃ taducyate tadeyaṃ pañcaratnasya kailāsoparisaṃsthitam evaṃ mantrodayaughaṃ tu vikhyātaṃ ratnapañcakam ekānekavibhedaistu gotra tat pañcaratnakam gotraliṅga tadākāraṃ bhedaiḥ ṣoḍaśabhiḥ sthitam pañcaratnavibhedena gotramamarikākramam kramānte kramamadhyasthaṃ pañcaratnaṃ śivecchayā parākāśaprayogena tadānuṣṭhānasaṃgraham svakulasya adhiṣṭhāna adhiṣṭhānaṃ ca bhairava tacca pañcaprakāraṃ tu pañcaviṃśātmaka kulam kularatnaṃ kuleśasya kulamārgakramādapi vicāraṃ ṣaḍvidhaṃ kṛtvā tadā jñānopadeśakam dṛḍhalakṣaṃ smṛtaṃ jñāna jñānaṃ ca dṛḍhalakṣaṇam lakṣalakṣaṇamadhyastha jñānaṃ tattvasvarūpataḥ kāraṇaika mano vidvān tūṣṇīmadhyagataṃ manaḥ tadā nirvāṇamāyāti vibhavānandakaulikam kumārikākhaṇḍaḥkaulīśasya tu madhyasthaṃ kamalākṛtigolakam sa ca vai kaulikānanda  sakala tat pragīyate sakalaṃ niṣkale kṛtvā niṣkala sakalātmani tadā yoga makārasya sakārakam ante vyāptiḥ  sphuṭīkṛtā sakārānte hakārākhya hakārānte visargayoḥ pañcaratnasya pātreda aṣṭātriṃśatkalāyutam mudrāpañcakasaṃpūrṇa śaśipātramudāhṛtam āpūrṇagaticittasya makāra saṃprayojayet ardhacandrapura kṛtvā vīrasiddhirbhavet tadā vīravīrendrayogīnā ratna ratnākarādapi ṭakārākṣaramadhyasthavīraśūlaprakāśakam  asyaiva ratnapiṇḍasya sahajaujapadāṅkitām kalāṃṭa saptādaśīṃ kṛtvā vīrapāśān  nikṛntayet kumārikākhaṇḍaḥkhakāra ca phakāra ca rakāratejabṛṃhitam  pañcapīṭhaiśca saṃbhedya vahniviṣaniyojitam kartarī sā samākhyātā pāśasya trividhasya ca śodhanī devatā kālī marmabhedapurāntikā kamala kartarīśasya viṣasya amṛtālayam prayogeda purā śodhya abhakṣa bhakṣayet tadā suvilīnagatairbhāvairmuktomukto na saṃśayaḥ niḥsaṃśayamati kṛtvā tadā kāraṇamādiśetṣaṭtyāgāt  saptame muktiḥ pañcatyāgād jito  manaḥ bhavane nityayogīnā raudrīṃ jñātvā pada labhet ārṇavasya aśeṣasya amarikā parā kriyā sarvadvandvaparityāgāt hṛdayaṃ labhate naraḥ karavīraṃ karavīraṃ karavīrakara tathā vikarāla  karālaṃ ca karālī punaḥ kartarī udaya saṃpradāya tu saṃvartakartarīkaram kartarī merumālā tu kapāla kartarīyutam kartṛtve karaṇaṃ jñānaṃ kāryakāraṇayogata   tadā sā paramā śakti saṃvarta karavīrakam viparītasya vṛkṣasya yadā jāyeta kaulikī tadā ubhayamelāpa ratnānāṃ ca parasparam kumārikākhaṇḍaparasparamano māyā paśyate ca gamāgamam parāparaprabhedasya parāparaparas ca evaṃ parasparaṃ jñānaṃ udayāstamanobhayoḥmahadākāśagā mūrtiraparaparamūrtimān tadā jñānaśalākā ca mūrtamūrtī hyubhau kramāt gamūrtaśca samūrtaśca pamūrtamanilasya tu mamūrtamaparaṃ tattvaṃ  namūrtaṃ pañcamaṃ padam mūrtipañcapuraikatvānmathanādapi raśmayaḥ vartate ca guṇāvāpti samudrādiva manthanāt mantro mantrottarā mudrā mantramudrā ca karṇikā vikarālā ca mudrākhyā prayoga manthanātmanaḥ viparītagatijñāna viparītaṃ ca siṃhakam viparītamanāmā ca viparītakramāt kramam tatraiva cāparaṃ jñānaṃślokāni dvādaśāni ca śmaśāna  vīrasiddhānāṃ cakramelāpakāraṇam kuryāt tanmantramārge tu vidyaikā ṣaṭsu bhedataḥ kumārikākhaṇḍadīpaka pañcaratnasya pātrasya kamalasya ca mudrā pañcaśalākā yā nābhirekākṣarā bhavetpañca kuryācca ādyante pañcaratnaiśca yojitā vīravṛttistadā  bhāti vīro pañcakāntasthā aiṃkārākṣaradīpitā ṣaḍbhirbhedakrama deva yugmapañcaviparyayāt kāraṇa pañcaratnānāṃ liṅgaika ṣaṭprabhedataḥ mūlabhūtaṃ kramācāra jñātvā pañcopadeśakam pañcapañcakamadhyastha pañca pañcākṣarāṇi ca nirapekṣa paro bhāvaḥ durvijña ratnapañcakam durgamasya upāyaṃ tu kadambākhya visargayoḥ karaṇāntargatā śaktiḥ śakti karṇāntare sthitā śaktiḥ karṇa tathā mantra jñātvā tūṣṇīśamācaret tūṣṇīmadhyagatastūṣṇī sa ca aiṃkārasaṃjñayākumārikākhaṇḍapañcaratnasya vijñeya aiṃkāra pañcaratnakam bhūmikā pañcaratnasya oghajñānasubhāsvarā jñātvā muktirna  saṃdeho ityājñā ratnapañcake pañcaratnabhūmikādhikāravarṇanekramodayo nāmānandaḥ śrīvakrā uvācatriṣaṣṭānandaḥbhūmikā jñānaṣaṭkasya vakṣyehaṃ śṛṇu sāmpratam yoginīṣaḍitattvānāṃ ṣaḍi   saptamakaṃ tathā ṣaḍi saptamikā vidyā ṣaḍi   saptamakaṃ kulam teṣā jñānādhikāraṃ tu sthita kūṭopadeśataḥ ṣaḍvarṇākṣarameka ca sthita candrapurasya ca candrabimbasya rājasya kule jātā kuleśvarī taccharīrād viniṣkrāntā guhāvāse kadambake vāmamārgeṇa anāmā ṣaḍidevatā tepi sākārabhūtāñca indriyeṣu sacetasaḥ plavanti gaganāmbhobhimītaryo nātra saṃśayaḥ teṣā ca sārathī vidyā kartarī vāmadevatā tiṣṭhate dakṣiṇe dvāre bhagāhlādena dakṣiṇā khasaṃjñājñānamātrā ca ṣaḍbhirbhedakramātmani lakārā calamadhyasthā latrikā pañcabheditā niyogajñānamekatra lakāre svādhikārikā kakārā ca kakārānte kadvaye saṃpuṭīkṛtā kamadhyasthā kharūpasya
